yattā bhavantas tiṣṭhantu neto gantavyam agrataḥ
aham eva gamiṣyāmi sumantro gurur eva ca  Ram
evam uktās tataḥ sarve tatra tasthuḥ samantataḥ
bharato yatra dhūmāgraṃ tatra dṛṣṭiṃ samādadhāt  Ram
vyavasthitā yā bharatena sā camūr nirīkṣamāṇāpi ca dhūmam agrataḥ
babhūva hṛṣṭā nacireṇa jānatī priyasya rāmasya samāgamaṃ tadā  Ram
dīrghakāloṣitas tasmin girau girivanapriyaḥ
vaidehyāḥ priyamākāṅkṣan svaṃ ca cittaṃ vilobhayan  Ram
atha dāśarathiś citraṃ citrakūṭam adarśayat
bhāryām amarasaṃkāśaḥ śacīm iva puraṃdaraḥ  Ram
na rājyād bhraṃśanaṃ bhadre na suhṛdbhir vinābhavaḥ
mano me bādhate dṛṣṭvā ramaṇīyam imaṃ girim  Ram
paśyemam acalaṃ bhadre nānādvijagaṇāyutam
śikharaiḥ kham ivodviddhair dhātumadbhir vibhūṣitam  Ram
kecid rajatasaṃkāśāḥ kecit kṣatajasaṃnibhāḥ
pītamāñjiṣṭhavarṇāś ca kecin maṇivaraprabhāḥ  Ram
puṣpārkaketakābhāś ca kecij jyotīrasaprabhāḥ
virājante 'calendrasya deśā dhātuvibhūṣitāḥ  Ram
nānāmṛgagaṇadvīpitarakṣvṛkṣagaṇair vṛtaḥ
aduṣṭair bhāty ayaṃ śailo bahupakṣisamākulaḥ  Ram
āmrajambvasanair lodhraiḥ priyālaiḥ panasair dhavaiḥ
aṅkolair bhavyatiniśair bilvatindukaveṇubhiḥ  Ram
kāśmaryariṣṭavaraṇair madhūkais tilakais tathā
badaryāmalakair nīpair vetradhanvanabījakaiḥ  Ram
puṣpavadbhiḥ phalopetaiś chāyāvadbhir manoramaiḥ
evamādibhir ākīrṇaḥ śriyaṃ puṣyaty ayaṃ giriḥ  Ram
śailaprastheṣu ramyeṣu paśyemān kāmaharṣaṇān
kiṃnarān dvaṃdvaśo bhadre ramamāṇān manasvinaḥ  Ram
śākhāvasaktān khaḍgāṃś ca pravarāṇy ambarāṇi ca
paśya vidyādharastrīṇāṃ krīḍoddeśān manoramān  Ram
jalaprapātair udbhedair nisyandaiś ca kvacit kvacit
sravadbhir bhāty ayaṃ śailaḥ sravan mada iva dvipaḥ  Ram
guhāsamīraṇo gandhān nānāpuṣpabhavān vahan
ghrāṇatarpaṇam abhyetya kaṃ naraṃ na praharṣayet  Ram
yadīha śarado 'nekās tvayā sārdham anindite
lakṣmaṇena ca vatsyāmi na māṃ śokaḥ pradhakṣyati  Ram
bahupuṣpaphale ramye nānādvijagaṇāyute
vicitraśikhare hy asmin ratavān asmi bhāmini  Ram
anena vanavāsena mayā prāptaṃ phaladvayam
pituś cānṛṇatā dharme bharatasya priyaṃ tathā  Ram
vaidehi ramase kaccic citrakūṭe mayā saha
paśyantī vividhān bhāvān manovākkāyasaṃyatān  Ram
idam evāmṛtaṃ prāhū rājñāṃ rājarṣayaḥ pare
vanavāsaṃ bhavārthāya pretya me prapitāmahāḥ  Ram
śilāḥ śailasya śobhante viśālāḥ śataśo 'bhitaḥ
bahulā bahulair varṇair nīlapītasitāruṇaiḥ  Ram
niśi bhānty acalendrasya hutāśanaśikhā iva
oṣadhyaḥ svaprabhā lakṣmyā bhrājamānāḥ sahasraśaḥ  Ram
kecit kṣayanibhā deśāḥ kecid udyānasaṃnibhāḥ
kecid ekaśilā bhānti parvatasyāsya bhāmini  Ram
bhittveva vasudhāṃ bhāti citrakūṭaḥ samutthitaḥ
citrakūṭasya kūṭo 'sau dṛśyate sarvataḥ śivaḥ  Ram
kuṣṭhapuṃnāgatagarabhūrjapatrottarachadān
kāmināṃ svāstarān paśya kuśeśayadalāyutān  Ram
mṛditāś cāpaviddhāś ca dṛśyante kamalasrajaḥ
kāmibhir vanite paśya phalāni vividhāni ca  Ram
vasvaukasārāṃ nalinīm atyetīvottarān kurūn
parvataś citrakūṭo 'sau bahumūlaphalodakaḥ  Ram
imaṃ tu kālaṃ vanite vijahrivāṃs tvayā ca sīte saha lakṣmaṇena ca
ratiṃ prapatsye kuladharmavardhinīṃ satāṃ pathi svair niyamaiḥ paraiḥ sthitaḥ  Ram
atha śailād viniṣkramya maithilīṃ kosaleśvaraḥ
adarśayac chubhajalāṃ ramyāṃ mandākinīṃ nadīm  Ram
abravīc ca varārohāṃ cārucandranibhānanām
videharājasya sutāṃ rāmo rājīvalocanaḥ  Ram
vicitrapulināṃ ramyāṃ haṃsasārasasevitām
kusumair upasaṃpannāṃ paśya mandākinīṃ nadīm  Ram
nānāvidhais tīraruhair vṛtāṃ puṣpaphaladrumaiḥ
rājantīṃ rājarājasya nalinīm iva sarvataḥ  Ram
mṛgayūthanipītāni kaluṣāmbhāṃsi sāmpratam
tīrthāni ramaṇīyāni ratiṃ saṃjanayanti me  Ram
jaṭājinadharāḥ kāle valkalottaravāsasaḥ
ṛṣayas tv avagāhante nadīṃ mandākinīṃ priye  Ram
ādityam upatiṣṭhante niyamād ūrdhvabāhavaḥ
ete 'pare viśālākṣi munayaḥ saṃśitavratāḥ  Ram
mārutoddhūtaśikharaiḥ pranṛtta iva parvataḥ
pādapaiḥ pattrapuṣpāṇi sṛjadbhir abhito nadīm  Ram
kaccin maṇinikāśodāṃ kaccit pulinaśālinīm
kaccit siddhajanākīrṇāṃ paśya mandākinīṃ nadīm  Ram
nirdhūtān vāyunā paśya vitatān puṣpasaṃcayān
poplūyamānān aparān paśya tvaṃ jalamadhyagān  Ram
tāṃś cātivalguvacaso rathāṅgāhvayanā dvijāḥ
adhirohanti kalyāṇi niṣkūjantaḥ śubhā giraḥ  Ram
darśanaṃ citrakūṭasya mandākinyāś ca śobhane
adhikaṃ puravāsāc ca manye ca tava darśanāt  Ram
vidhūtakaluṣaiḥ siddhais tapodamaśamānvitaiḥ
nityavikṣobhitajalāṃ vigāhasva mayā saha  Ram
sakhīvac ca vigāhasva sīte mandākinīm imām
kamalāny avamajjantī puṣkarāṇi ca bhāmini  Ram
tvaṃ paurajanavad vyālān ayodhyām iva parvatam
manyasva vanite nityaṃ sarayūvad imāṃ nadīm  Ram
lakṣmaṇaś caiva dharmātmā mannideśe vyavasthitaḥ
tvaṃ cānukūlā vaidehi prītiṃ janayatho mama  Ram
upaspṛśaṃs triṣavaṇaṃ madhumūlaphalāśanaḥ
nāyodhyāyai na rājyāya spṛhaye 'dya tvayā saha  Ram
imāṃ hi ramyāṃ gajayūthalolitāṃ nipītatoyāṃ gajasiṃhavānaraiḥ
supuṣpitaiḥ puṣpadharair alaṃkṛtāṃ na so 'sti yaḥ syān na gatakramaḥ sukhī  Ram
itīva rāmo bahusaṃgataṃ vacaḥ priyāsahāyaḥ saritaṃ prati bruvan
cacāra ramyaṃ nayanāñjanaprabhaṃ sa citrakūṭaṃ raghuvaṃśavardhanaḥ  Ram
tathā tatrāsatas tasya bharatasyopayāyinaḥ
sainyareṇuś ca śabdaś ca prādurāstāṃ nabhaḥspṛśau  Ram
etasminn antare trastāḥ śabdena mahatā tataḥ
arditā yūthapā mattāḥ sayūthā dudruvur diśaḥ  Ram
sa taṃ sainyasamudbhūtaṃ śabdaṃ śuśrava rāghavaḥ
tāṃś ca vipradrutān sarvān yūthapān anvavaikṣata  Ram
tāṃś ca vidravato dṛṣṭvā taṃ ca śrutvā sa niḥsvanam
uvāca rāmaḥ saumitriṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ dīptatejasam  Ram
hanta lakṣmaṇa paśyeha sumitrā suprajās tvayā
bhīmastanitagambhīras tumulaḥ śrūyate svanaḥ  Ram
rājā vā rājamātro vā mṛgayām aṭate vane
anyad vā śvāpadaṃ kiṃcit saumitre jñātum arhasi
sarvam etad yathātattvam acirāj jñātum arhasi  Ram
sa lakṣmaṇaḥ saṃtvaritaḥ sālam āruhya puṣpitam
prekṣamāṇo diśaḥ sarvāḥ pūrvāṃ diśam avaikṣata  Ram
udaṅmukhaḥ prekṣamāṇo dadarśa mahatīṃ camūm
rathāśvagajasambādhāṃ yattair yuktāṃ padātibhiḥ  Ram
tām aśvagajasampūrṇāṃ rathadhvajavibhūṣitām
śaśaṃsa senāṃ rāmāya vacanaṃ cedam abravīt  Ram
agniṃ saṃśamayatv āryaḥ sītā ca bhajatāṃ guhām
sajyaṃ kuruṣva cāpaṃ ca śarāṃś ca kavacaṃ tathā  Ram
taṃ rāmaḥ puruṣavyāghro lakṣmaṇaṃ pratyuvāca ha
aṅgāvekṣasva saumitre kasyaitāṃ manyase camūm  Ram
evam uktas tu rāmeṇa lakṣmaṇo vākyam abravīt
didhakṣann iva tāṃ senāṃ ruṣitaḥ pāvako yathā  Ram
sampannaṃ rājyam icchaṃs tu vyaktaṃ prāpyābhiṣecanam
āvāṃ hantuṃ samabhyeti kaikeyyā bharataḥ sutaḥ  Ram
eṣa vai sumahāñ śrīmān viṭapī saṃprakāśate
virājaty udgataskandhaḥ kovidāradhvajo rathe  Ram
bhajanty ete yathākāmam aśvān āruhya śīghragān
ete bhrājanti saṃhṛṣṭā gajān āruhya sādinaḥ  Ram
gṛhītadhanuṣau cāvāṃ giriṃ vīra śrayāvahe
api nau vaśam āgacchet kovidāradhvajo raṇe  Ram
api drakṣyāmi bharataṃ yatkṛte vyasanaṃ mahat
tvayā rāghava samprāptaṃ sītayā ca mayā tathā  Ram
yannimittaṃ bhavān rājyāc cyuto rāghava śāśvatāt
samprāpto 'yam arir vīra bharato vadhya eva me  Ram
bharatasya vadhe doṣaṃ nāhaṃ paśyāmi rāghava
pūrvāpakāriṇāṃ tyāge na hy adharmo vidhīyate
etasmin nihate kṛtsnām anuśādhi vasuṃdharām  Ram
adya putraṃ hataṃ saṃkhye kaikeyī rājyakāmukā
mayā paśyet suduḥkhārtā hastibhagnam iva drumam  Ram
kaikeyīṃ ca vadhiṣyāmi sānubandhāṃ sabāndhavām
kaluṣeṇādya mahatā medinī parimucyatām  Ram
adyemaṃ saṃyataṃ krodham asatkāraṃ ca mānada
mokṣyāmi śatrusainyeṣu kakṣeṣv iva hutāśanam  Ram
adyaitac citrakūṭasya kānanaṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
bhindañ śatruśarīrāṇi kariṣye śoṇitokṣitam  Ram
śarair nirbhinnahṛdayān kuñjarāṃs turagāṃs tathā
śvāpadāḥ parikarṣantu narāṃś ca nihatān mayā  Ram
śarāṇāṃ dhanuṣaś cāham anṛṇo 'smi mahāvane
sasainyaṃ bharataṃ hatvā bhaviṣyāmi na saṃśayaḥ  Ram
susaṃrabdhaṃ tu saumitriṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ krodhamūrchitam
rāmas tu parisāntvyātha vacanaṃ cedam abravīt  Ram
kim atra dhanuṣā kāryam asinā vā sacarmaṇā
maheṣvāse mahāprājñe bharate svayam āgate  Ram
prāptakālaṃ yad eṣo 'smān bharato draṣṭum icchati
asmāsu manasāpy eṣa nāhitaṃ kiṃcid ācaret  Ram
vipriyaṃ kṛtapūrvaṃ te bharatena kadā na kim
īdṛśaṃ vā bhayaṃ te 'dya bharataṃ yo 'tra śaṅkase  Ram
na hi te niṣṭhuraṃ vācyo bharato nāpriyaṃ vacaḥ
ahaṃ hy apriyam uktaḥ syāṃ bharatasyāpriye kṛte  Ram
kathaṃ nu putrāḥ pitaraṃ hanyuḥ kasyāṃcid āpadi
bhrātā vā bhrātaraṃ hanyāt saumitre prāṇam ātmanaḥ  Ram
yadi rājyasya hetos tvam imāṃ vācaṃ prabhāṣase
vakṣyāmi bharataṃ dṛṣṭvā rājyam asmai pradīyatām  Ram
ucyamāno hi bharato mayā lakṣmaṇa tattvataḥ
rājyam asmai prayaccheti bāḍham ity eva vakṣyati  Ram
tathokto dharmaśīlena bhrātrā tasya hite rataḥ
lakṣmaṇaḥ praviveśeva svāni gātrāṇi lajjayā  Ram
vrīḍitaṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā rāghavaḥ pratyuvāca ha
eṣa manye mahābāhur ihāsmān draṣṭum āgataḥ  Ram
vanavāsam anudhyāya gṛhāya pratineṣyati
imāṃ vāpy eṣa vaidehīm atyantasukhasevinīm  Ram
etau tau saṃprakāśete gotravantau manoramau
vāyuvegasamau vīra javanau turagottamau  Ram
sa eṣa sumahākāyaḥ kampate vāhinīmukhe
nāgaḥ śatruṃjayo nāma vṛddhas tātasya dhīmataḥ  Ram
avatīrya tu sālāgrāt tasmāt sa samitiṃjayaḥ
lakṣmaṇaḥ prāñjalir bhūtvā tasthau rāmasya pārśvataḥ  Ram
bharatenātha saṃdiṣṭā sammardo na bhaved iti
samantāt tasya śailasya senāvāsam akalpayat  Ram
adhyardham ikṣvākucamūr yojanaṃ parvatasya sā
pārśve nyaviśad āvṛtya gajavājirathākulā  Ram
sā citrakūṭe bharatena senā dharmaṃ puraskṛtya vidhūya darpam
prasādanārthaṃ raghunandanasya virocate nītimatā praṇītā  Ram
niveśya senāṃ tu vibhuḥ padbhyāṃ pādavatāṃ varaḥ
abhigantuṃ sa kākutstham iyeṣa guruvartakam  Ram
niviṣṭamātre sainye tu yathoddeśaṃ vinītavat
bharato bhrātaraṃ vākyaṃ śatrughnam idam abravīt  Ram
kṣipraṃ vanam idaṃ saumya narasaṃghaiḥ samantataḥ
lubdhaiś ca sahitair ebhis tvam anveṣitum arhasi  Ram
yāvan na rāmaṃ drakṣyāmi lakṣmaṇaṃ vā mahābalam
vaidehīṃ vā mahābhāgāṃ na me śāntir bhaviṣyati  Ram
yāvan na candrasaṃkāśaṃ drakṣyāmi śubham ānanam
bhrātuḥ padmapalāśākṣaṃ na me śāntir bhaviṣyati  Ram
yāvan na caraṇau bhrātuḥ pārthivavyañjanānvitau
śirasā dhārayiṣyāmi na me śāntir bhaviṣyati  Ram
yāvan na rājye rājyārhaḥ pitṛpaitāmahe sthitaḥ
abhiṣekajalaklinno na me śāntir bhaviṣyati  Ram
kṛtakṛtyā mahābhāgā vaidehī janakātmajā
bhartāraṃ sāgarāntāyāḥ pṛthivyā yānugacchati  Ram
subhagaś citrakūṭo 'sau girirājopamo giriḥ
yasmin vasati kākutsthaḥ kubera iva nandane  Ram
kṛtakāryam idaṃ durgaṃ vanaṃ vyālaniṣevitam
yad adhyāste mahātejā rāmaḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ  Ram
evam uktvā mahātejā bharataḥ puruṣarṣabhaḥ
padbhyām eva mahātejāḥ praviveśa mahad vanam  Ram
sa tāni drumajālāni jātāni girisānuṣu
puṣpitāgrāṇi madhyena jagāma vadatāṃ varaḥ  Ram
sa gireś citrakūṭasya sālam āsādya puṣpitam
rāmāśramagatasyāgner dadarśa dhvajam ucchritam  Ram
taṃ dṛṣṭvā bharataḥ śrīmān mumoda sahabāndhavaḥ
atra rāma iti jñātvā gataḥ pāram ivāmbhasaḥ  Ram
sa citrakūṭe tu girau niśāmya rāmāśramaṃ puṇyajanopapannam
guhena sārdhaṃ tvarito jagāma punar niveśyaiva camūṃ mahātmā  Ram
niviṣṭāyāṃ tu senāyām utsuko bharatas tadā
jagāma bhrātaraṃ draṣṭuṃ śatrughnam anudarśayan  Ram
ṛṣiṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ saṃdiśya mātṝn me śīghram ānaya
iti tvaritam agre sa jagāma guruvatsalaḥ  Ram
sumantras tv api śatrughnam adūrād anvapadyata
rāmadarśanajas tarṣo bharatasyeva tasya ca  Ram
gacchann evātha bharatas tāpasālayasaṃsthitām
bhrātuḥ parṇakuṭīṃ śrīmān uṭajaṃ ca dadarśa ha  Ram
śālāyās tv agratas tasyā dadarśa bharatas tadā
kāṣṭhāni cāvabhagnāni puṣpāṇy avacitāni ca  Ram
dadarśa ca vane tasmin mahataḥ saṃcayān kṛtān
mṛgāṇāṃ mahiṣāṇāṃ ca karīṣaiḥ śītakāraṇāt  Ram
gacchan eva mahābāhur dyutimān bharatas tadā
śatrughnaṃ cābravīd dhṛṣṭas tān amātyāṃś ca sarvaśaḥ  Ram
manye prāptāḥ sma taṃ deśaṃ bharadvājo yam abravīt
nātidūre hi manye 'haṃ nadīṃ mandākinīm itaḥ  Ram
uccair baddhāni cīrāṇi lakṣmaṇena bhaved ayam
abhijñānakṛtaḥ panthā vikāle gantum icchatā  Ram
idaṃ codāttadantānāṃ kuñjarāṇāṃ tarasvinām
śailapārśve parikrāntam anyonyam abhigarjatām  Ram
yam evādhātum icchanti tāpasāḥ satataṃ vane
tasyāsau dṛśyate dhūmaḥ saṃkulaḥ kṛṣṇavartmanaḥ  Ram
atrāhaṃ puruṣavyāghraṃ gurusatkārakāriṇam
āryaṃ drakṣyāmi saṃhṛṣṭo maharṣim iva rāghavam  Ram
atha gatvā muhūrtaṃ tu citrakūṭaṃ sa rāghavaḥ
mandākinīm anuprāptas taṃ janaṃ cedam abravīt  Ram
jagatyāṃ puruṣavyāghra āste vīrāsane rataḥ
janendro nirjanaṃ prāpya dhin me janma sajīvitam  Ram
matkṛte vyasanaṃ prāpto lokanātho mahādyutiḥ
sarvān kāmān parityajya vane vasati rāghavaḥ  Ram
iti lokasamākruṣṭaḥ pādeṣv adya prasādayan
rāmasya nipatiṣyāmi sītāyāś ca punaḥ punaḥ  Ram
evaṃ sa vilapaṃs tasmin vane daśarathātmajaḥ
dadarśa mahatīṃ puṇyāṃ parṇaśālāṃ manoramām  Ram
sālatālāśvakarṇānāṃ parṇair bahubhir āvṛtām
viśālāṃ mṛdubhis tīrṇāṃ kuśair vedim ivādhvare  Ram
śakrāyudhanikāśaiś ca kārmukair bhārasādhanaiḥ
rukmapṛṣṭhair mahāsāraiḥ śobhitāṃ śatrubādhakaiḥ  Ram
arkaraśmipratīkāśair ghorais tūṇīgataiḥ śaraiḥ
śobhitāṃ dīptavadanaiḥ sarpair bhogavatīm iva  Ram
mahārajatavāsobhyām asibhyāṃ ca virājitām
rukmabinduvicitrābhyāṃ carmabhyāṃ cāpi śobhitām  Ram
godhāṅgulitrair āsaktaiś citraiḥ kāñcanabhūṣitaiḥ
arisaṃghair anādhṛṣyāṃ mṛgaiḥ siṃhaguhām iva  Ram
prāgudaksravaṇāṃ vediṃ viśālāṃ dīptapāvakām
dadarśa bharatas tatra puṇyāṃ rāmaniveśane  Ram
nirīkṣya sa muhūrtaṃ tu dadarśa bharato gurum
uṭaje rāmam āsīnaṃ jaṭāmaṇḍaladhāriṇam  Ram
taṃ tu kṛṣṇājinadharaṃ cīravalkalavāsasam
dadarśa rāmam āsīnam abhitaḥ pāvakopamam  Ram
siṃhaskandhaṃ mahābāhuṃ puṇḍarīkanibhekṣaṇam
pṛthivyāḥ sagarāntāyā bhartāraṃ dharmacāriṇam  Ram
upaviṣṭaṃ mahābāhuṃ brahmāṇam iva śāśvatam
sthaṇḍile darbhasaṃstīrṇe sītayā lakṣmaṇena ca  Ram
taṃ dṛṣṭvā bharataḥ śrīmān duḥkhamohapariplutaḥ
abhyadhāvata dharmātmā bharataḥ kaikayīsutaḥ  Ram
dṛṣṭvā ca vilalāpārto bāṣpasaṃdigdhayā girā
aśaknuvan dhārayituṃ dhairyād vacanam abravīt  Ram
yaḥ saṃsadi prakṛtibhir bhaved yukta upāsitum
vanyair mṛgair upāsīnaḥ so 'yam āste mamāgrajaḥ  Ram
vāsobhir bahusāhasrair yo mahātmā purocitaḥ
mṛgājine so 'yam iha pravaste dharmam ācaran  Ram
adhārayad yo vividhāś citrāḥ sumanasas tadā
so 'yaṃ jaṭābhāram imaṃ sahate rāghavaḥ katham  Ram
yasya yajñair yathādiṣṭair yukto dharmasya saṃcayaḥ
śarīrakleśasambhūtaṃ sa dharmaṃ parimārgate  Ram
candanena mahārheṇa yasyāṅgam upasevitam
malena tasyāṅgam idaṃ katham āryasya sevyate  Ram
mannimittam idaṃ duḥkhaṃ prāpto rāmaḥ sukhocitaḥ
dhig jīvitaṃ nṛśaṃsasya mama lokavigarhitam  Ram
ity evaṃ vilapan dīnaḥ prasvinnamukhapaṅkajaḥ
pādāv aprāpya rāmasya papāta bharato rudan  Ram
duḥkhābhitapto bharato rājaputro mahābalaḥ
uktvāryeti sakṛd dīnaṃ punar novāca kiṃcana  Ram
bāṣpāpihitakaṇṭhaś ca prekṣya rāmaṃ yaśasvinam
āryety evābhisaṃkruśya vyāhartuṃ nāśakat tataḥ  Ram
śatrughnaś cāpi rāmasya vavande caraṇau rudan
tāv ubhau sa samāliṅgya rāmo 'py aśrūṇy avartayat  Ram
tataḥ sumantreṇa guhena caiva samīyatū rājasutāv araṇye
divākaraś caiva niśākaraś ca yathāmbare śukrabṛhaspatibhyām  Ram
tān pārthivān vāraṇayūthapābhān samāgatāṃs tatra mahaty araṇye
vanaukasas te 'pi samīkṣya sarve 'py aśrūṇy amuñcan pravihāya harṣam  Ram
āghrāya rāmas taṃ mūrdhni pariṣvajya ca rāghavaḥ
aṅke bharatam āropya paryapṛcchat samāhitaḥ  Ram
kva nu te 'bhūt pitā tāta yad araṇyaṃ tvam āgataḥ
na hi tvaṃ jīvatas tasya vanam āgantum arhasi  Ram
cirasya bata paśyāmi dūrād bharatam āgatam
duṣpratīkam araṇye 'smin kiṃ tāta vanam āgataḥ  Ram
kaccid daśaratho rājā kuśalī satyasaṃgaraḥ
rājasūyāśvamedhānām āhartā dharmaniścayaḥ  Ram
sa kaccid brāhmaṇo vidvān dharmanityo mahādyutiḥ
ikṣvākūṇām upādhyāyo yathāvat tāta pūjyate  Ram
tāta kaccic ca kausalyā sumitrā ca prajāvatī
sukhinī kaccid āryā ca devī nandati kaikayī  Ram
kaccid vinayasampannaḥ kulaputro bahuśrutaḥ
anasūyur anudraṣṭā satkṛtas te purohitaḥ  Ram
kaccid agniṣu te yukto vidhijño matimān ṛjuḥ
hutaṃ ca hoṣyamāṇaṃ ca kāle vedayate sadā  Ram
iṣvastravarasampannam arthaśāstraviśāradam
sudhanvānam upādhyāyaṃ kaccit tvaṃ tāta manyase  Ram
kaccid ātmasamāḥ śūrāḥ śrutavanto jitendriyāḥ
kulīnāś ceṅgitajñāś ca kṛtās te tāta mantriṇaḥ  Ram
mantro vijayamūlaṃ hi rājñāṃ bhavati rāghava
susaṃvṛto mantradharair amātyaiḥ śāstrakovidaiḥ  Ram
kaccin nidrāvaśaṃ naiṣi kaccit kāle vibudhyase
kaccic cāpararātriṣu cintayasy arthanaipuṇam  Ram
kaccin mantrayase naikaḥ kaccin na bahubhiḥ saha
kaccit te mantrito mantro rāṣṭraṃ na paridhāvati  Ram
kaccid arthaṃ viniścitya laghumūlaṃ mahodayam
kṣipram ārabhase kartuṃ na dīrghayasi rāghava  Ram
kaccit tu sukṛtāny eva kṛtarūpāṇi vā punaḥ
vidus te sarvakāryāṇi na kartavyāni pārthivāḥ  Ram
kaccin na tarkair yuktvā vā ye cāpy aparikīrtitāḥ
tvayā vā tava vāmātyair budhyate tāta mantritam  Ram
kaccit sahasrān mūrkhāṇām ekam icchasi paṇḍitam
paṇḍito hy arthakṛcchreṣu kuryān niḥśreyasaṃ mahat  Ram
sahasrāṇy api mūrkhāṇāṃ yady upāste mahīpatiḥ
atha vāpy ayutāny eva nāsti teṣu sahāyatā  Ram
eko 'py amātyo medhāvī śūro dakṣo vicakṣaṇaḥ
rājānaṃ rājamātraṃ vā prāpayen mahatīṃ śriyam  Ram
kaccin mukhyā mahatsv eva madhyameṣu ca madhyamāḥ
jaghanyāś ca jaghanyeṣu bhṛtyāḥ karmasu yojitāḥ  Ram
amātyān upadhātītān pitṛpaitāmahāñ śucīn
śreṣṭhāñ śreṣṭheṣu kaccit tvaṃ niyojayasi karmasu  Ram
kaccit tvāṃ nāvajānanti yājakāḥ patitaṃ yathā
ugrapratigrahītāraṃ kāmayānam iva striyaḥ  Ram
upāyakuśalaṃ vaidyaṃ bhṛtyasaṃdūṣaṇe ratam
śūram aiśvaryakāmaṃ ca yo na hanti sa vadhyate  Ram
kaccid dhṛṣṭaś ca śūraś ca dhṛtimān matimāñ śuciḥ
kulīnaś cānuraktaś ca dakṣaḥ senāpatiḥ kṛtaḥ  Ram
balavantaś ca kaccit te mukhyā yuddhaviśāradāḥ
dṛṣṭāpadānā vikrāntās tvayā satkṛtya mānitāḥ  Ram
kaccid balasya bhaktaṃ ca vetanaṃ ca yathocitam
samprāptakālaṃ dātavyaṃ dadāsi na vilambase  Ram
kālātikramaṇe hy eva bhaktavetanayor bhṛtāḥ
bhartuḥ kupyanti duṣyanti so 'narthaḥ sumahān smṛtaḥ  Ram
kaccit sarve 'nuraktās tvāṃ kulaputrāḥ pradhānataḥ
kaccit prāṇāṃs tavārtheṣu saṃtyajanti samāhitāḥ  Ram
kaccij jānapado vidvān dakṣiṇaḥ pratibhānavān
yathoktavādī dūtas te kṛto bharata paṇḍitaḥ  Ram
kaccid aṣṭādaśāny eṣu svapakṣe daśa pañca ca
tribhis tribhir avijñātair vetsi tīrthāni cārakaiḥ  Ram
kaccid vyapāstān ahitān pratiyātāṃś ca sarvadā
durbalān anavajñāya vartase ripusūdana  Ram
kaccin na lokāyatikān brāhmaṇāṃs tāta sevase
anarthakuśalā hy ete bālāḥ paṇḍitamāninaḥ  Ram
dharmaśāstreṣu mukhyeṣu vidyamāneṣu durbudhāḥ
buddhimān vīkṣikīṃ prāpya nirarthaṃ pravadanti te  Ram
vīrair adhyuṣitāṃ pūrvam asmākaṃ tāta pūrvakaiḥ
satyanāmāṃ dṛḍhadvārāṃ hastyaśvarathasaṃkulām  Ram
brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyair vaiśyaiḥ svakarmanirataiḥ sadā
jitendriyair mahotsāhair vṛtām āryaiḥ sahasraśaḥ  Ram
prāsādair vividhākārair vṛtāṃ vaidyajanākulām
kaccit samuditāṃ sphītām ayodhyāṃ parirakṣasi  Ram
kaccic caityaśatair juṣṭaḥ suniviṣṭajanākulaḥ
devasthānaiḥ prapābhiś ca taḍāgaiś copaśobhitaḥ  Ram
prahṛṣṭanaranārīkaḥ samājotsavaśobhitaḥ
sukṛṣṭasīmā paśumān hiṃsābhir parivarjitaḥ  Ram
adevamātṛko ramyaḥ śvāpadaiḥ parivarjitaḥ
kaccij janapadaḥ sphītaḥ sukhaṃ vasati rāghava  Ram
kaccit te dayitāḥ sarve kṛṣigorakṣajīvinaḥ
vārttāyāṃ saṃśritas tāta loko hi sukham edhate  Ram
teṣāṃ guptiparīhāraiḥ kaccit te bharaṇaṃ kṛtam
rakṣyā hi rājñā dharmeṇa sarve viṣayavāsinaḥ  Ram
kaccit striyaḥ sāntvayasi kaccit tāś ca surakṣitāḥ
kaccin na śraddadhāsyāsāṃ kaccid guhyaṃ na bhāṣase  Ram
kaccin nāgavanaṃ guptaṃ kuñjarāṇāṃ ca tṛpyasi
kaccid darśayase nityaṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ vibhūṣitam
utthāyotthāya pūrvāhṇe rājaputro mahāpathe  Ram
kaccit sarvāṇi durgāṇi dhanadhānyāyudhodakaiḥ
yantraiś ca paripūrṇāni tathā śilpidhanurdharaiḥ  Ram
āyas te vipulaḥ kaccit kaccid alpataro vyayaḥ
apātreṣu na te kaccit kośo gacchati rāghava  Ram
devatārthe ca pitrarthe brāhmaṇābhyāgateṣu ca
yodheṣu mitravargeṣu kaccid gacchati te vyayaḥ  Ram
kaccid āryo viśuddhātmā kṣāritaś corakarmaṇā
apṛṣṭaḥ śāstrakuśalair na lobhād badhyate śuciḥ  Ram
gṛhītaś caiva pṛṣṭaś ca kāle dṛṣṭaḥ sakāraṇaḥ
kaccin na mucyate coro dhanalobhān nararṣabha  Ram
vyasane kaccid āḍhyasya durgatasya ca rāghava
arthaṃ virāgāḥ paśyanti tavāmātyā bahuśrutāḥ  Ram
yāni mithyābhiśastānāṃ patanty asrāṇi rāghava
tāni putrapaśūn ghnanti prītyartham anuśāsataḥ  Ram
kaccid vṛddhāṃś ca bālāṃś ca vaidyamukhyāṃś ca rāghava
dānena manasā vācā tribhir etair bubhūṣase  Ram
kaccid gurūṃś ca vṛddhāṃś ca tāpasān devatātithīn
caityāṃś ca sarvān siddhārthān brāhmaṇāṃś ca namasyasi  Ram
kaccid arthena vā dharmaṃ dharmaṃ dharmeṇa vā punaḥ
ubhau vā prītilobhena kāmena na vibādhase  Ram
kaccid arthaṃ ca dharmaṃ ca kāmaṃ ca jayatāṃ vara
vibhajya kāle kālajña sarvān bharata sevase  Ram
kaccit te brāhmaṇāḥ śarma sarvaśāstrārthakovidāḥ
āśaṃsante mahāprājña paurajānapadaiḥ saha  Ram
nāstikyam anṛtaṃ krodhaṃ pramādaṃ dīrghasūtratām
adarśanaṃ jñānavatām ālasyaṃ pañcavṛttitām  Ram
ekacintanam arthānām anarthajñaiś ca mantraṇam
niścitānām anārambhaṃ mantrasyāparirakṣaṇam  Ram
maṅgalasyāprayogaṃ ca pratyutthānaṃ ca sarvaśaḥ
kaccit tvaṃ varjayasy etān rājadoṣāṃś caturdaśa  Ram
kaccit svādukṛtaṃ bhojyam eko nāśnāsi rāghava
kaccid āśaṃsamānebhyo mitrebhyaḥ samprayacchasi  Ram
rāmasya vacanaṃ śrutvā bharataḥ pratyuvāca ha
kiṃ me dharmād vihīnasya rājadharmaḥ kariṣyati  Ram
śāśvato 'yaṃ sadā dharmaḥ sthito 'smāsu nararṣabha
jyeṣṭhaputre sthite rājan na kanīyān bhaven nṛpaḥ  Ram
sa samṛddhāṃ mayā sārdham ayodhyāṃ gaccha rāghava
abhiṣecaya cātmānaṃ kulasyāsya bhavāya naḥ  Ram
rājānaṃ mānuṣaṃ prāhur devatve saṃmato mama
yasya dharmārthasahitaṃ vṛttam āhur amānuṣam  Ram
kekayasthe ca mayi tu tvayi cāraṇyam āśrite
divam ārya gato rājā yāyajūkaḥ satāṃ mataḥ  Ram
uttiṣṭha puruṣavyāghra kriyatām udakaṃ pituḥ
ahaṃ cāyaṃ ca śatrughnaḥ pūrvam eva kṛtodakau  Ram
priyeṇa kila dattaṃ hi pitṛlokeṣu rāghava
akṣayyaṃ bhavatīty āhur bhavāṃś caiva pituḥ priyaḥ  Ram
tāṃ śrutvā karuṇāṃ vācaṃ pitur maraṇasaṃhitām
rāghavo bharatenoktāṃ babhūva gatacetanaḥ  Ram
vāgvajraṃ bharatenoktam amanojñaṃ paraṃtapaḥ
pragṛhya bāhū rāmo vai puṣpitāgro yathā drumaḥ
vane paraśunā kṛttas tathā bhuvi papāta ha  Ram
tathā hi patitaṃ rāmaṃ jagatyāṃ jagatīpatim
kūlaghātapariśrāntaṃ prasuptam iva kuñjaram  Ram
bhrātaras te maheṣvāsaṃ sarvataḥ śokakarśitam
rudantaḥ saha vaidehyā siṣicuḥ salilena vai  Ram
sa tu saṃjñāṃ punar labdhvā netrābhyām āsram utsṛjan
upākrāmata kākutsthaḥ kṛpaṇaṃ bahubhāṣitum  Ram
kiṃ nu tasya mayā kāryaṃ durjātena mahātmanaḥ
yo mṛto mama śokena na mayā cāpi saṃskṛtaḥ  Ram
aho bharata siddhārtho yena rājā tvayānagha
śatrugheṇa ca sarveṣu pretakṛtyeṣu satkṛtaḥ  Ram
niṣpradhānām anekāgrāṃ narendreṇa vinākṛtām
nivṛttavanavāso 'pi nāyodhyāṃ gantum utsahe  Ram
samāptavanavāsaṃ mām ayodhyāyāṃ paraṃtapa
ko nu śāsiṣyati punas tāte lokāntaraṃ gate  Ram
purā prekṣya suvṛttaṃ māṃ pitā yāny āha sāntvayan
vākyāni tāni śroṣyāmi kutaḥ karṇasukhāny aham  Ram
evam uktvā sa bharataṃ bhāryām abhyetya rāghavaḥ
uvāca śokasaṃtaptaḥ pūrṇacandranibhānanām  Ram
sīte mṛtas te śvaśuraḥ pitrā hīno 'si lakṣmaṇa
bharato duḥkham ācaṣṭe svargataṃ pṛthivīpatim  Ram
sāntvayitvā tu tāṃ rāmo rudantīṃ janakātmajām
uvāca lakṣmaṇaṃ tatra duḥkhito duḥkhitaṃ vacaḥ  Ram
ānayeṅgudīpiṇyākaṃ cīram āhara cottaram
jalakriyārthaṃ tātasya gamiṣyāmi mahātmanaḥ  Ram
sītā purastād vrajatu tvam enām abhito vraja
ahaṃ paścād gamiṣyāmi gatir hy eṣā sudāruṇā  Ram
tato nityānugas teṣāṃ viditātmā mahāmatiḥ
mṛdur dāntaś ca śāntaś ca rāme ca dṛḍhabhaktimān  Ram
sumantras tair nṛpasutaiḥ sārdham āśvāsya rāghavam
avātārayad ālambya nadīṃ mandākinīṃ śivām  Ram
te sutīrthāṃ tataḥ kṛcchrād upāgamya yaśasvinaḥ
nadīṃ mandākinīṃ ramyāṃ sadā puṣpitakānanām  Ram
śīghrasrotasam āsādya tīrthaṃ śivam akardamam
siṣicus tūdakaṃ rājñe tata etad bhavatv iti  Ram
pragṛhya ca mahīpālo jalapūritam añjalim
diśaṃ yāmyām abhimukho rudan vacanam abravīt  Ram
etat te rājaśārdūla vimalaṃ toyam akṣayam
pitṛlokagatasyādya maddattam upatiṣṭhatu  Ram
tato mandākinītīrāt pratyuttīrya sa rāghavaḥ
pituś cakāra tejasvī nivāpaṃ bhrātṛbhiḥ saha  Ram
aiṅgudaṃ badarīmiśraṃ piṇyākaṃ darbhasaṃstare
nyasya rāmaḥ suduḥkhārto rudan vacanam abravīt  Ram
idaṃ bhuṅkṣva mahārāja prīto yadaśanā vayam
yadannaḥ puruṣo bhavati tadannās tasya devatāḥ  Ram
tatas tenaiva mārgeṇa pratyuttīrya nadītaṭāt
āruroha naravyāghro ramyasānuṃ mahīdharam  Ram
tataḥ parṇakuṭīdvāram āsādya jagatīpatiḥ
parijagrāha pāṇibhyām ubhau bharatalakṣmaṇau  Ram
teṣāṃ tu rudatāṃ śabdāt pratiśrutkābhavad girau
bhrātṝṇāṃ saha vaidehyā siṃhānāṃ nardatām iva  Ram
vijñāya tumulaṃ śabdaṃ trastā bharatasainikāḥ
abruvaṃś cāpi rāmeṇa bharataḥ saṃgato dhruvam
teṣām eva mahāñ śabdaḥ śocatāṃ pitaraṃ mṛtam  Ram
atha vāsān parityajya taṃ sarve 'bhimukhāḥ svanam
apy ekamanaso jagmur yathāsthānaṃ pradhāvitāḥ  Ram
hayair anye gajair anye rathair anye svalaṃkṛtaiḥ
sukumārās tathaivānye padbhir eva narā yayuḥ  Ram
aciraproṣitaṃ rāmaṃ ciraviproṣitaṃ yathā
draṣṭukāmo janaḥ sarvo jagāma sahasāśramam  Ram
bhrātṝṇāṃ tvaritās te tu draṣṭukāmāḥ samāgamam
yayur bahuvidhair yānaiḥ khuranemisamākulaiḥ  Ram
sā bhūmir bahubhir yānaiḥ khuranemisamāhatā
mumoca tumulaṃ śabdaṃ dyaur ivābhrasamāgame  Ram
tena vitrāsitā nāgāḥ kareṇuparivāritāḥ
āvāsayanto gandhena jagmur anyad vanaṃ tataḥ  Ram
varāhamṛgasiṃhāś ca mahiṣāḥ sarkṣavānarāḥ
vyāghragokarṇagavayā vitreṣuḥ pṛṣataiḥ saha  Ram
rathāṅgasāhvā natyūhā haṃsāḥ kāraṇḍavāḥ plavāḥ
tathā puṃskokilāḥ krauñcā visaṃjñā bhejire diśaḥ  Ram
tena śabdena vitrastair ākāśaṃ pakṣibhir vṛtam
manuṣyair āvṛtā bhūmir ubhayaṃ prababhau tadā  Ram
tān narān bāṣpapūrṇākṣān samīkṣyātha suduḥkhitān
paryaṣvajata dharmajñaḥ pitṛvan mātṛvac ca saḥ  Ram
sa tatra kāṃścit pariṣasvaje narān narāś ca kecit tu tam abhyavādayan
cakāra sarvān savayasyabāndhavān yathārham āsādya tadā nṛpātmajaḥ  Ram
tataḥ sa teṣāṃ rudatāṃ mahātmanāṃ bhuvaṃ ca khaṃ cānuvinādayan svanaḥ
guhā girīṇāṃ ca diśaś ca saṃtataṃ mṛdaṅgaghoṣapratimo viśuśruve  Ram
vasiṣṭhaḥ purataḥ kṛtvā dārān daśarathasya ca
abhicakrāma taṃ deśaṃ rāmadarśanatarṣitaḥ  Ram
rājapatnyaś ca gacchantyo mandaṃ mandākinīṃ prati
dadṛśus tatra tat tīrthaṃ rāmalakṣmaṇasevitam  Ram
kausalyā bāṣpapūrṇena mukhena pariśuṣyatā
sumitrām abravīd dīnā yāś cānyā rājayoṣitaḥ  Ram
idaṃ teṣām anāthānāṃ kliṣṭam akliṣṭakarmaṇām
vane prāk kevalaṃ tīrthaṃ ye te nirviṣayīkṛtāḥ  Ram
itaḥ sumitre putras te sadā jalam atandritaḥ
svayaṃ harati saumitrir mama putrasya kāraṇāt  Ram
dakṣiṇāgreṣu darbheṣu sā dadarśa mahītale
pitur iṅgudīpiṇyākaṃ nyastam āyatalocanā  Ram
taṃ bhūmau pitur ārtena nyastaṃ rāmeṇa vīkṣya sā
uvāca devī kausalyā sarvā daśarathastriyaḥ  Ram
idam ikṣvākunāthasya rāghavasya mahātmanaḥ
rāghaveṇa pitur dattaṃ paśyataitad yathāvidhi  Ram
tasya devasamānasya pārthivasya mahātmanaḥ
naitad aupayikaṃ manye bhuktabhogasya bhojanam  Ram
caturantāṃ mahīṃ bhuktvā mahendrasadṛśo vibhuḥ
katham iṅgudīpiṇyākaṃ sa bhuṅkte vasudhādhipaḥ  Ram
ato duḥkhataraṃ loke na kiṃcit pratibhāti mā
yatra rāmaḥ pitur dadyād iṅgudīkṣodam ṛddhimān  Ram
rāmeṇeṅgudīpiṇyākaṃ pitur dattaṃ samīkṣya me
kathaṃ duḥkhena hṛdayaṃ na sphoṭati sahasradhā  Ram
evam ārtāṃ sapatnyas tā jagmur āśvāsya tāṃ tadā
dadṛśuś cāśrame rāmaṃ svargāc cyutam ivāmaram  Ram
sarvabhogaiḥ parityaktaṃ rāmaṃ samprekṣya mātaraḥ
ārtā mumucur aśrūṇi sasvaraṃ śokakarśitāḥ  Ram
tāsāṃ rāmaḥ samutthāya jagrāha caraṇāñ śubhān
mātṝṇāṃ manujavyāghraḥ sarvāsāṃ satyasaṃgaraḥ  Ram
tāḥ pāṇibhiḥ sukhasparśair mṛdvaṅgulitalaiḥ śubhaiḥ
pramamārjū rajaḥ pṛṣṭhād rāmasyāyatalocanāḥ  Ram
saumitrir api tāḥ sarvā mātṝn samprekṣya duḥkhitaḥ
abhyavādayatāsaktaṃ śanai rāmād anantaram  Ram
yathā rāme tathā tasmin sarvā vavṛtire striyaḥ
vṛttiṃ daśarathāj jāte lakṣmaṇe śubhalakṣaṇe  Ram
sītāpi caraṇāṃs tāsām upasaṃgṛhya duḥkhitā
śvaśrūṇām aśrupūrṇākṣī sā babhūvāgrataḥ sthitā  Ram
tāṃ pariṣvajya duḥkhārtāṃ mātā duhitaraṃ yathā
vanavāsakṛśāṃ dīnāṃ kausalyā vākyam abravīt  Ram
videharājasya sutā snuṣā daśarathasya ca
rāmapatnī kathaṃ duḥkhaṃ samprāptā nirjane vane  Ram
padmam ātapasaṃtaptaṃ parikliṣṭam ivotpalam
kāñcanaṃ rajasā dhvastaṃ kliṣṭaṃ candram ivāmbudaiḥ  Ram
mukhaṃ te prekṣya māṃ śoko dahaty agnir ivāśrayam
bhṛśaṃ manasi vaidehi vyasanāraṇisambhavaḥ  Ram
bruvantyām evam ārtāyāṃ jananyāṃ bharatāgrajaḥ
pādāv āsādya jagrāha vasiṣṭhasya sa rāghavaḥ  Ram
purohitasyāgnisamasya tasya vai bṛhaspater indra ivāmarādhipaḥ
pragṛhya pādau susamṛddhatejasaḥ sahaiva tenopaviveśa rāghavaḥ  Ram
tato jaghanyaṃ sahitaiḥ sa mantribhiḥ purapradhānaiś ca sahaiva sainikaiḥ
janena dharmajñatamena dharmavān upopaviṣṭo bharatas tadāgrajam  Ram
upopaviṣṭas tu tadā sa vīryavāṃs tapasviveṣeṇa samīkṣya rāghavam
śriyā jvalantaṃ bharataḥ kṛtāñjalir yathā mahendraḥ prayataḥ prajāpatim  Ram
kim eṣa vākyaṃ bharato 'dya rāghavaṃ praṇamya satkṛtya ca sādhu vakṣyati
itīva tasyāryajanasya tattvato babhūva kautūhalam uttamaṃ tadā  Ram
sa rāghavaḥ satyadhṛtiś ca lakṣmaṇo mahānubhāvo bharataś ca dhārmikaḥ
vṛtāḥ suhṛdbhiś ca virejur adhvare yathā sadasyaiḥ sahitās trayo 'gnayaḥ  Ram
taṃ tu rāmaḥ samāśvāsya bhrātaraṃ guruvatsalam
lakṣmaṇena saha bhrātrā praṣṭuṃ samupacakrame  Ram
kim etad iccheyam ahaṃ śrotuṃ pravyāhṛtaṃ tvayā
yasmāt tvam āgato deśam imaṃ cīrajaṭājinī  Ram
yannimittam imaṃ deśaṃ kṛṣṇājinajaṭādharaḥ
hitvā rājyaṃ praviṣṭas tvaṃ tat sarvaṃ vaktum arhasi  Ram
ity uktaḥ kekayīputraḥ kākutsthena mahātmanā
pragṛhya balavad bhūyaḥ prāñjalir vākyam abravīt  Ram
āryaṃ tātaḥ parityajya kṛtvā karma suduṣkaram
gataḥ svargaṃ mahābāhuḥ putraśokābhipīḍitaḥ  Ram
striyā niyuktaḥ kaikeyyā mama mātrā paraṃtapa
cakāra sumahat pāpam idam ātmayaśoharam  Ram
sā rājyaphalam aprāpya vidhavā śokakarśitā
patiṣyati mahāghore niraye jananī mama  Ram
tasya me dāsabhūtasya prasādaṃ kartum arhasi
abhiṣiñcasva cādyaiva rājyena maghavān iva  Ram
imāḥ prakṛtayaḥ sarvā vidhavā mātaraś ca yāḥ
tvatsakāśam anuprāptāḥ prasādaṃ kartum arhasi  Ram
tadānupūrvyā yuktaṃ ca yuktaṃ cātmani mānada
rājyaṃ prāpnuhi dharmeṇa sakāmān suhṛdaḥ kuru  Ram
bhavatv avidhavā bhūmiḥ samagrā patinā tvayā
śaśinā vimaleneva śāradī rajanī yathā  Ram
ebhiś ca sacivaiḥ sārdhaṃ śirasā yācito mayā
bhrātuḥ śiṣyasya dāsasya prasādaṃ kartum arhasi  Ram
tad idaṃ śāśvataṃ pitryaṃ sarvaṃ sacivamaṇḍalam
pūjitaṃ puruṣavyāghra nātikramitum utsahe  Ram
evam uktvā mahābāhuḥ sabāṣpaḥ kekayīsutaḥ
rāmasya śirasā pādau jagrāha bharataḥ punaḥ  Ram
taṃ mattam iva mātaṃgaṃ niḥśvasantaṃ punaḥ punaḥ
bhrātaraṃ bharataṃ rāmaḥ pariṣvajyedam abravīt  Ram
kulīnaḥ sattvasampannas tejasvī caritavrataḥ
rājyahetoḥ kathaṃ pāpam ācaret tvadvidho janaḥ  Ram
na doṣaṃ tvayi paśyāmi sūkṣmam apy arisūdana
na cāpi jananīṃ bālyāt tvaṃ vigarhitum arhasi  Ram
yāvat pitari dharmajña gauravaṃ lokasatkṛte
tāvad dharmabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭha jananyām api gauravam  Ram
etābhyāṃ dharmaśīlābhyāṃ vanaṃ gaccheti rāghava
mātāpitṛbhyām ukto 'haṃ katham anyat samācare  Ram
tvayā rājyam ayodhyāyāṃ prāptavyaṃ lokasatkṛtam
vastavyaṃ daṇḍakāraṇye mayā valkalavāsasā  Ram
evaṃ kṛtvā mahārājo vibhāgaṃ lokasaṃnidhau
vyādiśya ca mahātejā divaṃ daśaratho gataḥ  Ram
sa ca pramāṇaṃ dharmātmā rājā lokagurus tava
pitrā dattaṃ yathābhāgam upabhoktuṃ tvam arhasi  Ram
caturdaśa samāḥ saumya daṇḍakāraṇyam āśritaḥ
upabhokṣye tv ahaṃ dattaṃ bhāgaṃ pitrā mahātmanā  Ram
yad abravīn māṃ naralokasatkṛtaḥ pitā mahātmā vibudhādhipopamaḥ
tad eva manye paramātmano hitaṃ na sarvalokeśvarabhāvam avyayam  Ram
tataḥ puruṣasiṃhānāṃ vṛtānāṃ taiḥ suhṛdgaṇaiḥ
śocatām eva rajanī duḥkhena vyatyavartata  Ram
rajanyāṃ suprabhātāyāṃ bhrātaras te suhṛdvṛtāḥ
mandākinyāṃ hutaṃ japyaṃ kṛtvā rāmam upāgaman  Ram
tūṣṇīṃ te samupāsīnā na kaścit kiṃcid abravīt
bharatas tu suhṛnmadhye rāmaṃ vacanam abravīt  Ram
sāntvitā māmikā mātā dattaṃ rājyam idaṃ mama
tad dadāmi tavaivāhaṃ bhuṅkṣva rājyam akaṇṭakam  Ram
mahatevāmbuvegena bhinnaḥ setur jalāgame
durāvāraṃ tvadanyena rājyakhaṇḍam idaṃ mahat  Ram
gatiṃ khara ivāśvasya tārkṣyasyeva patatriṇaḥ
anugantuṃ na śaktir me gatiṃ tava mahīpate  Ram
sujīvaṃ nityaśas tasya yaḥ parair upajīvyate
rāma tena tu durjīvaṃ yaḥ parān upajīvati  Ram
yathā tu ropito vṛkṣaḥ puruṣeṇa vivardhitaḥ
hrasvakena durāroho rūḍhaskandho mahādrumaḥ  Ram
sa yadā puṣpito bhūtvā phalāni na vidarśayet
sa tāṃ nānubhavet prītiṃ yasya hetoḥ prabhāvitaḥ  Ram
eṣopamā mahābāho tvam arthaṃ vettum arhasi
yadi tvam asmān ṛṣabho bhartā bhṛtyān na śādhi hi  Ram
śreṇayas tvāṃ mahārāja paśyantv agryāś ca sarvaśaḥ
pratapantam ivādityaṃ rājye sthitam ariṃdamam  Ram
tavānuyāne kākutstha mattā nardantu kuñjarāḥ
antaḥpuragatā nāryo nandantu susamāhitāḥ  Ram
tasya sādhv ity amanyanta nāgarā vividhā janāḥ
bharatasya vacaḥ śrutvā rāmaṃ pratyanuyācataḥ  Ram
tam evaṃ duḥkhitaṃ prekṣya vilapantaṃ yaśasvinam
rāmaḥ kṛtātmā bharataṃ samāśvāsayad ātmavān  Ram
nātmanaḥ kāmakāro 'sti puruṣo 'yam anīśvaraḥ
itaś cetarataś cainaṃ kṛtāntaḥ parikarṣati  Ram
sarve kṣayāntā nicayāḥ patanāntāḥ samucchrayāḥ
saṃyogā viprayogāntā maraṇāntaṃ ca jīvitam  Ram
yathā phalānāṃ pakvānāṃ nānyatra patanād bhayam
evaṃ narasya jātasya nānyatra maraṇād bhayam  Ram
yathāgāraṃ dṛḍhasthūṇaṃ jīrṇaṃ bhūtvāvasīdati
tathāvasīdanti narā jarāmṛtyuvaśaṃ gatāḥ  Ram
ahorātrāṇi gacchanti sarveṣāṃ prāṇinām iha
āyūṃṣi kṣapayanty āśu grīṣme jalam ivāṃśavaḥ  Ram
ātmānam anuśoca tvaṃ kim anyam anuśocasi
āyus te hīyate yasya sthitasya ca gatasya ca  Ram
sahaiva mṛtyur vrajati saha mṛtyur niṣīdati
gatvā sudīrgham adhvānaṃ saha mṛtyur nivartate  Ram
gātreṣu valayaḥ prāptāḥ śvetāś caiva śiroruhāḥ
jarayā puruṣo jīrṇaḥ kiṃ hi kṛtvā prabhāvayet  Ram
nandanty udita āditye nandanty astam ite ravau
ātmano nāvabudhyante manuṣyā jīvitakṣayam  Ram
hṛṣyanty ṛtumukhaṃ dṛṣṭvā navaṃ navam ihāgatam
ṛtūnāṃ parivartena prāṇināṃ prāṇasaṃkṣayaḥ  Ram
yathā kāṣṭhaṃ ca kāṣṭhaṃ ca sameyātāṃ mahārṇave
sametya ca vyapeyātāṃ kālam āsādya kaṃcana  Ram
evaṃ bhāryāś ca putrāś ca jñātayaś ca vasūni ca
sametya vyavadhāvanti dhruvo hy eṣāṃ vinābhavaḥ  Ram
nātra kaścid yathā bhāvaṃ prāṇī samabhivartate
tena tasmin na sāmarthyaṃ pretasyāsty anuśocataḥ  Ram
yathā hi sārthaṃ gacchantaṃ brūyāt kaścit pathi sthitaḥ
aham apy āgamiṣyāmi pṛṣṭhato bhavatām iti  Ram
evaṃ pūrvair gato mārgaḥ pitṛpaitāmaho dhruvaḥ
tam āpannaḥ kathaṃ śoced yasya nāsti vyatikramaḥ  Ram
vayasaḥ patamānasya srotaso vānivartinaḥ
ātmā sukhe niyoktavyaḥ sukhabhājaḥ prajāḥ smṛtāḥ  Ram
dharmātmā sa śubhaiḥ kṛtsnaiḥ kratubhiś cāptadakṣiṇaiḥ
dhūtapāpo gataḥ svargaṃ pitā naḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ  Ram
bhṛtyānāṃ bharaṇāt samyak prajānāṃ paripālanāt
arthādānāc ca dhārmeṇa pitā nas tridivaṃ gataḥ  Ram
iṣṭvā bahuvidhair yajñair bhogāṃś cāvāpya puṣkalān
uttamaṃ cāyur āsādya svar gataḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ  Ram
sa jīrṇaṃ mānuṣaṃ dehaṃ parityajya pitā hi naḥ
daivīm ṛddhim anuprāpto brahmalokavihāriṇīm  Ram
taṃ tu naivaṃvidhaḥ kaścit prājñaḥ śocitum arhati
tvadvidho yadvidhaś cāpi śrutavān buddhimattaraḥ  Ram
ete bahuvidhāḥ śokā vilāparudite tathā
varjanīyā hi dhīreṇa sarvāvasthāsu dhīmatā  Ram
sa svastho bhava mā śoco yātvā cāvasa tāṃ purīm
tathā pitrā niyukto 'si vaśinā vadatāṃ vara  Ram
yatrāham api tenaiva niyuktaḥ puṇyakarmaṇā
tatraivāhaṃ kariṣyāmi pitur āryasya śāsanam  Ram
na mayā śāsanaṃ tasya tyaktuṃ nyāyyam ariṃdama
tat tvayāpi sadā mānyaṃ sa vai bandhuḥ sa naḥ pitā  Ram
evam uktvā tu virate rāme vacanam arthavat
uvāca bharataś citraṃ dhārmiko dhārmikaṃ vacaḥ  Ram
ko hi syād īdṛśo loke yādṛśas tvam ariṃdama
na tvāṃ pravyathayed duḥkhaṃ prītir vā na praharṣayet  Ram
saṃmataś cāsi vṛddhānāṃ tāṃś ca pṛcchasi saṃśayān
yathā mṛtas tathā jīvan yathāsati tathā sati  Ram
yasyaiṣa buddhilābhaḥ syāt paritapyeta kena saḥ
sa evaṃ vyasanaṃ prāpya na viṣīditum arhati  Ram
amaropamasattvas tvaṃ mahātmā satyasaṃgaraḥ
sarvajñaḥ sarvadarśī ca buddhimāṃś cāsi rāghava  Ram
na tvām evaṃ guṇair yuktaṃ prabhavābhavakovidam
aviṣahyatamaṃ duḥkham āsādayitum arhati  Ram
proṣite mayi yat pāpaṃ mātrā matkāraṇāt kṛtam
kṣudrayā tad aniṣṭaṃ me prasīdatu bhavān mama  Ram
dharmabandhena baddho 'smi tenemāṃ neha mātaram
hanmi tīvreṇa daṇḍena daṇḍārhāṃ pāpakāriṇīm  Ram
kathaṃ daśarathāj jātaḥ śuddhābhijanakarmaṇaḥ
jānan dharmam adharmiṣṭhaṃ kuryāṃ karma jugupsitam  Ram
guruḥ kriyāvān vṛddhaś ca rājā pretaḥ piteti ca
tātaṃ na parigarheyaṃ daivataṃ ceti saṃsadi  Ram
ko hi dharmārthayor hīnam īdṛśaṃ karma kilbiṣam
striyāḥ priyacikīrṣuḥ san kuryād dharmajña dharmavit  Ram
antakāle hi bhūtāni muhyantīti purāśrutiḥ
rājñaivaṃ kurvatā loke pratyakṣā sā śrutiḥ kṛtā  Ram
sādhvartham abhisaṃdhāya krodhān mohāc ca sāhasāt
tātasya yad atikrāntaṃ pratyāharatu tad bhavān  Ram
pitur hi samatikrāntaṃ putro yaḥ sādhu manyate
tad apatyaṃ mataṃ loke viparītam ato 'nyathā  Ram
tad apatyaṃ bhavān astu mā bhavān duṣkṛtaṃ pituḥ
abhipattā kṛtaṃ karma loke dhīravigarhitam  Ram
kaikeyīṃ māṃ ca tātaṃ ca suhṛdo bāndhavāṃś ca naḥ
paurajānapadān sarvāṃs trātu sarvam idaṃ bhavān  Ram
kva cāraṇyaṃ kva ca kṣātraṃ kva jaṭāḥ kva ca pālanam
īdṛśaṃ vyāhataṃ karma na bhavān kartum arhati  Ram
atha kleśajam eva tvaṃ dharmaṃ caritum icchasi
dharmeṇa caturo varṇān pālayan kleśam āpnuhi  Ram
caturṇām āśramāṇāṃ hi gārhasthyaṃ śreṣṭham āśramam
āhur dharmajña dharmajñās taṃ kathaṃ tyaktum arhasi  Ram
śrutena bālaḥ sthānena janmanā bhavato hy aham
sa kathaṃ pālayiṣyāmi bhūmiṃ bhavati tiṣṭhati  Ram
hīnabuddhiguṇo bālo hīnaḥ sthānena cāpy aham
bhavatā ca vinā bhūto na vartayitum utsahe  Ram
idaṃ nikhilam avyagraṃ pitryaṃ rājyam akaṇṭakam
anuśādhi svadharmeṇa dharmajña saha bāndhavaiḥ  Ram
ihaiva tvābhiṣiñcantu dharmajña saha bāndhavaiḥ
ṛtvijaḥ savasiṣṭhāś ca mantravan mantrakovidāḥ  Ram
abhiṣiktas tvam asmābhir ayodhyāṃ pālane vraja
vijitya tarasā lokān marudbhir iva vāsavaḥ  Ram
ṛṇāni trīṇy apākurvan durhṛdaḥ sādhu nirdahan
suhṛdas tarpayan kāmais tvam evātrānuśādhi mām  Ram
adyārya muditāḥ santu suhṛdas te 'bhiṣecane
adya bhītāḥ pālayantāṃ durhṛdas te diśo daśa  Ram
ākrośaṃ mama mātuś ca pramṛjya puruṣarṣabha
adya tatra bhavantaṃ ca pitaraṃ rakṣa kilbiṣāt  Ram
śirasā tvābhiyāce 'haṃ kuruṣva karuṇāṃ mayi
bāndhaveṣu ca sarveṣu bhūteṣv iva maheśvaraḥ  Ram
atha vā pṛṣṭhataḥ kṛtvā vanam eva bhavān itaḥ
gamiṣyati gamiṣyāmi bhavatā sārdham apy aham  Ram
tathāpi rāmo bharatena tāmyatā prasādyamānaḥ śirasā mahīpatiḥ
na caiva cakre gamanāya sattvavān matiṃ pitus tadvacane pratiṣṭhitaḥ  Ram
tad adbhutaṃ sthairyam avekṣya rāghave samaṃ jano harṣam avāpa duḥkhitaḥ
na yāty ayodhyām iti duḥkhito 'bhavat sthirapratijñatvam avekṣya harṣitaḥ  Ram
tam ṛtvijo naigamayūthavallabhās tathā visaṃjñāśrukalāś ca mātaraḥ
tathā bruvāṇaṃ bharataṃ pratuṣṭuvuḥ praṇamya rāmaṃ ca yayācire saha  Ram
punar evaṃ bruvāṇaṃ tu bharataṃ lakṣmaṇāgrajaḥ
pratyuvāca tataḥ śrīmāñ jñātimadhye 'tisatkṛtaḥ  Ram
upapannam idaṃ vākyaṃ yat tvam evam abhāṣathāḥ
jātaḥ putro daśarathāt kaikeyyāṃ rājasattamāt  Ram
purā bhrātaḥ pitā naḥ sa mātaraṃ te samudvahan
mātāmahe samāśrauṣīd rājyaśulkam anuttamam  Ram
devāsure ca saṃgrāme jananyai tava pārthivaḥ
samprahṛṣṭo dadau rājā varam ārādhitaḥ prabhuḥ  Ram
tataḥ sā saṃpratiśrāvya tava mātā yaśasvinī
ayācata naraśreṣṭhaṃ dvau varau varavarṇinī  Ram
tava rājyaṃ naravyāghra mama pravrājanaṃ tathā
tac ca rājā tathā tasyai niyuktaḥ pradadau varam  Ram
tena pitrāham apy atra niyuktaḥ puruṣarṣabha
caturdaśa vane vāsaṃ varṣāṇi varadānikam  Ram
so 'haṃ vanam idaṃ prāpto nirjanaṃ lakṣmaṇānvitaḥ
śītayā cāpratidvandvaḥ satyavāde sthitaḥ pituḥ  Ram
bhavān api tathety eva pitaraṃ satyavādinam
kartum arhati rājendraṃ kṣipram evābhiṣecanāt  Ram
ṛṇān mocaya rājānaṃ matkṛte bharata prabhum
pitaraṃ trāhi dharmajña mātaraṃ cābhinandaya  Ram
śrūyate hi purā tāta śrutir gītā yaśasvinī
gayena yajamānena gayeṣv eva pitṝn prati  Ram
puṃnāmnā narakād yasmāt pitaraṃ trāyate sutaḥ
tasmāt putra iti proktaḥ pitṝn yat pāti vā sutaḥ  Ram
eṣṭavyā bahavaḥ putrā guṇavanto bahuśrutāḥ
teṣāṃ vai samavetānām api kaścid gayāṃ vrajet  Ram
evaṃ rājarṣayaḥ sarve pratītā rājanandana
tasmāt trāhi naraśreṣṭha pitaraṃ narakāt prabho  Ram
ayodhyāṃ gaccha bharata prakṛtīr anurañjaya
śatrughnasahito vīra saha sarvair dvijātibhiḥ  Ram
pravekṣye daṇḍakāraṇyam aham apy avilambayan
ābhyāṃ tu sahito rājan vaidehyā lakṣmaṇena ca  Ram
tvaṃ rājā bhava bharata svayaṃ narāṇāṃ vanyānām aham api rājarāṇ mṛgāṇām
gaccha tvaṃ puravaram adya samprahṛṣṭaḥ saṃhṛṣṭas tv aham api daṇḍakān pravekṣye  Ram
chāyāṃ te dinakarabhāḥ prabādhamānaṃ varṣatraṃ bharata karotu mūrdhni śītām
eteṣām aham api kānanadrumāṇāṃ chāyāṃ tām atiśayinīṃ sukhaṃ śrayiṣye  Ram
śatrughnaḥ kuśalamatis tu te sahāyaḥ saumitrir mama viditaḥ pradhānamitram
catvāras tanayavarā vayaṃ narendraṃ satyasthaṃ bharata carāma mā viṣādam  Ram
āśvāsayantaṃ bharataṃ jābālir brāhmaṇottamaḥ
uvāca rāmaṃ dharmajñaṃ dharmāpetam idaṃ vacaḥ  Ram
sādhu rāghava mā bhūt te buddhir evaṃ nirarthakā
prākṛtasya narasyeva āryabuddhes tapasvinaḥ  Ram
kaḥ kasya puruṣo bandhuḥ kim āpyaṃ kasya kenacit
yad eko jāyate jantur eka eva vinaśyati  Ram
tasmān mātā pitā ceti rāma sajjeta yo naraḥ
unmatta iva sa jñeyo nāsti kāciddhi kasyacit  Ram
yathā grāmāntaraṃ gacchan naraḥ kaścit kvacid vaset
utsṛjya ca tam āvāsaṃ pratiṣṭhetāpare 'hani  Ram
evam eva manuṣyāṇāṃ pitā mātā gṛhaṃ vasu
āvāsamātraṃ kākutstha sajjante nātra sajjanāḥ  Ram
pitryaṃ rājyaṃ samutsṛjya sa nārhati narottama
āsthātuṃ kāpathaṃ duḥkhaṃ viṣamaṃ bahukaṇṭakam  Ram
samṛddhāyām ayodhyāyām ātmānam abhiṣecaya
ekaveṇīdharā hi tvāṃ nagarī sampratīkṣate  Ram
rājabhogān anubhavan mahārhān pārthivātmaja
vihara tvam ayodhyāyāṃ yathā śakras triviṣṭape  Ram
na te kaścid daśaratas tvaṃ ca tasya na kaścana
anyo rājā tvam anyaś ca tasmāt kuru yad ucyate  Ram
gataḥ sa nṛpatis tatra gantavyaṃ yatra tena vai
pravṛttir eṣā martyānāṃ tvaṃ tu mithyā vihanyase  Ram
arthadharmaparā ye ye tāṃs tāñ śocāmi netarān
te hi duḥkham iha prāpya vināśaṃ pretya bhejire  Ram
aṣṭakāpitṛdaivatyam ity ayaṃ prasṛto janaḥ
annasyopadravaṃ paśya mṛto hi kim aśiṣyati  Ram
yadi bhuktam ihānyena deham anyasya gacchati
dadyāt pravasataḥ śrāddhaṃ na tat pathy aśanaṃ bhavet  Ram
dānasaṃvananā hy ete granthā medhāvibhiḥ kṛtāḥ
yajasva dehi dīkṣasva tapas tapyasva saṃtyaja  Ram
sa nāsti param ity eva kuru buddhiṃ mahāmate
pratyakṣaṃ yat tad ātiṣṭha parokṣaṃ pṛṣṭhataḥ kuru  Ram
satāṃ buddhiṃ puraskṛtya sarvalokanidarśinīm
rājyaṃ tvaṃ pratigṛhṇīṣva bharatena prasāditaḥ  Ram
jābāles tu vacaḥ śrutvā rāmaḥ satyātmanāṃ varaḥ
uvāca parayā yuktyā svabuddhyā cāvipannayā  Ram
bhavān me priyakāmārthaṃ vacanaṃ yad ihoktavān
akāryaṃ kāryasaṃkāśam apathyaṃ pathyasaṃmitam  Ram
nirmaryādas tu puruṣaḥ pāpācārasamanvitaḥ
mānaṃ na labhate satsu bhinnacāritradarśanaḥ  Ram
kulīnam akulīnaṃ vā vīraṃ puruṣamāninam
cāritram eva vyākhyāti śuciṃ vā yadi vāśucim  Ram
anāryas tv āryasaṃkāśaḥ śaucāddhīnas tathā śuciḥ
lakṣaṇyavad alakṣaṇyo duḥśīlaḥ śīlavān iva  Ram
adharmaṃ dharmaveṣeṇa yadīmaṃ lokasaṃkaram
abhipatsye śubhaṃ hitvā kriyāvidhivivarjitam  Ram
kaś cetayānaḥ puruṣaḥ kāryākāryavicakṣaṇaḥ
bahu maṃsyati māṃ loke durvṛttaṃ lokadūṣaṇam  Ram
kasya yāsyāmy ahaṃ vṛttaṃ kena vā svargam āpnuyām
anayā vartamāno 'haṃ vṛttyā hīnapratijñayā  Ram
kāmavṛttas tv ayaṃ lokaḥ kṛtsnaḥ samupavartate
yadvṛttāḥ santi rājānas tadvṛttāḥ santi hi prajāḥ  Ram
satyam evānṛśaṃsyaṃ ca rājavṛttaṃ sanātanam
tasmāt satyātmakaṃ rājyaṃ satye lokaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ  Ram
ṛṣayaś caiva devāś ca satyam eva hi menire
satyavādī hi loke 'smin paramaṃ gacchati kṣayam  Ram
udvijante yathā sarpān narād anṛtavādinaḥ
dharmaḥ satyaṃ paro loke mūlaṃ svargasya cocyate  Ram
satyam eveśvaro loke satyaṃ padmā samāśritā
satyamūlāni sarvāṇi satyān nāsti paraṃ padam  Ram
dattam iṣṭaṃ hutaṃ caiva taptāni ca tapāṃsi ca
vedāḥ satyapratiṣṭhānās tasmāt satyaparo bhavet  Ram
ekaḥ pālayate lokam ekaḥ pālayate kulam
majjaty eko hi niraya ekaḥ svarge mahīyate  Ram
so 'haṃ pitur nideśaṃ tu kimarthaṃ nānupālaye
satyapratiśravaḥ satyaṃ satyena samayīkṛtaḥ  Ram
naiva lobhān na mohād vā na cājñānāt tamo'nvitaḥ
setuṃ satyasya bhetsyāmi guroḥ satyapratiśravaḥ  Ram
asatyasaṃdhasya sataś calasyāsthiracetasaḥ
naiva devā na pitaraḥ pratīcchantīti naḥ śrutam  Ram
pratyagātmam imaṃ dharmaṃ satyaṃ paśyāmy ahaṃ svayam
bhāraḥ satpuruṣācīrṇas tadartham abhinandyate  Ram
kṣātraṃ dharmam ahaṃ tyakṣye hy adharmaṃ dharmasaṃhitam
kṣudrair nṛśaṃsair lubdhaiś ca sevitaṃ pāpakarmabhiḥ  Ram
kāyena kurute pāpaṃ manasā sampradhārya ca
anṛtaṃ jihvayā cāha trividhaṃ karma pātakam  Ram
bhūmiḥ kīrtir yaśo lakṣmīḥ puruṣaṃ prārthayanti hi
svargasthaṃ cānubadhnanti satyam eva bhajeta tat  Ram
śreṣṭhaṃ hy anāryam eva syād yad bhavān avadhārya mām
āha yuktikarair vākyair idaṃ bhadraṃ kuruṣva ha  Ram
kathaṃ hy ahaṃ pratijñāya vanavāsam imaṃ guroḥ
bharatasya kariṣyāmi vaco hitvā guror vacaḥ  Ram
sthirā mayā pratijñātā pratijñā gurusaṃnidhau
prahṛṣṭamānasā devī kaikeyī cābhavat tadā  Ram
vanavāsaṃ vasann evaṃ śucir niyatabhojanaḥ
mūlaiḥ puṣpaiḥ phalaiḥ puṇyaiḥ pitṝn devāṃś ca tarpayan  Ram
saṃtuṣṭapañcavargo 'haṃ lokayātrāṃ pravartaye
akuhaḥ śraddadhānaḥ san kāryākāryavicakṣaṇaḥ  Ram
karmabhūmim imāṃ prāpya kartavyaṃ karma yac chubham
agnir vāyuś ca somaś ca karmaṇāṃ phalabhāginaḥ  Ram
śataṃ kratūnām āhṛtya devarāṭ tridivaṃ gataḥ
tapāṃsy ugrāṇi cāsthāya divaṃ yātā maharṣayaḥ  Ram
satyaṃ ca dharmaṃ ca parākramaṃ ca bhūtānukampāṃ priyavāditāṃ ca
dvijātidevātithipūjanaṃ ca panthānam āhus tridivasya santaḥ  Ram
dharme ratāḥ satpuruṣaiḥ sametās tejasvino dānaguṇapradhānāḥ
ahiṃsakā vītamalāś ca loke bhavanti pūjyā munayaḥ pradhānāḥ  Ram
kruddham ājñāya rāmaṃ tu vasiṣṭhaḥ pratyuvāca ha
jābālir api jānīte lokasyāsya gatāgatim
nivartayitukāmas tu tvām etad vākyam abravīt  Ram
imāṃ lokasamutpattiṃ lokanātha nibodha me
sarvaṃ salilam evāsīt pṛthivī yatra nirmitā
tataḥ samabhavad brahmā svayambhūr daivataiḥ saha  Ram
sa varāhas tato bhūtvā projjahāra vasuṃdharām
asṛjac ca jagat sarvaṃ saha putraiḥ kṛtātmabhiḥ  Ram
ākāśaprabhavo brahmā śāśvato nitya avyayaḥ
tasmān marīciḥ saṃjajñe marīceḥ kaśyapaḥ sutaḥ  Ram
vivasvān kaśyapāj jajñe manur vaivasvataḥ smṛtaḥ
sa tu prajāpatiḥ pūrvam ikṣvākus tu manoḥ sutaḥ  Ram
yasyeyaṃ prathamaṃ dattā samṛddhā manunā mahī
tam ikṣvākum ayodhyāyāṃ rājānaṃ viddhi pūrvakam  Ram
ikṣvākos tu sutaḥ śrīmān kukṣir eveti viśrutaḥ
kukṣer athātmajo vīro vikukṣir udapadyata  Ram
vikukṣes tu mahātejā bāṇaḥ putraḥ pratāpavān
bāṇasya tu mahābāhur anaraṇyo mahāyaśāḥ  Ram
nānāvṛṣṭir babhūvāsmin na durbhikṣaṃ satāṃ vare
anaraṇye mahārāje taskaro vāpi kaścana  Ram
anaraṇyān mahābāhuḥ pṛthū rājā babhūva ha
tasmāt pṛthor mahārājas triśaṅkur udapadyata
sa satyavacanād vīraḥ saśarīro divaṃ gataḥ  Ram
triśaṅkor abhavat sūnur dhundhumāro mahāyaśāḥ
dhundhumārān mahātejā yuvanāśvo vyajāyata  Ram
yuvanāśvasutaḥ śrīmān māndhātā samapadyata
māndhātus tu mahātejāḥ susaṃdhir udapadyata  Ram
susaṃdher api putrau dvau dhruvasaṃdhiḥ prasenajit
yaśasvī dhruvasaṃdhes tu bharato ripusūdanaḥ  Ram
bharatāt tu mahābāhor asito nāma jāyata
yasyaite pratirājāna udapadyanta śatravaḥ
haihayās tālajaṅghāś ca śūrāś ca śaśabindavaḥ  Ram
tāṃs tu sarvān prativyūhya yuddhe rājā pravāsitaḥ
sa ca śailavare ramye babhūvābhirato muniḥ
dve cāsya bhārye garbhiṇyau babhūvatur iti śrutiḥ  Ram
bhārgavaś cyavano nāma himavantam upāśritaḥ
tam ṛṣiṃ samupāgamya kālindī tv abhyavādayat  Ram
sa tām abhyavadad vipro varepsuṃ putrajanmani
tataḥ sā gṛham āgamya devī putraṃ vyajāyata  Ram
sapatnyā tu garas tasyai datto garbhajighāṃsayā
gareṇa saha tenaiva jātaḥ sa sagaro 'bhavat  Ram
sa rājā sagaro nāma yaḥ samudram akhānayat
iṣṭvā parvaṇi vegena trāsayantam imāḥ prajāḥ  Ram
asamañjas tu putro 'bhūt sagarasyeti naḥ śrutam
jīvann eva sa pitrā tu nirastaḥ pāpakarmakṛt  Ram
aṃśumān iti putro 'bhūd asamañjasya vīryavān
dilīpo 'ṃśumataḥ putro dilīpasya bhagīrathaḥ  Ram
bhagīrathāt kakutsthas tu kākutsthā yena tu smṛtāḥ
kakutsthasya tu putro 'bhūd raghur yena tu rāghavaḥ  Ram
raghos tu putras tejasvī pravṛddhaḥ puruṣādakaḥ
kalmāṣapādaḥ saudāsa ity evaṃ prathito bhuvi  Ram
kalmāṣapādaputro 'bhūc chaṅkhaṇas tv iti viśrutaḥ
yas tu tad vīryam āsādya sahaseno vyanīnaśat  Ram
śaṅkhaṇasya tu putro 'bhūc chūraḥ śrīmān sudarśanaḥ
sudarśanasyāgnivarṇa agnivarṇasya śīghragaḥ  Ram
śīghragasya maruḥ putro maroḥ putraḥ praśuśrukaḥ
praśuśrukasya putro 'bhūd ambarīṣo mahādyutiḥ  Ram
ambarīṣasya putro 'bhūn nahuṣaḥ satyavikramaḥ
nahuṣasya ca nābhāgaḥ putraḥ paramadhārmikaḥ  Ram
ajaś ca suvrataś caiva nābhāgasya sutāv ubhau
ajasya caiva dharmātmā rājā daśarathaḥ sutaḥ  Ram
tasya jyeṣṭho 'si dāyādo rāma ity abhiviśrutaḥ
tad gṛhāṇa svakaṃ rājyam avekṣasva jagan nṛpa  Ram
ikṣvākūṇāṃ hi sarveṣāṃ rājā bhavati pūrvajaḥ
pūrvajenāvaraḥ putro jyeṣṭho rājye 'bhiṣicyate  Ram
sa rāghavāṇāṃ kuladharmam ātmanaḥ sanātanaṃ nādya vihātum arhasi
prabhūtaratnām anuśādhi medinīṃ prabhūtarāṣṭrāṃ pitṛvan mahāyaśāḥ  Ram
vasiṣṭhas tu tadā rāmam uktvā rājapurohitaḥ
abravīd dharmasaṃyuktaṃ punar evāparaṃ vacaḥ  Ram
puruṣasyeha jātasya bhavanti guravas trayaḥ
ācāryaś caiva kākutstha pitā mātā ca rāghava  Ram
pitā hy enaṃ janayati puruṣaṃ puruṣarṣabha
prajñāṃ dadāti cācāryas tasmāt sa gurur ucyate  Ram
sa te 'haṃ pitur ācāryas tava caiva paraṃtapa
mama tvaṃ vacanaṃ kurvan nātivarteḥ satāṃ gatim  Ram
imā hi te pariṣadaḥ śreṇayaś ca samāgatāḥ
eṣu tāta caran dharmaṃ nātivarteḥ satāṃ gatim  Ram
vṛddhāyā dharmaśīlāyā mātur nārhasy avartitum
asyās tu vacanaṃ kurvan nātivarteḥ satāṃ gatim  Ram
bharatasya vacaḥ kurvan yācamānasya rāghava
ātmānaṃ nātivartes tvaṃ satyadharmaparākrama  Ram
evaṃ madhuram uktas tu guruṇā rāghavaḥ svayam
pratyuvāca samāsīnaṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ puruṣarṣabhaḥ  Ram
yan mātāpitarau vṛttaṃ tanaye kurutaḥ sadā
na supratikaraṃ tat tu mātrā pitrā ca yat kṛtam  Ram
yathāśakti pradānena snāpanāc chādanena ca
nityaṃ ca priyavādena tathā saṃvardhanena ca  Ram
sa hi rājā janayitā pitā daśaratho mama
ājñātaṃ yan mayā tasya na tan mithyā bhaviṣyati  Ram
evam uktas tu rāmeṇa bharataḥ pratyanantaram
uvāca paramodāraḥ sūtaṃ paramadurmanāḥ  Ram
iha me sthaṇḍile śīghraṃ kuśān āstara sārathe
āryaṃ pratyupavekṣyāmi yāvan me na prasīdati  Ram
anāhāro nirāloko dhanahīno yathā dvijaḥ
śeṣye purastāc chālāyā yāvan na pratiyāsyati  Ram
sa tu rāmam avekṣantaṃ sumantraṃ prekṣya durmanāḥ
kuśottaram upasthāpya bhūmāv evāstarat svayam  Ram
tam uvāca mahātejā rāmo rājarṣisattamāḥ
kiṃ māṃ bharata kurvāṇaṃ tāta pratyupavekṣyasi  Ram
brāhmaṇo hy ekapārśvena narān roddhum ihārhati
na tu mūrdhāvasiktānāṃ vidhiḥ pratyupaveśane  Ram
uttiṣṭha naraśārdūla hitvaitad dāruṇaṃ vratam
puravaryām itaḥ kṣipram ayodhyāṃ yāhi rāghava  Ram
āsīnas tv eva bharataḥ paurajānapadaṃ janam
uvāca sarvataḥ prekṣya kim āryaṃ nānuśāsatha  Ram
te tam ūcur mahātmānaṃ paurajānapadā janāḥ
kākutstham abhijānīmaḥ samyag vadati rāghavaḥ  Ram
eṣo 'pi hi mahābhāgaḥ pitur vacasi tiṣṭhati
ata eva na śaktāḥ smo vyāvartayitum añjasā  Ram
teṣām ājñāya vacanaṃ rāmo vacanam abravīt
evaṃ nibodha vacanaṃ suhṛdāṃ dharmacakṣuṣām  Ram
etac caivobhayaṃ śrutvā samyak saṃpaśya rāghava
uttiṣṭha tvaṃ mahābāho māṃ ca spṛśa tathodakam  Ram
athotthāya jalaṃ spṛṣṭvā bharato vākyam abravīt
śṛṇvantu me pariṣado mantriṇaḥ śreṇayas tathā  Ram
na yāce pitaraṃ rājyaṃ nānuśāsāmi mātaram
āryaṃ paramadharmajñam abhijānāmi rāghavam  Ram
yadi tv avaśyaṃ vastavyaṃ kartavyaṃ ca pitur vacaḥ
aham eva nivatsyāmi caturdaśa vane samāḥ  Ram
dharmātmā tasya tathyena bhrātur vākyena vismitaḥ
uvāca rāmaḥ samprekṣya paurajānapadaṃ janam  Ram
vikrītam āhitaṃ krītaṃ yat pitrā jīvatā mama
na tal lopayituṃ śakyaṃ mayā vā bharatena vā  Ram
upadhir na mayā kāryo vanavāse jugupsitaḥ
yuktam uktaṃ ca kaikeyyā pitrā me sukṛtaṃ kṛtam  Ram
jānāmi bharataṃ kṣāntaṃ gurusatkārakāriṇam
sarvam evātra kalyāṇaṃ satyasaṃdhe mahātmani  Ram
anena dharmaśīlena vanāt pratyāgataḥ punaḥ
bhrātrā saha bhaviṣyāmi pṛthivyāḥ patir uttamaḥ  Ram
vṛto rājā hi kaikeyyā mayā tadvacanaṃ kṛtam
anṛtān mocayānena pitaraṃ taṃ mahīpatim  Ram
tam apratimatejobhyāṃ bhrātṛbhyāṃ romaharṣaṇam
vismitāḥ saṃgamaṃ prekṣya samavetā maharṣayaḥ  Ram
antarhitās tv ṛṣigaṇāḥ siddhāś ca paramarṣayaḥ
tau bhrātarau mahātmānau kākutsthau praśaśaṃsire  Ram
sa dhanyo yasya putrau dvau dharmajñau dharmavikramau
śrutvā vayaṃ hi sambhāṣām ubhayoḥ spṛhayāmahe  Ram
tatas tv ṛṣigaṇāḥ kṣipraṃ daśagrīvavadhaiṣiṇaḥ
bharataṃ rājaśārdūlam ity ūcuḥ saṃgatā vacaḥ  Ram
kule jāta mahāprājña mahāvṛtta mahāyaśaḥ
grāhyaṃ rāmasya vākyaṃ te pitaraṃ yady avekṣase  Ram
sadānṛṇam imaṃ rāmaṃ vayam icchāmahe pituḥ
anṛṇatvāc ca kaikeyyāḥ svargaṃ daśaratho gataḥ  Ram
etāvad uktvā vacanaṃ gandharvāḥ samaharṣayaḥ
rājarṣayaś caiva tathā sarve svāṃ svāṃ gatiṃ gatāḥ  Ram
hlāditas tena vākyena śubhena śubhadarśanaḥ
rāmaḥ saṃhṛṣṭavadanas tān ṛṣīn abhyapūjayat  Ram
srastagātras tu bharataḥ sa vācā sajjamānayā
kṛtāñjalir idaṃ vākyaṃ rāghavaṃ punar abravīt  Ram
rājadharmam anuprekṣya kuladharmānusaṃtatim
kartum arhasi kākutstha mama mātuś ca yācanām  Ram
rakṣituṃ sumahad rājyam aham ekas tu notsahe
paurajānapadāṃś cāpi raktān rañjayituṃ tathā  Ram
jñātayaś ca hi yodhāś ca mitrāṇi suhṛdaś ca naḥ
tvām eva pratikāṅkṣante parjanyam iva karṣakāḥ  Ram
idaṃ rājyaṃ mahāprājña sthāpaya pratipadya hi
śaktimān asi kākutstha lokasya paripālane  Ram
ity uktvā nyapatad bhrātuḥ pādayor bharatas tadā
bhṛśaṃ samprārthayāmāsa rāmam evaṃ priyaṃvadaḥ  Ram
tam aṅke bhrātaraṃ kṛtvā rāmo vacanam abravīt
śyāmaṃ nalinapattrākṣaṃ mattahaṃsasvaraṃ svayam  Ram
āgatā tvām iyaṃ buddhiḥ svajā vainayikī ca yā
bhṛśam utsahase tāta rakṣituṃ pṛthivīm api  Ram
amātyaiś ca suhṛdbhiś ca buddhimadbhiś ca mantribhiḥ
sarvakāryāṇi saṃmantrya sumahānty api kāraya  Ram
lakṣmīś candrād apeyād vā himavān vā himaṃ tyajet
atīyāt sāgaro velāṃ na pratijñām ahaṃ pituḥ  Ram
kāmād vā tāta lobhād vā mātrā tubhyam idaṃ kṛtam
na tan manasi kartavyaṃ vartitavyaṃ ca mātṛvat  Ram
evaṃ bruvāṇaṃ bharataḥ kausalyāsutam abravīt
tejasādityasaṃkāśaṃ pratipaccandradarśanam  Ram
adhirohārya pādābhyāṃ pāduke hemabhūṣite
ete hi sarvalokasya yogakṣemaṃ vidhāsyataḥ  Ram
so 'dhiruhya naravyāghraḥ pāduke hy avaruhya ca
prāyacchat sumahātejā bharatāya mahātmane  Ram
sa pāduke te bharataḥ pratāpavān svalaṃkṛte samparigṛhya dharmavit
pradakṣiṇaṃ caiva cakāra rāghavaṃ cakāra caivottamanāgamūrdhani  Ram
athānupūrvyāt pratipūjya taṃ janaṃ gurūṃś ca mantriprakṛtīs tathānujau
vyasarjayad rāghavavaṃśavardhanaḥ sthitaḥ svadharme himavān ivācalaḥ  Ram
taṃ mātaro bāṣpagṛhītakaṇṭhyo duḥkhena nāmantrayituṃ hi śekuḥ
sa tv eva mātṝn abhivādya sarvā rudan kuṭīṃ svāṃ praviveśa rāmaḥ  Ram
tataḥ śirasi kṛtvā tu pāduke bharatas tadā
āruroha rathaṃ hṛṣṭaḥ śatrughnena samanvitaḥ  Ram
vasiṣṭho vāmadevaś ca jābāliś ca dṛḍhavrataḥ
agrataḥ prayayuḥ sarve mantriṇo mantrapūjitāḥ  Ram
mandākinīṃ nadīṃ ramyāṃ prāṅmukhās te yayus tadā
pradakṣiṇaṃ ca kurvāṇāś citrakūṭaṃ mahāgirim  Ram
paśyan dhātusahasrāṇi ramyāṇi vividhāni ca
prayayau tasya pārśvena sasainyo bharatas tadā  Ram
adūrāc citrakūṭasya dadarśa bharatas tadā
āśramaṃ yatra sa munir bharadvājaḥ kṛtālayaḥ  Ram
sa tam āśramam āgamya bharadvājasya buddhimān
avatīrya rathāt pādau vavande kulanandanaḥ  Ram
tato hṛṣṭo bharadvājo bharataṃ vākyam abravīt
api kṛtyaṃ kṛtaṃ tāta rāmeṇa ca samāgatam  Ram
evam uktas tu bharato bharadvājena dhīmatā
pratyuvāca bharadvājaṃ bharato dharmavatsalaḥ  Ram
sa yācyamāno guruṇā mayā ca dṛḍhavikramaḥ
rāghavaḥ paramaprīto vasiṣṭhaṃ vākyam abravīt  Ram
pituḥ pratijñāṃ tām eva pālayiṣyāmi tattvataḥ
caturdaśa hi varṣāṇi yā pratijñā pitur mama  Ram
evam ukto mahāprājño vasiṣṭhaḥ pratyuvāca ha
vākyajño vākyakuśalaṃ rāghavaṃ vacanaṃ mahat  Ram
ete prayaccha saṃhṛṣṭaḥ pāduke hemabhūṣite
ayodhyāyāṃ mahāprājña yogakṣemakare tava  Ram
evam ukto vasiṣṭhena rāghavaḥ prāṅmukhaḥ sthitaḥ
pāduke hemavikṛte mama rājyāya te dadau  Ram
nivṛtto 'ham anujñāto rāmeṇa sumahātmanā
ayodhyām eva gacchāmi gṛhītvā pāduke śubhe  Ram
etac chrutvā śubhaṃ vākyaṃ bharatasya mahātmanaḥ
bharadvājaḥ śubhataraṃ munir vākyam udāharat  Ram
naitac citraṃ naravyāghra śīlavṛttavatāṃ vara
yad āryaṃ tvayi tiṣṭhet tu nimne vṛṣṭim ivodakam  Ram
amṛtaḥ sa mahābāhuḥ pitā daśarathas tava
yasya tvam īdṛśaḥ putro dharmātmā dharmavatsalaḥ  Ram
tam ṛṣiṃ tu mahātmānam uktavākyaṃ kṛtāñjaliḥ
āmantrayitum ārebhe caraṇāv upagṛhya ca  Ram
tataḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā bharadvājaṃ punaḥ punaḥ
bharatas tu yayau śrīmān ayodhyāṃ saha mantribhiḥ  Ram
yānaiś ca śakaṭaiś caiva hayair nāgaiś ca sā camūḥ
punar nivṛttā vistīrṇā bharatasyānuyāyinī  Ram
tatas te yamunāṃ divyāṃ nadīṃ tīrtvormimālinīm
dadṛśus tāṃ punaḥ sarve gaṅgāṃ śivajalāṃ nadīm  Ram
tāṃ ramyajalasampūrṇāṃ saṃtīrya sahabāndhavaḥ
śṛṅgaverapuraṃ ramyaṃ praviveśa sasainikaḥ  Ram
śṛṅgaverapurād bhūya ayodhyāṃ saṃdadarśa ha
bharato duḥkhasaṃtaptaḥ sārathiṃ cedam abravīt  Ram
sārathe paśya vidhvastā ayodhyā na prakāśate
nirākārā nirānandā dīnā pratihatasvanā  Ram
snigdhagambhīraghoṣeṇa syandanenopayān prabhuḥ
ayodhyāṃ bharataḥ kṣipraṃ praviveśa mahāyaśāḥ  Ram
biḍālolūkacaritām ālīnanaravāraṇām
timirābhyāhatāṃ kālīm aprakāśāṃ niśām iva  Ram
rāhuśatroḥ priyāṃ patnīṃ śriyā prajvalitaprabhām
graheṇābhyutthitenaikāṃ rohiṇīm iva pīḍitām  Ram
alpoṣṇakṣubdhasalilāṃ gharmottaptavihaṃgamām
līnamīnajhaṣagrāhāṃ kṛśāṃ girinadīm iva  Ram
vidhūmām iva hemābhām adhvarāgnisamutthitām
havirabhyukṣitāṃ paścāc chikhāṃ vipralayaṃ gatām  Ram
vidhvastakavacāṃ rugṇagajavājirathadhvajām
hatapravīrām āpannāṃ camūm iva mahāhave  Ram
saphenāṃ sasvanāṃ bhūtvā sāgarasya samutthitām
praśāntamārutoddhūtāṃ jalormim iva niḥsvanām  Ram
tyaktāṃ yajñāyudhaiḥ sarvair abhirūpaiś ca yājakaiḥ
sutyākāle vinirvṛtte vediṃ gataravām iva  Ram
goṣṭhamadhye sthitām ārtām acarantīṃ navaṃ tṛṇam
govṛṣeṇa parityaktāṃ gavāṃ patnīm ivotsukām  Ram
prabhākarālaiḥ susnigdhaiḥ prajvaladbhir ivottamaiḥ
viyuktāṃ maṇibhir jātyair navāṃ muktāvalīm iva  Ram
sahasā calitāṃ sthānān mahīṃ puṇyakṣayād gatām
saṃhṛtadyutivistārāṃ tārām iva divaś cyutām  Ram
puṣpanaddhāṃ vasantānte mattabhramaraśālinīm
drutadāvāgnivipruṣṭāṃ klāntāṃ vanalatām iva  Ram
saṃmūḍhanigamāṃ sarvāṃ saṃkṣiptavipaṇāpaṇām
pracchannaśaśinakṣatrāṃ dyām ivāmbudharair vṛtām  Ram
kṣīṇapānottamair bhinnaiḥ śarāvair abhisaṃvṛtām
hataśauṇḍām ivākāśe pānabhūmim asaṃskṛtām  Ram
vṛkṇabhūmitalāṃ nimnāṃ vṛkṇapātraiḥ samāvṛtām
upayuktodakāṃ bhagnāṃ prapāṃ nipatitām iva  Ram
vipulāṃ vitatāṃ caiva yuktapāśāṃ tarasvinām
bhūmau bāṇair viniṣkṛttāṃ patitāṃ jyām ivāyudhāt  Ram
sahasā yuddhaśauṇḍena hayāroheṇa vāhitām
nikṣiptabhāṇḍām utsṛṣṭāṃ kiśorīm iva durbalām  Ram
prāvṛṣi pravigāḍhāyāṃ praviṣṭasyābhramaṇḍalam
pracchannāṃ nīlajīmūtair bhāskarasya prabhām iva  Ram
bharatas tu rathasthaḥ sañ śrīmān daśarathātmajaḥ
vāhayantaṃ rathaśreṣṭhaṃ sārathiṃ vākyam abravīt  Ram
kiṃ nu khalv adya gambhīro mūrchito na niśamyate
yathāpuram ayodhyāyāṃ gītavāditraniḥsvanaḥ  Ram
vāruṇīmadagandhāś ca mālyagandhaś ca mūrchitaḥ
dhūpitāgarugandhaś ca na pravāti samantataḥ  Ram
yānapravaraghoṣaś ca snigdhaś ca hayaniḥsvanaḥ
pramattagajanādaś ca mahāṃś ca rathaniḥsvanaḥ
nedānīṃ śrūyate puryām asyāṃ rāme vivāsite  Ram
taruṇaiś cāruveṣaiś ca narair unnatagāmibhiḥ
saṃpatadbhir ayodhyāyāṃ na vibhānti mahāpathāḥ  Ram
evaṃ bahuvidhaṃ jalpan viveśa vasatiṃ pituḥ
tena hīnāṃ narendreṇa siṃhahīnāṃ guhām iva  Ram
tato nikṣipya mātṝn sa ayodhyāyāṃ dṛḍhavrataḥ
bharataḥ śokasaṃtapto gurūn idam athābravīt  Ram
nandigrāmaṃ gamiṣyāmi sarvān āmantraye 'dya vaḥ
tatra duḥkham idaṃ sarvaṃ sahiṣye rāghavaṃ vinā  Ram
gataś ca hi divaṃ rājā vanasthaś ca gurur mama
rāmaṃ pratīkṣe rājyāya sa hi rājā mahāyaśāḥ  Ram
etac chrutvā śubhaṃ vākyaṃ bharatasya mahātmanaḥ
abruvan mantriṇaḥ sarve vasiṣṭhaś ca purohitaḥ  Ram
sadṛśaṃ ślāghanīyaṃ ca yad uktaṃ bharata tvayā
vacanaṃ bhrātṛvātsalyād anurūpaṃ tavaiva tat  Ram
nityaṃ te bandhulubdhasya tiṣṭhato bhrātṛsauhṛde
āryamārgaṃ prapannasya nānumanyeta kaḥ pumān  Ram
mantriṇāṃ vacanaṃ śrutvā yathābhilaṣitaṃ priyam
abravīt sārathiṃ vākyaṃ ratho me yujyatām iti  Ram
prahṛṣṭavadanaḥ sarvā mātṝn samabhivādya saḥ
āruroha rathaṃ śrīmāñ śatrughnena samanvitaḥ  Ram
āruhya tu rathaṃ śīghraṃ śatrughnabharatāv ubhau
yayatuḥ paramaprītau vṛtau mantripurohitaiḥ  Ram
agrato guravas tatra vasiṣṭhapramukhā dvijāḥ
prayayuḥ prāṅmukhāḥ sarve nandigrāmo yato 'bhavat  Ram
balaṃ ca tad anāhūtaṃ gajāśvarathasaṃkulam
prayayau bharate yāte sarve ca puravāsinaḥ  Ram
rathasthaḥ sa tu dharmātmā bharato bhrātṛvatsalaḥ
nandigrāmaṃ yayau tūrṇaṃ śirasy ādhāya pāduke  Ram
tatas tu bharataḥ kṣipraṃ nandigrāmaṃ praviśya saḥ
avatīrya rathāt tūrṇaṃ gurūn idam uvāca ha  Ram
etad rājyaṃ mama bhrātrā dattaṃ saṃnyāsavat svayam
yogakṣemavahe ceme pāduke hemabhūṣite
tam imaṃ pālayiṣyāmi rāghavāgamanaṃ prati  Ram
kṣipraṃ saṃyojayitvā tu rāghavasya punaḥ svayam
caraṇau tau tu rāmasya drakṣyāmi sahapādukau  Ram
tato nikṣiptabhāro 'haṃ rāghaveṇa samāgataḥ
nivedya gurave rājyaṃ bhajiṣye guruvṛttitām  Ram
rāghavāya ca saṃnyāsaṃ dattveme varapāduke
rājyaṃ cedam ayodhyāṃ ca dhūtapāpo bhavāmi ca  Ram
abhiṣikte tu kākutsthe prahṛṣṭamudite jane
prītir mama yaśaś caiva bhaved rājyāc caturguṇam  Ram
evaṃ tu vilapan dīno bharataḥ sa mahāyaśāḥ
nandigrāme 'karod rājyaṃ duḥkhito mantribhiḥ saha  Ram
sa valkalajaṭādhārī muniveṣadharaḥ prabhuḥ
nandigrāme 'vasad vīraḥ sasainyo bharatas tadā  Ram
rāmāgamanam ākāṅkṣan bharato bhrātṛvatsalaḥ
bhrātur vacanakārī ca pratijñāpāragas tadā  Ram
pāduke tv abhiṣicyātha nandigrāme 'vasat tadā
bharataḥ śāsanaṃ sarvaṃ pādukābhyāṃ nyavedayat  Ram
pratiprayāte bharate vasan rāmas tapovane
lakṣayāmāsa sodvegam athautsukyaṃ tapasvinām  Ram
ye tatra citrakūṭasya purastāt tāpasāśrame
rāmam āśritya niratās tān alakṣayad utsukān  Ram
nayanair bhṛkuṭībhiś ca rāmaṃ nirdiśya śaṅkitāḥ
anyonyam upajalpantaḥ śanaiś cakrur mithaḥ kathāḥ  Ram
teṣām autsukyam ālakṣya rāmas tv ātmani śaṅkitaḥ
kṛtāñjalir uvācedam ṛṣiṃ kulapatiṃ tataḥ  Ram
na kaccid bhagavan kiṃcit pūrvavṛttam idaṃ mayi
dṛśyate vikṛtaṃ yena vikriyante tapasvinaḥ  Ram
pramādāc caritaṃ kaccit kiṃcin nāvarajasya me
lakṣmaṇasyarṣibhir dṛṣṭaṃ nānurūpam ivātmanaḥ  Ram
kaccic chuśrūṣamāṇā vaḥ śuśrūṣaṇaparā mayi
pramadābhyucitāṃ vṛttiṃ sītā yuktaṃ na vartate  Ram
atharṣir jarayā vṛddhas tapasā ca jarāṃ gataḥ
vepamāna ivovāca rāmaṃ bhūtadayāparam  Ram
kutaḥ kalyāṇasattvāyāḥ kalyāṇābhirates tathā
calanaṃ tāta vaidehyās tapasviṣu viśeṣataḥ  Ram
tvannimittam idaṃ tāvat tāpasān prati vartate
rakṣobhyas tena saṃvignāḥ kathayanti mithaḥ kathāḥ  Ram
rāvaṇāvarajaḥ kaścit kharo nāmeha rākṣasaḥ
utpāṭya tāpasān sarvāñ janasthānaniketanān  Ram
dhṛṣṭaś ca jitakāśī ca nṛśaṃsaḥ puruṣādakaḥ
avaliptaś ca pāpaś ca tvāṃ ca tāta na mṛṣyate  Ram
tvaṃ yadā prabhṛti hy asminn āśrame tāta vartase
tadā prabhṛti rakṣāṃsi viprakurvanti tāpasān  Ram
darśayanti hi bībhatsaiḥ krūrair bhīṣaṇakair api
nānā rūpair virūpaiś ca rūpair asukhadarśanaiḥ  Ram
apraśastair aśucibhiḥ saṃprayojya ca tāpasān
pratighnanty aparān kṣipram anāryāḥ purataḥ sthitāḥ  Ram
teṣu teṣv āśramasthāneṣv abuddham avalīya ca
ramante tāpasāṃs tatra nāśayanto 'lpacetasaḥ  Ram
apakṣipanti srugbhāṇḍān agnīn siñcanti vāriṇā
kalaśāṃś ca pramṛdnanti havane samupasthite  Ram
tair durātmabhir āviṣṭān āśramān prajihāsavaḥ
gamanāyānyadeśasya codayanty ṛṣayo 'dya mām  Ram
tat purā rāma śārīrām upahiṃsāṃ tapasviṣu
darśayanti hi duṣṭās te tyakṣyāma imam āśramam  Ram
bahumūlaphalaṃ citram avidūrād ito vanam
purāṇāśramam evāhaṃ śrayiṣye sagaṇaḥ punaḥ  Ram
kharas tvayy api cāyuktaṃ purā tāta pravartate
sahāsmābhir ito gaccha yadi buddhiḥ pravartate  Ram
sakalatrasya saṃdeho nityaṃ yat tasya rāghava
samarthasyāpi hi sato vāso duḥkham ihādya te  Ram
ity uktavantaṃ rāmas taṃ rājaputras tapasvinam
na śaśākottarair vākyair avaroddhuṃ samutsukam  Ram
abhinandya samāpṛcchya samādhāya ca rāghavam
sa jagāmāśramaṃ tyaktvā kulaiḥ kulapatiḥ saha  Ram
rāmaḥ saṃsādhya tv ṛṣigaṇam anugamanād deśāt tasmāccit kulapatim abhivādya rṣim
samyakprītais tair anumata upadiṣṭārthaḥ puṇyaṃ vāsāya svanilayam upasaṃpede  Ram
āśramaṃ tv ṛṣivirahitaṃ prabhuḥ kṣaṇam api na jahau sa rāghavaḥ
rāghavaṃ hi satatam anugatās tāpasāś cārṣicaritadhṛtaguṇāḥ  Ram
rāghavas tv apayāteṣu tapasviṣu vicintayan
na tatrārocayad vāsaṃ kāraṇair bahubhis tadā  Ram
iha me bharato dṛṣṭo mātaraś ca sanāgarāḥ
sā ca me smṛtir anveti tān nityam anuśocataḥ  Ram
skandhāvāraniveśena tena tasya mahātmanaḥ
hayahastikarīṣaiś ca upamardaḥ kṛto bhṛśam  Ram
tasmād anyatra gacchāma iti saṃcintya rāghavaḥ
prātiṣṭhata sa vaidehyā lakṣmaṇena ca saṃgataḥ  Ram
so 'trer āśramam āsādya taṃ vavande mahāyaśāḥ
taṃ cāpi bhagavān atriḥ putravat pratyapadyata  Ram
svayam ātithyam ādiśya sarvam asya susatkṛtam
saumitriṃ ca mahābhāgāṃ sītāṃ ca samasāntvayat  Ram
patnīṃ ca samanuprāptāṃ vṛddhām āmantrya satkṛtām
sāntvayāmāsa dharmajñaḥ sarvabhūtahite rataḥ  Ram
anasūyāṃ mahābhāgāṃ tāpasīṃ dharmacāriṇīm
pratigṛhṇīṣva vaidehīm abravīd ṛṣisattamaḥ  Ram
rāmāya cācacakṣe tāṃ tāpasīṃ dharmacāriṇīm
daśa varṣāṇy anāvṛṣṭyā dagdhe loke nirantaram  Ram
yayā mūlaphale sṛṣṭe jāhnavī ca pravartitā
ugreṇa tapasā yuktā niyamaiś cāpy alaṃkṛtā  Ram
daśavarṣasahasrāṇi yayā taptaṃ mahat tapaḥ
anasūyāvratais tāta pratyūhāś ca nibarhitāḥ  Ram
devakāryanimittaṃ ca yayā saṃtvaramāṇayā
daśarātraṃ kṛtvā rātriḥ seyaṃ māteva te 'nagha  Ram
tām imāṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ namaskāryāṃ yaśasvinīm
abhigacchatu vaidehī vṛddhām akrodhanāṃ sadā  Ram
evaṃ bruvāṇaṃ tam ṛṣiṃ tathety uktvā sa rāghavaḥ
sītām uvāca dharmajñām idaṃ vacanam uttamam  Ram
rājaputri śrutaṃ tv etan muner asya samīritam
śreyo'rtham ātmanaḥ śīghram abhigaccha tapasvinīm  Ram
anasūyeti yā loke karmabhiḥ khyātim āgatā
tāṃ śīghram abhigaccha tvam abhigamyāṃ tapasvinīm  Ram
sītā tv etad vacaḥ śrutvā rāghavasya hitaiṣiṇī
tām atripatnīṃ dharmajñām abhicakrāma maithilī  Ram
śithilāṃ valitāṃ vṛddhāṃ jarāpāṇḍuramūrdhajām
satataṃ vepamānāṅgīṃ pravāte kadalī yathā  Ram
tāṃ tu sītā mahābhāgām anasūyāṃ pativratām
abhyavādayad avyagrā svaṃ nāma samudāharat  Ram
abhivādya ca vaidehī tāpasīṃ tām aninditām
baddhāñjalipuṭā hṛṣṭā paryapṛcchad anāmayam  Ram
tataḥ sītāṃ mahābhāgāṃ dṛṣṭvā tāṃ dharmacāriṇīm
sāntvayanty abravīd dhṛṣṭā diṣṭyā dharmam avekṣase  Ram
tyaktvā jñātijanaṃ sīte mānam ṛddhiṃ ca mānini
avaruddhaṃ vane rāmaṃ diṣṭyā tvam anugacchasi  Ram
nagarastho vanastho vā pāpo vā yadi vāśubhaḥ
yāsāṃ strīṇāṃ priyo bhartā tāsāṃ lokā mahodayāḥ  Ram
duḥśīlaḥ kāmavṛtto vā dhanair vā parivarjitaḥ
strīṇām āryasvabhāvānāṃ paramaṃ daivataṃ patiḥ  Ram
nāto viśiṣṭaṃ paśyāmi bāndhavaṃ vimṛśanty aham
sarvatra yogyaṃ vaidehi tapaḥ kṛtam ivāvyayam  Ram
na tv evam avagacchanti guṇadoṣam asatstriyaḥ
kāmavaktavyahṛdayā bhartṛnāthāś caranti yāḥ  Ram
prāpnuvanty ayaśaś caiva dharmabhraṃśaṃ ca maithili
akāryavaśam āpannāḥ striyo yāḥ khalu tadvidhāḥ  Ram
tvadvidhās tu guṇair yuktā dṛṣṭalokaparāvarāḥ
striyaḥ svarge cariṣyanti yathā puṇyakṛtas tathā  Ram
sā tv evam uktā vaidehī anasūyānasūyayā
pratipūjya vaco mandaṃ pravaktum upacakrame  Ram
naitad āścaryam āryāyā yan māṃ tvam anubhāṣase
viditaṃ tu mamāpy etad yathā nāryāḥ patir guruḥ  Ram
yady apy eṣa bhaved bhartā mamārye vṛttavarjitaḥ
advaidham upacartavyas tathāpy eṣa mayā bhavet  Ram
kiṃ punar yo guṇaślāghyaḥ sānukrośo jitendriyaḥ
sthirānurāgo dharmātmā mātṛvartī pitṛpriyaḥ  Ram
yāṃ vṛttiṃ vartate rāmaḥ kausalyāyāṃ mahābalaḥ
tām eva nṛpanārīṇām anyāsām api vartate  Ram
sakṛd dṛṣṭāsv api strīṣu nṛpeṇa nṛpavatsalaḥ
mātṛvad vartate vīro mānam utsṛjya dharmavit  Ram
āgacchantyāś ca vijanaṃ vanam evaṃ bhayāvaham
samāhitaṃ hi me śvaśrvā hṛdaye yat sthitaṃ mama  Ram
pāṇipradānakāle ca yat purā tv agnisaṃnidhau
anuśiṣṭā jananyāsmi vākyaṃ tad api me dhṛtam  Ram
navīkṛtaṃ tu tat sarvaṃ vākyais te dharmacāriṇi
patiśuśrūṣaṇān nāryās tapo nānyad vidhīyate  Ram
sāvitrī patiśuśrūṣāṃ kṛtvā svarge mahīyate
tathā vṛttiś ca yātā tvaṃ patiśuśrūṣayā divam  Ram
variṣṭhā sarvanārīṇām eṣā ca divi devatā
rohiṇī ca vinā candraṃ muhūrtam api dṛśyate  Ram
evaṃvidhāś ca pravarāḥ striyo bhartṛdṛḍhavratāḥ
devaloke mahīyante puṇyena svena karmaṇā  Ram
tato 'nasūyā saṃhṛṣṭā śrutvoktaṃ sītayā vacaḥ
śirasy āghrāya covāca maithilīṃ harṣayanty uta  Ram
niyamair vividhair āptaṃ tapo hi mahad asti me
tat saṃśritya balaṃ sīte chandaye tvāṃ śucivrate  Ram
upapannaṃ ca yuktaṃ ca vacanaṃ tava maithili
prītā cāsmy ucitaṃ kiṃ te karavāṇi bravīhi me
kṛtam ity abravīt sītā tapobalasamanvitām  Ram
sā tv evam uktā dharmajñā tayā prītatarābhavat
saphalaṃ ca praharṣaṃ te hanta sīte karomy aham  Ram
idaṃ divyaṃ varaṃ mālyaṃ vastram ābharaṇāni ca
aṅgarāgaṃ ca vaidehi mahārham anulepanam  Ram
mayā dattam idaṃ sīte tava gātrāṇi śobhayet
anurūpam asaṃkliṣṭaṃ nityam eva bhaviṣyati  Ram
aṅgarāgeṇa divyena liptāṅgī janakātmaje
śobhayiṣyāmi bhartāraṃ yathā śrīr viṣṇum avyayam  Ram
sā vastram aṅgarāgaṃ ca bhūṣaṇāni srajas tathā
maithilī pratijagrāha prītidānam anuttamam  Ram
pratigṛhya ca tat sītā prītidānaṃ yaśasvinī
śliṣṭāñjalipuṭā dhīrā samupāsta tapodhanām  Ram
tathā sītām upāsīnām anasūyā dṛḍhavratā
vacanaṃ praṣṭum ārebhe kathāṃ kāṃcid anupriyām  Ram
svayaṃvare kila prāptā tvam anena yaśasvinā
rāghaveṇeti me sīte kathā śrutim upāgatā  Ram
tāṃ kathāṃ śrotum icchāmi vistareṇa ca maithili
yathānubhūtaṃ kārtsnyena tan me tvaṃ vaktum arhasi  Ram
evam uktā tu sā sītā tāṃ tato dharmacāriṇīm
śrūyatām iti coktvā vai kathayāmāsa tāṃ kathām  Ram
mithilādhipatir vīro janako nāma dharmavit
kṣatradharmaṇy abhirato nyāyataḥ śāsti medinīm  Ram
tasya lāṅgalahastasya karṣataḥ kṣetramaṇḍalam
ahaṃ kilotthitā bhittvā jagatīṃ nṛpateḥ sutā  Ram
sa māṃ dṛṣṭvā narapatir muṣṭivikṣepatatparaḥ
pāṃśuguṇṭhitasarvāṅgīṃ vismito janako 'bhavat  Ram
anapatyena ca snehād aṅkam āropya ca svayam
mameyaṃ tanayety uktvā sneho mayi nipātitaḥ  Ram
antarikṣe ca vāg uktā pratimāmānuṣī kila
evam etan narapate dharmeṇa tanayā tava  Ram
tataḥ prahṛṣṭo dharmātmā pitā me mithilādhipaḥ
avāpto vipulām ṛddhiṃ mām avāpya narādhipaḥ  Ram
dattā cāsmīṣṭavad devyai jyeṣṭhāyai puṇyakarmaṇā
tayā saṃbhāvitā cāsmi snigdhayā mātṛsauhṛdāt  Ram
patisaṃyogasulabhaṃ vayo dṛṣṭvā tu me pitā
cintām abhyagamad dīno vittanāśād ivādhanaḥ  Ram
sadṛśāc cāpakṛṣṭāc ca loke kanyāpitā janāt
pradharṣaṇām avāpnoti śakreṇāpi samo bhuvi  Ram
tāṃ dharṣaṇām adūrasthāṃ saṃdṛśyātmani pārthivaḥ
cintārṇavagataḥ pāraṃ nāsasādāplavo yathā  Ram
ayonijāṃ hi māṃ jñātvā nādhyagacchat sa cintayan
sadṛśaṃ cānurūpaṃ ca mahīpālaḥ patiṃ mama  Ram
tasya buddhir iyaṃ jātā cintayānasya saṃtatam
svayaṃ varaṃ tanūjāyāḥ kariṣyāmīti dhīmataḥ  Ram
mahāyajñe tadā tasya varuṇena mahātmanā
dattaṃ dhanurvaraṃ prītyā tūṇī cākṣayasāyakau  Ram
asaṃcālyaṃ manuṣyaiś ca yatnenāpi ca gauravāt
tan na śaktā namayituṃ svapneṣv api narādhipāḥ  Ram
tad dhanuḥ prāpya me pitrā vyāhṛtaṃ satyavādinā
samavāye narendrāṇāṃ pūrvam āmantrya pārthivān  Ram
idaṃ ca dhanur udyamya sajyaṃ yaḥ kurute naraḥ
tasya me duhitā bhāryā bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ  Ram
tac ca dṛṣṭvā dhanuḥśreṣṭhaṃ gauravād girisaṃnibham
abhivādya nṛpā jagmur aśaktās tasya tolane  Ram
sudīrghasya tu kālasya rāghavo 'yaṃ mahādyutiḥ
viśvāmitreṇa sahito yajñaṃ draṣṭuṃ samāgataḥ  Ram
lakṣmaṇena saha bhrātrā rāmaḥ satyaparākramaḥ
viśvāmitras tu dharmātmā mama pitrā supūjitaḥ  Ram
provāca pitaraṃ tatra bhrātarau rāmalakṣmaṇau
sutau daśarathasyemau dhanurdarśanakāṅkṣiṇau
ity uktas tena vipreṇa tad dhanuḥ samupānayat  Ram
nimeṣāntaramātreṇa tad ānamya sa vīryavān
jyāṃ samāropya jhaṭiti pūrayāmāsa vīryavān  Ram
tena pūrayatā vegān madhye bhagnaṃ dvidhā dhanuḥ
tasya śabdo 'bhavad bhīmaḥ patitasyāśaner iva  Ram
tato 'haṃ tatra rāmāya pitrā satyābhisaṃdhinā
udyatā dātum udyamya jalabhājanam uttamam  Ram
dīyamānāṃ na tu tadā pratijagrāha rāghavaḥ
avijñāya pituś chandam ayodhyādhipateḥ prabhoḥ  Ram
tataḥ śvaśuram āmantrya vṛddhaṃ daśarathaṃ nṛpam
mama pitrā ahaṃ dattā rāmāya viditātmane  Ram
mama caivānujā sādhvī ūrmilā priyadarśanā
bhāryārthe lakṣmaṇasyāpi dattā pitrā mama svayam  Ram
evaṃ dattāsmi rāmāya tadā tasmin svayaṃvare
anuraktā ca dharmeṇa patiṃ vīryavatāṃ varam  Ram
anasūyā tu dharmajñā śrutvā tāṃ mahatīṃ kathām
paryaṣvajata bāhubhyāṃ śirasy āghrāya maithilīm  Ram
vyaktākṣarapadaṃ citraṃ bhāṣitaṃ madhuraṃ tvayā
yathā svayaṃvaraṃ vṛttaṃ tat sarvaṃ hi śrutaṃ mayā  Ram
rame 'haṃ kathayā te tu dṛḍhaṃ madhurabhāṣiṇi
ravir astaṃ gataḥ śrīmān upohya rajanīṃ śivām  Ram
divasaṃ pratikīrṇānām āhārārthaṃ patatriṇām
saṃdhyākāle nilīnānāṃ nidrārthaṃ śrūyate dhvaniḥ  Ram
ete cāpy abhiṣekārdrā munayaḥ phalaśodhanāḥ
sahitā upavartante salilāplutavalkalāḥ  Ram
ṛṣīṇām agnihotreṣu huteṣu vidhipurvakam
kapotāṅgāruṇo dhūmo dṛśyate pavanoddhataḥ  Ram
alpaparṇā hi taravo ghanībhūtāḥ samantataḥ
viprakṛṣṭe 'pi ye deśe na prakāśanti vai diśaḥ  Ram
rajanīcarasattvāni pracaranti samantataḥ
tapovanamṛgā hy ete veditīrtheṣu śerate  Ram
sampravṛttā niśā sīte nakṣatrasamalaṃkṛtā
jyotsnāprāvaraṇaś candro dṛśyate 'bhyudito 'mbare  Ram
gamyatām anujānāmi rāmasyānucarī bhava
kathayantyā hi madhuraṃ tvayāhaṃ paritoṣitā  Ram
alaṃkuru ca tāvat tvaṃ pratyakṣaṃ mama maithili
prītiṃ janaya me vatsa divyālaṃkāraśobhinī  Ram
sā tadā samalaṃkṛtya sītā surasutopamā
praṇamya śirasā tasyai rāmaṃ tv abhimukhī yayau  Ram
tathā tu bhūṣitāṃ sītāṃ dadarśa vadatāṃ varaḥ
rāghavaḥ prītidānena tapasvinyā jaharṣa ca  Ram
nyavedayat tataḥ sarvaṃ sītā rāmāya maithilī
prītidānaṃ tapasvinyā vasanābharaṇasrajām  Ram
prahṛṣṭas tv abhavad rāmo lakṣmaṇaś ca mahārathaḥ
maithilyāḥ satkriyāṃ dṛṣṭvā mānuṣeṣu sudurlabhām  Ram
tatas tāṃ śarvarīṃ prītaḥ puṇyāṃ śaśinibhānanaḥ
arcitas tāpasaiḥ siddhair uvāsa raghunandanaḥ  Ram
tasyāṃ rātryāṃ vyatītāyām abhiṣicya hutāgnikān
āpṛcchetāṃ naravyāghrau tāpasān vanagocarān  Ram
tāv ūcus te vanacarās tāpasā dharmacāriṇaḥ
vanasya tasya saṃcāraṃ rākṣasaiḥ samabhiplutam  Ram
eṣa panthā maharṣīṇāṃ phalāny āharatāṃ vane
anena tu vanaṃ durgaṃ gantuṃ rāghava te kṣamam  Ram
itīva taiḥ prāñjalibhis tapasvibhir dvijaiḥ kṛtasvastyayanaḥ paraṃtapaḥ
vanaṃ sabhāryaḥ praviveśa rāghavaḥ salakṣmaṇaḥ sūrya ivābhramaṇḍalam  Ram
praviśya tu mahāraṇyaṃ daṇḍakāraṇyam ātmavān
dadarśa rāmo durdharṣas tāpasāśramamaṇḍalam  Ram
kuśacīraparikṣiptaṃ brāhmyā lakṣmyā samāvṛtam
yathā pradīptaṃ durdharṣaṃ gagane sūryamaṇḍalam  Ram
śaraṇyaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ susaṃmṛṣṭājiraṃ sadā
pūjitaṃ copanṛttaṃ ca nityam apsarasāṃ gaṇaiḥ  Ram
viśālair agniśaraṇaiḥ srugbhāṇḍair ajinaiḥ kuśaiḥ
samidbhis toyakalaśaiḥ phalamūlaiś ca śobhitam  Ram
āraṇyaiś ca mahāvṛkṣaiḥ puṇyaiḥ svāduphalair vṛtam
balihomārcitaṃ puṇyaṃ brahmaghoṣanināditam  Ram
puṣpair vanyaiḥ parikṣiptaṃ padminyā ca sapadmayā
phalamūlāśanair dāntaiś cīrakṛṣṇājināmbaraiḥ  Ram
sūryavaiśvānarābhaiś ca purāṇair munibhir vṛtam
puṇyaiś ca niyatāhāraiḥ śobhitaṃ paramarṣibhiḥ  Ram
tad brahmabhavanaprakhyaṃ brahmaghoṣanināditam
brahmavidbhir mahābhāgair brāhmaṇair upaśobhitam  Ram
tad dṛṣṭvā rāghavaḥ śrīmāṃs tāpasāśramamaṇḍalam
abhyagacchan mahātejā vijyaṃ kṛtvā mahad dhanuḥ  Ram
divyajñānopapannās te rāmaṃ dṛṣṭvā maharṣayaḥ
abhyagacchaṃs tadā prītā vaidehīṃ ca yaśasvinīm  Ram
te taṃ somam ivodyantaṃ dṛṣṭvā vai dharmacāriṇaḥ
maṅgalāni prayuñjānāḥ pratyagṛhṇan dṛḍhavratāḥ  Ram
rūpasaṃhananaṃ lakṣmīṃ saukumāryaṃ suveṣatām
dadṛśur vismitākārā rāmasya vanavāsinaḥ  Ram
vaidehīṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ rāmaṃ netrair animiṣair iva
āścaryabhūtān dadṛśuḥ sarve te vanacāriṇaḥ  Ram
atrainaṃ hi mahābhāgāḥ sarvabhūtahite ratāḥ
atithiṃ parṇaśālāyāṃ rāghavaṃ saṃnyaveśayan  Ram
tato rāmasya satkṛtya vidhinā pāvakopamāḥ
ājahrus te mahābhāgāḥ salilaṃ dharmacāriṇaḥ  Ram
mūlaṃ puṣpaṃ phalaṃ vanyam āśramaṃ ca mahātmanaḥ
nivedayitvā dharmajñās tataḥ prāñjalayo 'bruvan  Ram
dharmapālo janasyāsya śaraṇyaś ca mahāyaśāḥ
pūjanīyaś ca mānyaś ca rājā daṇḍadharo guruḥ  Ram
indrasyeva caturbhāgaḥ prajā rakṣati rāghava
rājā tasmād varān bhogān bhuṅkte lokanamaskṛtaḥ  Ram
te vayaṃ bhavatā rakṣyā bhavadviṣayavāsinaḥ
nagarastho vanastho vā tvaṃ no rājā janeśvaraḥ  Ram
nyastadaṇḍā vayaṃ rājañ jitakrodhā jitendriyāḥ
rakṣitavyās tvayā śaśvad garbhabhūtās tapodhanāḥ  Ram
evam uktvā phalair mūlaiḥ puṣpair vanyaiś ca rāghavam
anyaiś ca vividhāhāraiḥ salakṣmaṇam apūjayan  Ram
tathānye tāpasāḥ siddhā rāmaṃ vaiśvānaropamāḥ
nyāyavṛttā yathānyāyaṃ tarpayāmāsur īśvaram  Ram
kṛtātithyo 'tha rāmas tu sūryasyodayanaṃ prati
āmantrya sa munīn sarvān vanam evānvagāhata  Ram
nānāmṛgagaṇākīrṇaṃ śārdūlavṛkasevitam
dhvastavṛkṣalatāgulmaṃ durdarśasalilāśayam  Ram
niṣkūjanānāśakuni jhillikāgaṇanāditam
lakṣmaṇānugato rāmo vanamadhyaṃ dadarśa ha  Ram
vanamadhye tu kākutsthas tasmin ghoramṛgāyute
dadarśa giriśṛṅgābhaṃ puruṣādaṃ mahāsvanam  Ram
gabhīrākṣaṃ mahāvaktraṃ vikaṭaṃ viṣamodaram
bībhatsaṃ viṣamaṃ dīrghaṃ vikṛtaṃ ghoradarśanam  Ram
vasānaṃ carma vaiyāghraṃ vasārdraṃ rudhirokṣitam
trāsanaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ vyāditāsyam ivāntakam  Ram
trīn siṃhāṃś caturo vyāghrān dvau vṛkau pṛṣatān daśa
saviṣāṇaṃ vasādigdhaṃ gajasya ca śiro mahat  Ram
avasajyāyase śūle vinadantaṃ mahāsvanam
sa rāmaṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ caiva sītāṃ dṛṣṭvā ca maithilīm  Ram
abhyadhāvat susaṃkruddhaḥ prajāḥ kāla ivāntakaḥ
sa kṛtvā bhairavaṃ nādaṃ cālayann iva medinīm  Ram
aṅgenādāya vaidehīm apakramya tato 'bravīt
yuvāṃ jaṭācīradharau sabhāryau kṣīṇajīvitau  Ram
praviṣṭau daṇḍakāraṇyaṃ śaracāpāsidhāriṇau
kathaṃ tāpasayor vāṃ ca vāsaḥ pramadayā saha  Ram
adharmacāriṇau pāpau kau yuvāṃ munidūṣakau
ahaṃ vanam idaṃ durgaṃ virādho nāma rākṣasaḥ  Ram
carāmi sāyudho nityam ṛṣimāṃsāni bhakṣayan
iyaṃ nārī varārohā mama bhāryā bhaviṣyati
yuvayoḥ pāpayoś cāhaṃ pāsyāmi rudhiraṃ mṛdhe  Ram
tasyaivaṃ bruvato dhṛṣṭaṃ virādhasya durātmanaḥ
śrutvā sagarvitaṃ vākyaṃ saṃbhrāntā janakātmajā
sītā prāvepatodvegāt pravāte kadalī yathā  Ram
tāṃ dṛṣṭvā rāghavaḥ sītāṃ virādhāṅkagatāṃ śubhām
abravīl lakṣmaṇaṃ vākyaṃ mukhena pariśuṣyatā  Ram
paśya saumya narendrasya janakasyātmasambhavām
mama bhāryāṃ śubhācārāṃ virādhāṅke praveśitām
atyantasukhasaṃvṛddhāṃ rājaputrīṃ yaśasvinīm  Ram
yad abhipretam asmāsu priyaṃ varavṛtaṃ ca yat
kaikeyyās tu susaṃvṛttaṃ kṣipram adyaiva lakṣmaṇa  Ram
yā na tuṣyati rājyena putrārthe dīrghadarśinī
yayāhaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ hitaḥ prasthāpito vanam
adyedānīṃ sakāmā sā yā mātā mama madhyamā  Ram
parasparśāt tu vaidehyā na duḥkhataram asti me
pitur vināśāt saumitre svarājyaharaṇāt tathā  Ram
iti bruvati kākutsthe bāṣpaśokapariplute
abravīl lakṣmaṇaḥ kruddho ruddho nāga iva śvasan  Ram
anātha iva bhūtānāṃ nāthas tvaṃ vāsavopamaḥ
mayā preṣyeṇa kākutstha kimarthaṃ paritapyase  Ram
śareṇa nihatasyādya mayā kruddhena rakṣasaḥ
virādhasya gatāsor hi mahī pāsyati śoṇitam  Ram
rājyakāme mama krodho bharate yo babhūva ha
taṃ virādhe vimokṣyāmi vajrī vajram ivācale  Ram
mama bhujabalavegavegitaḥ patatu śaro 'sya mahān mahorasi
vyapanayatu tanoś ca jīvitaṃ patatu tataś ca mahīṃ vighūrṇitaḥ  Ram
athovāca punar vākyaṃ virādhaḥ pūrayan vanam
ātmānaṃ pṛcchate brūtaṃ kau yuvāṃ kva gamiṣyathaḥ  Ram
tam uvāca tato rāmo rākṣasaṃ jvalitānanam
pṛcchantaṃ sumahātejā ikṣvākukulam ātmanaḥ  Ram
kṣatriyau vṛttasampannau viddhi nau vanagocarau
tvāṃ tu veditum icchāvaḥ kas tvaṃ carasi daṇḍakān  Ram
tam uvāca virādhas tu rāmaṃ satyaparākramam
hanta vakṣyāmi te rājan nibodha mama rāghava  Ram
putraḥ kila jayasyāhaṃ mātā mama śatahradā
virādha iti mām āhuḥ pṛthivyāṃ sarvarākṣasāḥ  Ram
tapasā cāpi me prāptā brahmaṇo hi prasādajā
śastreṇāvadhyatā loke 'cchedyābhedyatvam eva ca  Ram
utsṛjya pramadām enām anapekṣau yathāgatam
tvaramāṇau pālayethāṃ na vāṃ jīvitam ādade  Ram
taṃ rāmaḥ pratyuvācedaṃ kopasaṃraktalocanaḥ
rākṣasaṃ vikṛtākāraṃ virādhaṃ pāpacetasam  Ram
kṣudra dhik tvāṃ tu hīnārthaṃ mṛtyum anveṣase dhruvam
raṇe samprāpsyase tiṣṭha na me jīvan gamiṣyasi  Ram
tataḥ sajyaṃ dhanuḥ kṛtvā rāmaḥ suniśitāñ śarān
suśīghram abhisaṃdhāya rākṣasaṃ nijaghāna ha  Ram
dhanuṣā jyāguṇavatā saptabāṇān mumoca ha
rukmapuṅkhān mahāvegān suparṇānilatulyagān  Ram
te śarīraṃ virādhasya bhittvā barhiṇavāsasaḥ
nipetuḥ śoṇitādigdhā dharaṇyāṃ pāvakopamāḥ  Ram
sa vinadya mahānādaṃ śūlaṃ śakradhvajopamam
pragṛhyāśobhata tadā vyāttānana ivāntakaḥ  Ram
tac chūlaṃ vajrasaṃkāśaṃ gagane jvalanopamam
dvābhyāṃ śarābhyāṃ cicheda rāmaḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ  Ram
tasya raudrasya saumitrir bāhuṃ savyaṃ babhañja ha
rāmas tu dakṣiṇaṃ bāhuṃ tarasā tasya rakṣasaḥ  Ram
sa bhagnabāhuḥ saṃvigno nipapātāśu rākṣasaḥ
dharaṇyāṃ meghasaṃkāśo vajrabhinna ivācalaḥ
idaṃ provāca kākutsthaṃ virādhaḥ puruṣarṣabham  Ram
kausalyā suprajās tāta rāmas tvaṃ vidito mayā
vaidehī ca mahābhāgā lakṣmaṇaś ca mahāyaśāḥ  Ram
abhiśāpād ahaṃ ghorāṃ praviṣṭo rākṣasīṃ tanum
tumburur nāma gandharvaḥ śapto vaiśravaṇena hi  Ram
prasādyamānaś ca mayā so 'bravīn māṃ mahāyaśāḥ
yadā dāśarathī rāmas tvāṃ vadhiṣyati saṃyuge  Ram
tadā prakṛtim āpanno bhavān svargaṃ gamiṣyati
iti vaiśravaṇo rājā rambhāsaktam uvāca ha  Ram
anupasthīyamāno māṃ saṃkruddho vyājahāra ha
tava prasādān mukto 'ham abhiśāpāt sudāruṇāt
bhavanaṃ svaṃ gamiṣyāmi svasti vo 'stu paraṃtapa  Ram
ito vasati dharmātmā śarabhaṅgaḥ pratāpavān
adhyardhayojane tāta maharṣiḥ sūryasaṃnibhaḥ  Ram
taṃ kṣipram abhigaccha tvaṃ sa te śreyo vidhāsyati
avaṭe cāpi māṃ rāma nikṣipya kuśalī vraja  Ram
rakṣasāṃ gatasattvānām eṣa dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ
avaṭe ye nidhīyante teṣāṃ lokāḥ sanātanāḥ  Ram
evam uktvā tu kākutsthaṃ virādhaḥ śarapīḍitaḥ
babhūva svargasamprāpto nyastadeho mahābalaḥ  Ram
taṃ muktakaṇṭham utkṣipya śaṅkukarṇaṃ mahāsvanam
virādhaṃ prākṣipac chvabhre nadantaṃ bhairavasvanam  Ram
tatas tu tau kāñcanacitrakārmukau nihatya rakṣaḥ parigṛhya maithilīm
vijahratus tau muditau mahāvane divi sthitau candradivākarāv iva  Ram
hatvā tu taṃ bhīmabalaṃ virādhaṃ rākṣasaṃ vane
tataḥ sītāṃ pariṣvajya samāśvāsya ca vīryavān
abravīl lakṣmaṇaṃ rāmo bhrātaraṃ dīptatejasam  Ram
kaṣṭaṃ vanam idaṃ durgaṃ na ca smo vanagocarāḥ
abhigacchāmahe śīghraṃ śarabhaṅgaṃ tapodhanam  Ram
āśramaṃ śarabhaṅgasya rāghavo 'bhijagāma ha  Ram
tasya devaprabhāvasya tapasā bhāvitātmanaḥ
samīpe śarabhaṅgasya dadarśa mahad adbhutam  Ram
vibhrājamānaṃ vapuṣā sūryavaiśvānaropamam
asaṃspṛśantaṃ vasudhāṃ dadarśa vibudheśvaram  Ram
suprabhābharaṇaṃ devaṃ virajo'mbaradhāriṇam
tadvidhair eva bahubhiḥ pūjyamānaṃ mahātmabhiḥ  Ram
haribhir vājibhir yuktam antarikṣagataṃ ratham
