dadarśādūratas tasya taruṇādityasaṃnibham  Ram
pāṇḍurābhraghanaprakhyaṃ candramaṇḍalasaṃnibham
apaśyad vimalaṃ chattraṃ citramālyopaśobhitam  Ram
cāmaravyajane cāgrye rukmadaṇḍe mahādhane
gṛhīte vananārībhyāṃ dhūyamāne ca mūrdhani  Ram
gandharvāmarasiddhāś ca bahavaḥ paramarṣayaḥ
antarikṣagataṃ devaṃ vāgbhir agryābhir īḍire  Ram
dṛṣṭvā śatakratuṃ tatra rāmo lakṣmaṇam abravīt
ye hayāḥ puruhūtasya purā śakrasya naḥ śrutāḥ
antarikṣagatā divyās ta ime harayo dhruvam  Ram
ime ca puruṣavyāghra ye tiṣṭhanty abhito ratham
śataṃ śataṃ kuṇḍalino yuvānaḥ khaḍgapāṇayaḥ  Ram
urodeśeṣu sarveṣāṃ hārā jvalanasaṃnibhāḥ
rūpaṃ bibhrati saumitre pañcaviṃśativārṣikam  Ram
etaddhi kila devānāṃ vayo bhavati nityadā
yatheme puruṣavyāghrā dṛśyante priyadarśanāḥ  Ram
ihaiva saha vaidehyā muhūrtaṃ tiṣṭha lakṣmaṇa
yāvaj janāmy ahaṃ vyaktaṃ ka eṣa dyutimān rathe  Ram
tam evam uktvā saumitrim ihaiva sthīyatām iti
abhicakrāma kākutsthaḥ śarabhaṅgāśramaṃ prati  Ram
tataḥ samabhigacchantaṃ prekṣya rāmaṃ śacīpatiḥ
śarabhaṅgam anujñāpya vibudhān idam abravīt  Ram
ihopayāty asau rāmo yāvan māṃ nābhibhāṣate
niṣṭhāṃ nayata tāvat tu tato māṃ draṣṭum arhati  Ram
jitavantaṃ kṛtārthaṃ ca draṣṭāham acirād imam
karma hy anena kartavyaṃ mahad anyaiḥ suduṣkaram  Ram
iti vajrī tam āmantrya mānayitvā ca tāpasam
rathena hariyuktena yayau divam ariṃdamaḥ  Ram
prayāte tu sahasrākṣe rāghavaḥ saparicchadaḥ
agnihotram upāsīnaṃ śarabhaṅgam upāgamat  Ram
tasya pādau ca saṃgṛhya rāmaḥ sītā ca lakṣmaṇaḥ
niṣedus tadanujñātā labdhavāsā nimantritāḥ  Ram
tataḥ śakropayānaṃ tu paryapṛcchat sa rāghavaḥ
śarabhaṅgaś ca tat sarvaṃ rāghavāya nyavedayat  Ram
mām eṣa varado rāma brahmalokaṃ ninīṣati
jitam ugreṇa tapasā duṣprāpam akṛtātmabhiḥ  Ram
ahaṃ jñātvā naravyāghra vartamānam adūrataḥ
brahmalokaṃ na gacchāmi tvām adṛṣṭvā priyātithim  Ram
samāgamya gamiṣyāmi tridivaṃ devasevitam
akṣayā naraśārdūla jitā lokā mayā śubhāḥ
brāhmyāś ca nākapṛṣṭhyāś ca pratigṛhṇīṣva māmakān  Ram
evam ukto naravyāghraḥ sarvaśāstraviśāradaḥ
ṛṣiṇā śarabhaṅgena rāghavo vākyam abravīt  Ram
aham evāhariṣyāmi sarvāṃl lokān mahāmune
āvāsaṃ tv aham icchāmi pradiṣṭam iha kānane  Ram
rāghaveṇaivam uktas tu śakratulyabalena vai
śarabhaṅgo mahāprājñaḥ punar evābravīd vacaḥ  Ram
sutīkṣṇam abhigaccha tvaṃ śucau deśe tapasvinam
ramaṇīye vanoddeśe sa te vāsaṃ vidhāsyati  Ram
eṣa panthā naravyāghra muhūrtaṃ paśya tāta mām
yāvaj jahāmi gātrāṇi jīrṇāṃ tvacam ivoragaḥ  Ram
tato 'gniṃ sa samādhāya hutvā cājyena mantravit
śarabhaṅgo mahātejāḥ praviveśa hutāśanam  Ram
tasya romāṇi keśāṃś ca dadāhāgnir mahātmanaḥ
jīrṇāṃ tvacaṃ tathāsthīni yac ca māṃsaṃ ca śoṇitam  Ram
sa ca pāvakasaṃkāśaḥ kumāraḥ samapadyata
utthāyāgnicayāt tasmāc charabhaṅgo vyarocata  Ram
sa lokān āhitāgnīnām ṛṣīṇāṃ ca mahātmanām
devānāṃ ca vyatikramya brahmalokaṃ vyarohata  Ram
sa puṇyakarmā bhuvane dvijarṣabhaḥ pitāmahaṃ sānucaraṃ dadarśa ha
pitāmahaś cāpi samīkṣya taṃ dvijaṃ nananda susvāgatam ity uvāca ha  Ram
śarabhaṅge divaṃ prāpte munisaṃghāḥ samāgatāḥ
abhyagacchanta kākutsthaṃ rāmaṃ jvalitatejasam  Ram
vaikhānasā vālakhilyāḥ samprakṣālā marīcipāḥ
aśmakuṭṭāś ca bahavaḥ pattrāhārāś ca tāpasāḥ  Ram
dantolūkhalinaś caiva tathaivonmajjakāḥ pare
munayaḥ salilāhārā vāyubhakṣās tathāpare  Ram
ākāśanilayāś caiva tathā sthaṇḍilaśāyinaḥ
tathordhvavāsino dāntās tathārdrapaṭavāsasaḥ  Ram
sajapāś ca taponityās tathā pañcatapo'nvitāḥ
sarve brāhmyā śriyā juṣṭā dṛḍhayogasamāhitāḥ
śarabhaṅgāśrame rāmam abhijagmuś ca tāpasāḥ  Ram
abhigamya ca dharmajñā rāmaṃ dharmabhṛtāṃ varam
ūcuḥ paramadharmajñam ṛṣisaṃghāḥ samāhitāḥ  Ram
tvam ikṣvākukulasyāsya pṛthivyāś ca mahārathaḥ
pradhānaś cāsi nāthaś ca devānāṃ maghavān iva  Ram
viśrutas triṣu lokeṣu yaśasā vikrameṇa ca
pitṛvratatvaṃ satyaṃ ca tvayi dharmaś ca puṣkalaḥ  Ram
tvām āsādya mahātmānaṃ dharmajñaṃ dharmavatsalam
arthitvān nātha vakṣyāmas tac ca naḥ kṣantum arhasi  Ram
adharmas tu mahāṃs tāta bhavet tasya mahīpateḥ
yo hared baliṣaḍbhāgaṃ na ca rakṣati putravat  Ram
yuñjānaḥ svān iva prāṇān prāṇair iṣṭān sutān iva
nityayuktaḥ sadā rakṣan sarvān viṣayavāsinaḥ  Ram
prāpnoti śāśvatīṃ rāma kīrtiṃ sa bahuvārṣikīm
brahmaṇaḥ sthānam āsādya tatra cāpi mahīyate  Ram
yat karoti paraṃ dharmaṃ munir mūlaphalāśanaḥ
tatra rājñaś caturbhāgaḥ prajā dharmeṇa rakṣataḥ  Ram
so 'yaṃ brāhmaṇabhūyiṣṭho vānaprasthagaṇo mahān
tvan nātho 'nāthavad rāma rākṣasair vadhyate bhṛśam  Ram
ehi paśya śarīrāṇi munīnāṃ bhāvitātmanām
hatānāṃ rākṣasair ghorair bahūnāṃ bahudhā vane  Ram
pampānadīnivāsānām anumandākinīm api
citrakūṭālayānāṃ ca kriyate kadanaṃ mahat  Ram
evaṃ vayaṃ na mṛṣyāmo viprakāraṃ tapasvinām
kriyamāṇaṃ vane ghoraṃ rakṣobhir bhīmakarmabhiḥ  Ram
tatas tvāṃ śaraṇārthaṃ ca śaraṇyaṃ samupasthitāḥ
paripālaya no rāma vadhyamānān niśācaraiḥ  Ram
etac chrutvā tu kākutsthas tāpasānāṃ tapasvinām
idaṃ provāca dharmātmā sarvān eva tapasvinaḥ
naivam arhatha māṃ vaktum ājñāpyo 'haṃ tapasvinām  Ram
bhavatām arthasiddhyartham āgato 'haṃ yadṛcchayā
tasya me 'yaṃ vane vāso bhaviṣyati mahāphalaḥ
tapasvināṃ raṇe śatrūn hantum icchāmi rākṣasān  Ram
dattvā varaṃ cāpi tapodhanānāṃ dharme dhṛtātmā saha lakṣmaṇena
tapodhanaiś cāpi sabhājyavṛttaḥ sutīkṣṇam evābhijagāma vīraḥ  Ram
rāmas tu sahito bhrātrā sītayā ca paraṃtapaḥ
sutīkṣṇasyāśramapadaṃ jagāma saha tair dvijaiḥ  Ram
sa gatvā dūram adhvānaṃ nadīs tīrtvā bahūdakāḥ
dadarśa vipulaṃ śailaṃ mahāmegham ivonnatam  Ram
tatas tad ikṣvākuvarau satataṃ vividhair drumaiḥ
kānanaṃ tau viviśatuḥ sītayā saha rāghavau  Ram
praviṣṭas tu vanaṃ ghoraṃ bahupuṣpaphaladrumam
dadarśāśramam ekānte cīramālāpariṣkṛtam  Ram
tatra tāpasam āsīnaṃ malapaṅkajaṭādharam
rāmaḥ sutīkṣṇaṃ vidhivat tapovṛddham abhāṣata  Ram
rāmo 'ham asmi bhagavan bhavantaṃ draṣṭum āgataḥ
tan mābhivada dharmajña maharṣe satyavikrama  Ram
sa nirīkṣya tato vīraṃ rāmaṃ dharmabhṛtāṃ varam
samāśliṣya ca bāhubhyām idaṃ vacanam abravīt  Ram
svāgataṃ khalu te vīra rāma dharmabhṛtāṃ vara
āśramo 'yaṃ tvayākrāntaḥ sanātha iva sāmpratam  Ram
pratīkṣamāṇas tvām eva nārohe 'haṃ mahāyaśaḥ
devalokam ito vīra dehaṃ tyaktvā mahītale  Ram
citrakūṭam upādāya rājyabhraṣṭo 'si me śrutaḥ
ihopayātaḥ kākutstho devarājaḥ śatakratuḥ
sarvāṃl lokāñ jitān āha mama puṇyena karmaṇā  Ram
teṣu devarṣijuṣṭeṣu jiteṣu tapasā mayā
matprasādāt sabhāryas tvaṃ viharasva salakṣmaṇaḥ  Ram
tam ugratapasaṃ dīptaṃ maharṣiṃ satyavādinam
pratyuvācātmavān rāmo brahmāṇam iva vāsavaḥ  Ram
aham evāhariṣyāmi svayaṃ lokān mahāmune
āvāsaṃ tv aham icchāmi pradiṣṭam iha kānane  Ram
bhavān sarvatra kuśalaḥ sarvabhūtahite rataḥ
ākhyātaḥ śarabhaṅgena gautamena mahātmanā  Ram
evam uktas tu rāmeṇa maharṣir lokaviśrutaḥ
abravīn madhuraṃ vākyaṃ harṣeṇa mahatāplutaḥ  Ram
ayam evāśramo rāma guṇavān ramyatām iha
ṛṣisaṃghānucaritaḥ sadā mūlaphalair yutaḥ  Ram
imam āśramam āgamya mṛgasaṃghā mahāyaśaḥ
aṭitvā pratigacchanti lobhayitvākutobhayāḥ  Ram
tac chrutvā vacanaṃ tasya maharṣer lakṣmaṇāgrajaḥ
uvāca vacanaṃ dhīro vikṛṣya saśaraṃ dhanuḥ  Ram
tān ahaṃ sumahābhāga mṛgasaṃghān samāgatān
hanyāṃ niśitadhāreṇa śareṇāśanivarcasā  Ram
bhavāṃs tatrābhiṣajyeta kiṃ syāt kṛcchrataraṃ tataḥ
etasminn āśrame vāsaṃ ciraṃ tu na samarthaye  Ram
tam evam uktvā varadaṃ rāmaḥ saṃdhyām upāgamat
anvāsya paścimāṃ saṃdhyāṃ tatra vāsam akalpayat  Ram
tataḥ śubhaṃ tāpasabhojyam annaṃ svayaṃ sutīkṣṇaḥ puruṣarṣabhābhyām
tābhyāṃ susatkṛtya dadau mahātmā saṃdhyānivṛttau rajanīṃ samīkṣya  Ram
rāmas tu sahasaumitriḥ sutīkṣṇenābhipūjitaḥ
pariṇāmya niśāṃ tatra prabhāte pratyabudhyata  Ram
utthāya tu yathākālaṃ rāghavaḥ saha sītayā
upāspṛśat suśītena jalenotpalagandhinā  Ram
atha te 'gniṃ surāṃś caiva vaidehī rāmalakṣmaṇau
kālyaṃ vidhivad abhyarcya tapasviśaraṇe vane  Ram
udayantaṃ dinakaraṃ dṛṣṭvā vigatakalmaṣāḥ
sutīkṣṇam abhigamyedaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ vacanam abruvan  Ram
sukhoṣitāḥ sma bhagavaṃs tvayā pūjyena pūjitāḥ
āpṛcchāmaḥ prayāsyāmo munayas tvarayanti naḥ  Ram
tvarāmahe vayaṃ draṣṭuṃ kṛtsnam āśramamaṇḍalam
ṛṣīṇāṃ puṇyaśīlānāṃ daṇḍakāraṇyavāsinām  Ram
abhyanujñātum icchāmaḥ sahaibhir munipuṃgavaiḥ
dharmanityais tapodāntair viśikhair iva pāvakaiḥ  Ram
aviṣahyātapo yāvat sūryo nātivirājate
amārgeṇāgatāṃ lakṣmīṃ prāpyevānvayavarjitaḥ  Ram
tāvad icchāmahe gantum ity uktvā caraṇau muneḥ
vavande sahasaumitriḥ sītayā saha rāghavaḥ  Ram
tau saṃspṛśantau caraṇāv utthāpya munipuṃgavaḥ
gāḍham āliṅgya sasneham idaṃ vacanam abravīt  Ram
ariṣṭaṃ gaccha panthānaṃ rāma saumitriṇā saha
sītayā cānayā sārdhaṃ chāyayevānuvṛttayā  Ram
paśyāśramapadaṃ ramyaṃ daṇḍakāraṇyavāsinām
eṣāṃ tapasvināṃ vīra tapasā bhāvitātmanām  Ram
suprājyaphalamūlāni puṣpitāni vanāni ca
praśāntamṛgayūthāni śāntapakṣigaṇāni ca  Ram
phullapaṅkajaṣaṇḍāni prasannasalilāni ca
kāraṇḍavavikīrṇāni taṭākāni sarāṃsi ca  Ram
drakṣyase dṛṣṭiramyāṇi giriprasravaṇāni ca
ramaṇīyāny araṇyāni mayūrābhirutāni ca  Ram
gamyatāṃ vatsa saumitre bhavān api ca gacchatu
āgantavyaṃ ca te dṛṣṭvā punar evāśramaṃ mama  Ram
evam uktas tathety uktvā kākutsthaḥ sahalakṣmaṇaḥ
pradakṣiṇaṃ muniṃ kṛtvā prasthātum upacakrame  Ram
tataḥ śubhatare tūṇī dhanuṣī cāyatekṣaṇā
dadau sītā tayor bhrātroḥ khaḍgau ca vimalau tataḥ  Ram
ābadhya ca śubhe tūṇī cāpau cādāya sasvanau
niṣkrāntāv āśramād gantum ubhau tau rāmalakṣmaṇau  Ram
sutīkṣṇenābhyanujñātaṃ prasthitaṃ raghunandanam
vaidehī snigdhayā vācā bhartāram idam abravīt  Ram
ayaṃ dharmaḥ susūkṣmeṇa vidhinā prāpyate mahān
nivṛttena ca śakyo 'yaṃ vyasanāt kāmajād iha  Ram
trīṇy eva vyasanāny atra kāmajāni bhavanty uta
mithyāvākyaṃ paramakaṃ tasmād gurutarāv ubhau
paradārābhigamanaṃ vinā vairaṃ ca raudratā  Ram
mithyāvākyaṃ na te bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati rāghava
kuto 'bhilaṣaṇaṃ strīṇāṃ pareṣāṃ dharmanāśanam  Ram
tac ca sarvaṃ mahābāho śakyaṃ voḍhuṃ jitendriyaiḥ
tava vaśyendriyatvaṃ ca jānāmi śubhadarśana  Ram
tṛtīyaṃ yad idaṃ raudraṃ paraprāṇābhihiṃsanam
nirvairaṃ kriyate mohāt tac ca te samupasthitam  Ram
pratijñātas tvayā vīra daṇḍakāraṇyavāsinām
ṛṣīṇāṃ rakṣaṇārthāya vadhaḥ saṃyati rakṣasām  Ram
etannimittaṃ ca vanaṃ daṇḍakā iti viśrutam
prasthitas tvaṃ saha bhrātrā dhṛtabāṇaśarāsanaḥ  Ram
tatas tvāṃ prasthitaṃ dṛṣṭvā mama cintākulaṃ manaḥ
tvadvṛttaṃ cintayantyā vai bhaven niḥśreyasaṃ hitam  Ram
na hi me rocate vīra gamanaṃ daṇḍakān prati
kāraṇaṃ tatra vakṣyāmi vadantyāḥ śrūyatāṃ mama  Ram
tvaṃ hi bāṇadhanuṣpāṇir bhrātrā saha vanaṃ gataḥ
dṛṣṭvā vanacarān sarvān kaccit kuryāḥ śaravyayam  Ram
kṣatriyāṇām iha dhanur hutāśasyendhanāni ca
samīpataḥ sthitaṃ tejobalam ucchrayate bhṛśam  Ram
purā kila mahābāho tapasvī satyavāk śuciḥ
kasmiṃścid abhavat puṇye vane ratamṛgadvije  Ram
tasyaiva tapaso vighnaṃ kartum indraḥ śacīpatiḥ
khaḍgapāṇir athāgacchad āśramaṃ bhaṭarūpadhṛk  Ram
tasmiṃs tadāśramapade nihitaḥ khaḍga uttamaḥ
sa nyāsavidhinā dattaḥ puṇye tapasi tiṣṭhataḥ  Ram
sa tac chastram anuprāpya nyāsarakṣaṇatatparaḥ
vane tu vicaraty eva rakṣan pratyayam ātmanaḥ  Ram
yatra gacchaty upādātuṃ mūlāni ca phalāni ca
na vinā yāti taṃ khaḍgaṃ nyāsarakṣaṇatatparaḥ  Ram
nityaṃ śastraṃ parivahan krameṇa sa tapodhanaḥ
cakāra raudrīṃ svāṃ buddhiṃ tyaktvā tapasi niścayam  Ram
tataḥ sa raudrābhirataḥ pramatto 'dharmakarṣitaḥ
tasya śastrasya saṃvāsāj jagāma narakaṃ muniḥ  Ram
snehāc ca bahumānāc ca smāraye tvāṃ na śikṣaye
na kathaṃcana sā kāryā gṛhītadhanuṣā tvayā  Ram
buddhir vairaṃ vinā hantuṃ rākṣasān daṇḍakāśritān
aparādhaṃ vinā hantuṃ lokān vīra na kāmaye  Ram
kṣatriyāṇāṃ tu vīrāṇāṃ vaneṣu niyatātmanām
dhanuṣā kāryam etāvad ārtānām abhirakṣaṇam  Ram
kva ca śastraṃ kva ca vanaṃ kva ca kṣātraṃ tapaḥ kva ca
vyāviddham idam asmābhir deśadharmas tu pūjyatām  Ram
tadārya kaluṣā buddhir jāyate śastrasevanāt
punar gatvā tv ayodhyāyāṃ kṣatradharmaṃ cariṣyasi  Ram
akṣayā tu bhavet prītiḥ śvaśrūśvaśurayor mama
yadi rājyaṃ hi saṃnyasya bhaves tvaṃ nirato muniḥ  Ram
dharmād arthaḥ prabhavati dharmāt prabhavate sukham
dharmeṇa labhate sarvaṃ dharmasāram idaṃ jagat  Ram
ātmānaṃ niyamais tais taiḥ karṣayitvā prayatnataḥ
prāpyate nipuṇair dharmo na sukhāl labhyate sukham  Ram
nityaṃ śucimatiḥ saumya cara dharmaṃ tapovane
sarvaṃ hi viditaṃ tubhyaṃ trailokyam api tattvataḥ  Ram
strīcāpalād etad udāhṛtaṃ me dharmaṃ ca vaktuṃ tava kaḥ samarthaḥ
vicārya buddhyā tu sahānujena yad rocate tat kuru mācireṇa  Ram
vākyam etat tu vaidehyā vyāhṛtaṃ bhartṛbhaktayā
śrutvā dharme sthito rāmaḥ pratyuvācātha maithilīm  Ram
hitam uktaṃ tvayā devi snigdhayā sadṛśaṃ vacaḥ
kulaṃ vyapadiśantyā ca dharmajñe janakātmaje  Ram
kiṃ tu vakṣyāmy ahaṃ devi tvayaivoktam idaṃ vacaḥ
kṣatriyair dhāryate cāpo nārtaśabdo bhaved iti  Ram
te cārtā daṇḍakāraṇye munayaḥ saṃśitavratāḥ
māṃ sīte svayam āgamya śaraṇyāḥ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ  Ram
vasanto dharmaniratā vane mūlaphalāśanāḥ
na labhante sukhaṃ bhītā rākṣasaiḥ krūrakarmabhiḥ  Ram
kāle kāle ca niratā niyamair vividhair vane
bhakṣyante rākṣasair bhīmair naramāṃsopajīvibhiḥ  Ram
te bhakṣyamāṇā munayo daṇḍakāraṇyavāsinaḥ
asmān abhyavapadyeti mām ūcur dvijasattamāḥ  Ram
mayā tu vacanaṃ śrutvā teṣām evaṃ mukhāc cyutam
kṛtvā caraṇaśuśrūṣāṃ vākyam etad udāhṛtam  Ram
prasīdantu bhavanto me hrīr eṣā hi mamātulā
yadīdṛśair ahaṃ viprair upastheyair upasthitaḥ
kiṃ karomīti ca mayā vyāhṛtaṃ dvijasaṃnidhau  Ram
sarvair eva samāgamya vāg iyaṃ samudāhṛtā
rākṣasair daṇḍakāraṇye bahubhiḥ kāmarūpibhiḥ
arditāḥ sma bhṛśaṃ rāma bhavān nas trātum arhati  Ram
homakāle tu samprāpte parvakāleṣu cānagha
dharṣayanti sma durdharṣā rākṣasāḥ piśitāśanāḥ  Ram
rākṣasair dharṣitānāṃ ca tāpasānāṃ tapasvinām
gatiṃ mṛgayamāṇānāṃ bhavān naḥ paramā gatiḥ  Ram
kāmaṃ tapaḥprabhāvena śaktā hantuṃ niśācarān
cirārjitaṃ tu necchāmas tapaḥ khaṇḍayituṃ vayam  Ram
bahuvighnaṃ taponityaṃ duścaraṃ caiva rāghava
tena śāpaṃ na muñcāmo bhakṣyamāṇāś ca rākṣasaiḥ  Ram
tad ardyamānān rakṣobhir daṇḍakāraṇyavāsibhiḥ
rakṣa nas tvaṃ saha bhrātrā tvannāthā hi vayaṃ vane  Ram
mayā caitad vacaḥ śrutvā kārtsnyena paripālanam
ṛṣīṇāṃ daṇḍakāraṇye saṃśrutaṃ janakātmaje  Ram
saṃśrutya ca na śakṣyāmi jīvamānaḥ pratiśravam
munīnām anyathā kartuṃ satyam iṣṭaṃ hi me sadā  Ram
apy ahaṃ jīvitaṃ jahyāṃ tvāṃ vā sīte salakṣmaṇām
na tu pratijñāṃ saṃśrutya brāhmaṇebhyo viśeṣataḥ  Ram
tad avaśyaṃ mayā kāryam ṛṣīṇāṃ paripālanam
anuktenāpi vaidehi pratijñāya tu kiṃ punaḥ  Ram
mama snehāc ca sauhārdād idam uktaṃ tvayā vacaḥ
parituṣṭo 'smy ahaṃ sīte na hy aniṣṭo 'nuśiṣyate
sadṛśaṃ cānurūpaṃ ca kulasya tava śobhane  Ram
ity evam uktvā vacanaṃ mahātmā sītāṃ priyāṃ maithilarājaputrīm
rāmo dhanuṣmān saha lakṣmaṇena jagāma ramyāṇi tapovanāni  Ram
agrataḥ prayayau rāmaḥ sītā madhye sumadhyamā
pṛṣṭhatas tu dhanuṣpāṇir lakṣmaṇo 'nujagāma ha  Ram
tau paśyamānau vividhāñ śailaprasthān vanāni ca
nadīś ca vividhā ramyā jagmatuḥ saha sītayā  Ram
sārasāṃś cakravākāṃś ca nadīpulinacāriṇaḥ
sarāṃsi ca sapadmāni yutāni jalajaiḥ khagaiḥ  Ram
yūthabaddhāṃś ca pṛṣatān madonmattān viṣāṇinaḥ
mahiṣāṃś ca varāhāṃś ca gajāṃś ca drumavairiṇaḥ  Ram
te gatvā dūram adhvānaṃ lambamāne divākare
dadṛśuḥ sahitā ramyaṃ taṭākaṃ yojanāyatam  Ram
padmapuṣkarasambādhaṃ gajayūthair alaṃkṛtam
sārasair haṃsakādambaiḥ saṃkulaṃ jalacāribhiḥ  Ram
prasannasalile ramye tasmin sarasi śuśruve
gītavāditranirghoṣo na tu kaścana dṛśyate  Ram
tataḥ kautūhalād rāmo lakṣmaṇaś ca mahārathaḥ
muniṃ dharmabhṛtaṃ nāma praṣṭuṃ samupacakrame  Ram
idam atyadbhutaṃ śrutvā sarveṣāṃ no mahāmune
kautūhalaṃ mahaj jātaṃ kim idaṃ sādhu kathyatām  Ram
tenaivam ukto dharmātmā rāghaveṇa munis tadā
prabhāvaṃ sarasaḥ kṛtsnam ākhyātum upacakrame  Ram
idaṃ pañcāpsaro nāma taṭākaṃ sārvakālikam
nirmitaṃ tapasā rāma muninā māṇḍakarṇinā  Ram
sa hi tepe tapas tīvraṃ māṇḍakarṇir mahāmuniḥ
daśavarṣasahasrāṇi vāyubhakṣo jalāśrayaḥ  Ram
tataḥ pravyathitāḥ sarve devāḥ sāgnipurogamāḥ
abruvan vacanaṃ sarve parasparasamāgatāḥ
asmākaṃ kasyacit sthānam eṣa prārthayate muniḥ  Ram
tataḥ kartuṃ tapovighnaṃ sarvair devair niyojitāḥ
pradhānāpsarasaḥ pañcavidyuccalitavarcasaḥ  Ram
apsarobhis tatas tābhir munir dṛṣṭaparāvaraḥ
nīto madanavaśyatvaṃ surāṇāṃ kāryasiddhaye  Ram
tāś caivāpsarasaḥ pañca muneḥ patnītvam āgatāḥ
taṭāke nirmitaṃ tāsām asminn antarhitaṃ gṛham  Ram
tatraivāpsarasaḥ pañca nivasantyo yathāsukham
ramayanti tapoyogān muniṃ yauvanam āsthitam  Ram
tāsāṃ saṃkrīḍamānānām eṣa vāditraniḥsvanaḥ
śrūyate bhūṣaṇonmiśro gītaśabdo manoharaḥ  Ram
āścaryam iti tasyaitad vacanaṃ bhāvitātmanaḥ
rāghavaḥ pratijagrāha saha bhrātrā mahāyaśāḥ  Ram
evaṃ kathayamānasya dadarśāśramamaṇḍalam
kuśacīraparikṣiptaṃ nānāvṛkṣasamāvṛtam  Ram
praviśya saha vaidehyā lakṣmaṇena ca rāghavaḥ
tadā tasmin sa kākutsthaḥ śrīmaty āśramamaṇḍale  Ram
uṣitvā susukhaṃ tatra pūjyamāno maharṣibhiḥ
jagāma cāśramāṃs teṣāṃ paryāyeṇa tapasvinām  Ram
yeṣām uṣitavān pūrvaṃ sakāśe sa mahāstravit
kvacit paridaśān māsān ekaṃ saṃvatsaraṃ kvacit  Ram
kvacic ca caturo māsān pañcaṣaṭ cāparān kvacit
aparatrādhikān māsān adhyardham adhikaṃ kvacit  Ram
trīn māsān aṣṭamāsāṃś ca rāghavo nyavasat sukham
tathā saṃvasatas tasya munīnām āśrameṣu vai
ramataś cānukūlyena yayuḥ saṃvatsarā daśa  Ram
parisṛtya ca dharmajño rāghavaḥ saha sītayā
sutīkṣṇasyāśramaṃ śrīmān punar evājagāma ha  Ram
sa tam āśramam āgamya munibhiḥ pratipūjitaḥ
tatrāpi nyavasad rāmaḥ kaṃcit kālam ariṃdamaḥ  Ram
athāśramastho vinayāt kadācit taṃ mahāmunim
upāsīnaḥ sa kākutsthaḥ sutīkṣṇam idam abravīt  Ram
asminn araṇye bhagavann agastyo munisattamaḥ
vasatīti mayā nityaṃ kathāḥ kathayatāṃ śrutam  Ram
na tu jānāmi taṃ deśaṃ vanasyāsya mahattayā
kutrāśramapadaṃ puṇyaṃ maharṣes tasya dhīmataḥ  Ram
prasādāt tatra bhavataḥ sānujaḥ saha sītayā
agastyam abhigaccheyam abhivādayituṃ munim  Ram
manoratho mahān eṣa hṛdi samparivartate
yad ahaṃ taṃ munivaraṃ śuśrūṣeyam api svayam  Ram
iti rāmasya sa muniḥ śrutvā dharmātmano vacaḥ
sutīkṣṇaḥ pratyuvācedaṃ prīto daśarathātmajam  Ram
aham apy etad eva tvāṃ vaktukāmaḥ salakṣmaṇam
agastyam abhigaccheti sītayā saha rāghava  Ram
diṣṭyā tv idānīm arthe 'smin svayam eva bravīṣi mām
aham ākhyāsi te vatsa yatrāgastyo mahāmuniḥ  Ram
yojanāny āśramāt tāta yāhi catvāri vai tataḥ
dakṣiṇena mahāñ śrīmān agastyabhrātur āśramaḥ  Ram
sthalaprāye vanoddeśe pippalīvanaśobhite
bahupuṣpaphale ramye nānāśakuninādite  Ram
padminyo vividhās tatra prasannasalilāḥ śivāḥ
haṃsakāraṇḍavākīrṇāś cakravākopaśobhitāḥ  Ram
tatraikāṃ rajanīm uṣya prabhāte rāma gamyatām
dakṣiṇāṃ diśam āsthāya vanakhaṇḍasya pārśvataḥ  Ram
tatrāgastyāśramapadaṃ gatvā yojanam antaram
ramaṇīye vanoddeśe bahupādapasaṃvṛte
raṃsyate tatra vaidehī lakṣmaṇaś ca tvayā saha  Ram
sa hi ramyo vanoddeśo bahupādapasaṃkulaḥ
yadi buddhiḥ kṛtā draṣṭum agastyaṃ taṃ mahāmunim
adyaiva gamane buddhiṃ rocayasva mahāyaśaḥ  Ram
iti rāmo muneḥ śrutvā saha bhrātrābhivādya ca
pratasthe 'gastyam uddiśya sānujaḥ saha sītayā  Ram
paśyan vanāni citrāṇi parvatāṃś cābhrasaṃnibhān
sarāṃsi saritaś caiva pathi mārgavaśānugāḥ  Ram
sutīkṣṇenopadiṣṭena gatvā tena pathā sukham
idaṃ paramasaṃhṛṣṭo vākyaṃ lakṣmaṇam abravīt  Ram
etad evāśramapadaṃ nūnaṃ tasya mahātmanaḥ
agastyasya muner bhrātur dṛśyate puṇyakarmaṇaḥ  Ram
yathā hīme vanasyāsya jñātāḥ pathi sahasraśaḥ
saṃnatāḥ phalabhāreṇa puṣpabhāreṇa ca drumāḥ  Ram
pippalīnāṃ ca pakvānāṃ vanād asmād upāgataḥ
gandho 'yaṃ pavanotkṣiptaḥ sahasā kaṭukodayaḥ  Ram
tatra tatra ca dṛśyante saṃkṣiptāḥ kāṣṭhasaṃcayāḥ
lūnāś ca pathi dṛśyante darbhā vaiḍūryavarcasaḥ  Ram
etac ca vanamadhyasthaṃ kṛṣṇābhraśikharopamam
pāvakasyāśramasthasya dhūmāgraṃ sampradṛśyate  Ram
vivikteṣu ca tīrtheṣu kṛtasnānā dvijātayaḥ
puṣpopahāraṃ kurvanti kusumaiḥ svayam ārjitaiḥ  Ram
tat sutīkṣṇasya vacanaṃ yathā saumya mayā śrutam
agastyasyāśramo bhrātur nūnam eṣa bhaviṣyati  Ram
nigṛhya tarasā mṛtyuṃ lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā
yasya bhrātrā kṛteyaṃ dik śaraṇyā puṇyakarmaṇā  Ram
ihaikadā kila krūro vātāpir api celvalaḥ
bhrātarau sahitāv āstāṃ brāhmaṇaghnau mahāsurau  Ram
dhārayan brāhmaṇaṃ rūpam ilvalaḥ saṃskṛtaṃ vadan
āmantrayati viprān sa śrāddham uddiśya nirghṛṇaḥ  Ram
bhrātaraṃ saṃskṛtaṃ bhrātā tatas taṃ meṣarūpiṇam
tān dvijān bhojayāmāsa śrāddhadṛṣṭena karmaṇā  Ram
tato bhuktavatāṃ teṣāṃ viprāṇām ilvalo 'bravīt
vātāpe niṣkramasveti svareṇa mahatā vadan  Ram
tato bhrātur vacaḥ śrutvā vātāpir meṣavan nadan
bhittvā bhittvā śarīrāṇi brāhmaṇānāṃ viniṣpatat  Ram
brāhmaṇānāṃ sahasrāṇi tair evaṃ kāmarūpibhiḥ
vināśitāni saṃhatya nityaśaḥ piśitāśanaiḥ  Ram
agastyena tadā devaiḥ prārthitena maharṣiṇā
anubhūya kila śrāddhe bhakṣitaḥ sa mahāsuraḥ  Ram
tataḥ sampannam ity uktvā dattvā hastāvasecanam
bhrātaraṃ niṣkramasveti ilvalaḥ so 'bhyabhāṣata  Ram
taṃ tathā bhāṣamāṇaṃ tu bhrātaraṃ vipraghātinam
abravīt prahasan dhīmān agastyo munisattamaḥ  Ram
kuto niṣkramituṃ śaktir mayā jīrṇasya rakṣasaḥ
bhrātus te meṣarūpasya gatasya yamasādanam  Ram
atha tasya vacaḥ śrutvā bhrātur nidhanasaṃśritam
pradharṣayitum ārebhe muniṃ krodhān niśācaraḥ  Ram
so 'bhyadravad dvijendraṃ taṃ muninā dīptatejasā
cakṣuṣānalakalpena nirdagdho nidhanaṃ gataḥ  Ram
tasyāyam āśramo bhrātus taṭākavanaśobhitaḥ
viprānukampayā yena karmedaṃ duṣkaraṃ kṛtam  Ram
evaṃ kathayamānasya tasya saumitriṇā saha
rāmasyāstaṃ gataḥ sūryaḥ saṃdhyākālo 'bhyavartata  Ram
upāsya paścimāṃ saṃdhyāṃ saha bhrātrā yathāvidhi
praviveśāśramapadaṃ tam ṛṣiṃ cābhyavādayan  Ram
samyak pratigṛhītas tu muninā tena rāghavaḥ
nyavasat tāṃ niśām ekāṃ prāśya mūlaphalāni ca  Ram
tasyāṃ rātryāṃ vyatītāyāṃ vimale sūryamaṇḍale
bhrātaraṃ tam agastyasya āmantrayata rāghavaḥ  Ram
abhivādaye tvā bhagavan sukham adhyuṣito niśām
āmantraye tvāṃ gacchāmi guruṃ te draṣṭum agrajam  Ram
gamyatām iti tenokto jagāma raghunandanaḥ
yathoddiṣṭena mārgeṇa vanaṃ tac cāvalokayan  Ram
nīvārān panasāṃs tālāṃs timiśān vañjulān dhavān
ciribilvān madhūkāṃś ca bilvān api ca tindukān  Ram
puṣpitān puṣpitāgrābhir latābhir anuveṣṭitān
dadarśa rāmaḥ śataśas tatra kāntārapādapān  Ram
hastihastair vimṛditān vānarair upaśobhitān
mattaiḥ śakunisaṃghaiś ca śataśaḥ pratināditān  Ram
tato 'bravīt samīpasthaṃ rāmo rājīvalocanaḥ
pṛṣṭhato 'nugataṃ vīraṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ lakṣmivardhanam  Ram
snigdhapattrā yathā vṛkṣā yathā kṣāntā mṛgadvijāḥ
āśramo nātidūrastho maharṣer bhāvitātmanaḥ  Ram
agastya iti vikhyāto loke svenaiva karmaṇā
āśramo dṛśyate tasya pariśrāntaśramāpahaḥ  Ram
prājyadhūmākulavanaś cīramālāpariṣkṛtaḥ
praśāntamṛgayūthaś ca nānāśakunināditaḥ  Ram
nigṛhya tarasā mṛtyuṃ lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā
dakṣiṇā dik kṛtā yena śaraṇyā puṇyakarmaṇā  Ram
tasyedam āśramapadaṃ prabhāvād yasya rākṣasaiḥ
dig iyaṃ dakṣiṇā trāsād dṛśyate nopabhujyate  Ram
yadāprabhṛti cākrāntā dig iyaṃ puṇyakarmaṇā
tadā prabhṛti nirvairāḥ praśāntā rajanīcarāḥ  Ram
nāmnā ceyaṃ bhagavato dakṣiṇā dik pradakṣiṇā
prathitā triṣu lokeṣu durdharṣā krūrakarmabhiḥ  Ram
mārgaṃ niroddhuṃ satataṃ bhāskarasyācalottamaḥ
saṃdeśaṃ pālayaṃs tasya vindhyaḥ śailo na vardhate  Ram
ayaṃ dīrghāyuṣas tasya loke viśrutakarmaṇaḥ
agastyasyāśramaḥ śrīmān vinītamṛgasevitaḥ  Ram
eṣa lokārcitaḥ sādhur hite nityaṃ rataḥ satām
asmān adhigatān eṣa śreyasā yojayiṣyati  Ram
ārādhayiṣyāmy atrāham agastyaṃ taṃ mahāmunim
śeṣaṃ ca vanavāsasya saumya vatsyāmy ahaṃ prabho  Ram
atra devāḥ sagandharvāḥ siddhāś ca paramarṣayaḥ
agastyaṃ niyatāhāraṃ satataṃ paryupāsate  Ram
nātra jīven mṛṣāvādī krūro vā yadi vā śaṭhaḥ
nṛśaṃsaḥ kāmavṛtto vā munir eṣa tathāvidhaḥ  Ram
atra devāś ca yakṣāś ca nāgāś ca patagaiḥ saha
vasanti niyatāhārā dharmam ārādhayiṣṇavaḥ  Ram
atra siddhā mahātmāno vimānaiḥ sūryasaṃnibhaiḥ
tyaktvā dehān navair dehaiḥ svaryātāḥ paramarṣayaḥ  Ram
yakṣatvam amaratvaṃ ca rājyāni vividhāni ca
atra devāḥ prayacchanti bhūtair ārādhitāḥ śubhaiḥ  Ram
āgatāḥ smāśramapadaṃ saumitre praviśāgrataḥ
nivedayeha māṃ prāptam ṛṣaye saha sītayā  Ram
sa praviśyāśramapadaṃ lakṣmaṇo rāghavānujaḥ
agastyaśiṣyam āsādya vākyam etad uvāca ha  Ram
rājā daśaratho nāma jyeṣṭhas tasya suto balī
rāmaḥ prāpto muniṃ draṣṭuṃ bhāryayā saha sītayā  Ram
lakṣmaṇo nāma tasyāhaṃ bhrātā tv avarajo hitaḥ
anukūlaś ca bhaktaś ca yadi te śrotram āgataḥ  Ram
te vayaṃ vanam atyugraṃ praviṣṭāḥ pitṛśāsanāt
draṣṭum icchāmahe sarve bhagavantaṃ nivedyatām  Ram
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā lakṣmaṇasya tapodhanaḥ
tathety uktvāgniśaraṇaṃ praviveśa niveditum  Ram
sa praviśya muniśreṣṭhaṃ tapasā duṣpradharṣaṇam
kṛtāñjalir uvācedaṃ rāmāgamanam añjasā  Ram
putrau daśarathasyemau rāmo lakṣmaṇa eva ca
praviṣṭāv āśramapadaṃ sītayā saha bhāryayā  Ram
draṣṭuṃ bhavantam āyātau śuśrūṣārtham ariṃdamau
yad atrānantaraṃ tattvam ājñāpayitum arhasi  Ram
tataḥ śiṣyād upaśrutya prāptaṃ rāmaṃ salakṣmaṇam
vaidehīṃ ca mahābhāgām idaṃ vacanam abravīt  Ram
diṣṭyā rāmaś cirasyādya draṣṭuṃ māṃ samupāgataḥ
manasā kāṅkṣitaṃ hy asya mayāpy āgamanaṃ prati  Ram
gamyatāṃ satkṛto rāmaḥ sabhāryaḥ sahalakṣmaṇaḥ
praveśyatāṃ samīpaṃ me kiṃ cāsau na praveśitaḥ  Ram
evam uktas tu muninā dharmajñena mahātmanā
abhivādyābravīc chiṣyas tatheti niyatāñjaliḥ  Ram
tato niṣkramya saṃbhrāntaḥ śiṣyo lakṣmaṇam abravīt
kvāsau rāmo muniṃ draṣṭum etu praviśatu svayam  Ram
tato gatvāśramapadaṃ śiṣyeṇa sahalakṣmaṇaḥ
darśayāmāsa kākutsthaṃ sītāṃ ca janakātmajām  Ram
taṃ śiṣyaḥ praśritaṃ vākyam agastyavacanaṃ bruvan
prāveśayad yathānyāyaṃ satkārārthaṃ susatkṛtam  Ram
praviveśa tato rāmaḥ sītayā sahalakṣmaṇaḥ
praśāntahariṇākīrṇam āśramaṃ hy avalokayan  Ram
sa tatra brahmaṇaḥ sthānam agneḥ sthānaṃ tathaiva ca
viṣṇoḥ sthānaṃ mahendrasya sthānaṃ caiva vivasvataḥ  Ram
somasthānaṃ bhagasthānaṃ sthānaṃ kauberam eva ca
dhātur vidhātuḥ sthānaṃ ca vāyoḥ sthānaṃ tathaiva ca  Ram
tataḥ śiṣyaiḥ parivṛto munir apy abhiniṣpatat
taṃ dadarśāgrato rāmo munīnāṃ dīptatejasam
abravīd vacanaṃ vīro lakṣmaṇaṃ lakṣmivardhanam  Ram
eṣa lakṣmaṇa niṣkrāmaty agastyo bhagavān ṛṣiḥ
audāryeṇāvagacchāmi nidhānaṃ tapasām imam  Ram
evam uktvā mahābāhur agastyaṃ sūryavarcasam
jagrāha paramaprītas tasya pādau paraṃtapaḥ  Ram
abhivādya tu dharmātmā tasthau rāmaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ
sītayā saha vaidehyā tadā rāmaḥ salakṣmaṇaḥ  Ram
pratigṛhya ca kākutstham arcayitvāsanodakaiḥ
kuśalapraśnam uktvā ca āsyatām iti so 'bravīt  Ram
agniṃ hutvā pradāyārghyam atithiṃ pratipūjya ca
vānaprasthena dharmeṇa sa teṣāṃ bhojanaṃ dadau  Ram
prathamaṃ copaviśyātha dharmajño munipuṃgavaḥ
uvāca rāmam āsīnaṃ prāñjaliṃ dharmakovidam  Ram
anyathā khalu kākutstha tapasvī samudācaran
duḥsākṣīva pare loke svāni māṃsāni bhakṣayet  Ram
rājā sarvasya lokasya dharmacārī mahārathaḥ
pūjanīyaś ca mānyaś ca bhavān prāptaḥ priyātithiḥ  Ram
evam uktvā phalair mūlaiḥ puṣpaiś cānyaiś ca rāghavam
pūjayitvā yathākāmaṃ punar eva tato 'bravīt  Ram
idaṃ divyaṃ mahac cāpaṃ hemavajravibhūṣitam
vaiṣṇavaṃ puruṣavyāghra nirmitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā  Ram
amoghaḥ sūryasaṃkāśo brahmadattaḥ śarottamaḥ
datto mama mahendreṇa tūṇī cākṣayasāyakau  Ram
sampūrṇau niśitair bāṇair jvaladbhir iva pāvakaiḥ
mahārajatakośo 'yam asir hemavibhūṣitaḥ  Ram
anena dhanuṣā rāma hatvā saṃkhye mahāsurān
ājahāra śriyaṃ dīptāṃ purā viṣṇur divaukasām  Ram
tad dhanus tau ca tūṇīrau śaraṃ khaḍgaṃ ca mānada
jayāya pratigṛhṇīṣva vajraṃ vajradharo yathā  Ram
evam uktvā mahātejāḥ samastaṃ tad varāyudham
dattvā rāmāya bhagavān agastyaḥ punar abravīt  Ram
rāma prīto 'smi bhadraṃ te parituṣṭo 'smi lakṣmaṇa
abhivādayituṃ yan māṃ prāptau sthaḥ saha sītayā  Ram
adhvaśrameṇa vāṃ khedo bādhate pracuraśramaḥ
vyaktam utkaṇṭhate cāpi maithilī janakātmajā  Ram
eṣā hi sukumārī ca duḥkhaiś ca na vimānitā
prājyadoṣaṃ vanaṃ prāptā bhartṛsnehapracoditā  Ram
yathaiṣā ramate rāma iha sītā tathā kuru
duṣkaraṃ kṛtavaty eṣā vane tvām anugacchatī  Ram
eṣā hi prakṛtiḥ strīṇām āsṛṣṭe raghunandana
samastham anurajyante viṣamasthaṃ tyajanti ca  Ram
śatahradānāṃ lolatvaṃ śastrāṇāṃ tīkṣṇatāṃ tathā
garuḍānilayoḥ śaighryam anugacchanti yoṣitaḥ  Ram
iyaṃ tu bhavato bhāryā doṣair etair vivarjitā
ślāghyā ca vyapadeśyā ca yathā devī hy arundhatī  Ram
alaṃkṛto 'yaṃ deśaś ca yatra saumitriṇā saha
vaidehyā cānayā rāma vatsyasi tvam ariṃdama  Ram
evam uktas tu muninā rāghavaḥ saṃyatāñjaliḥ
uvāca praśritaṃ vākyam ṛṣiṃ dīptam ivānalam  Ram
dhanyo 'smy anugṛhīto 'smi yasya me munipuṃgavaḥ
guṇaiḥ sabhrātṛbhāryasya varadaḥ parituṣyati  Ram
kiṃ tu vyādiśa me deśaṃ sodakaṃ bahukānanam
yatrāśramapadaṃ kṛtvā vaseyaṃ nirataḥ sukham  Ram
tato 'bravīn muniśreṣṭhaḥ śrutvā rāmasya bhāṣitam
dhyātvā muhūrtaṃ dharmātmā dhīro dhīrataraṃ vacaḥ  Ram
ito dviyojane tāta bahumūlaphalodakaḥ
deśo bahumṛgaḥ śrīmān pañcavaṭy abhiviśrutaḥ  Ram
tatra gatvāśramapadaṃ kṛtvā saumitriṇā saha
ramasva tvaṃ pitur vākyaṃ yathoktam anupālayan  Ram
vidito hy eṣa vṛttānto mama sarvas tavānagha
tapasaś ca prabhāvena snehād daśarathasya ca  Ram
hṛdayasthaś ca te chando vijñātas tapasā mayā
iha vāsaṃ pratijñāya mayā saha tapovane  Ram
ataś ca tvām ahaṃ brūmi gaccha pañcavaṭīm iti
sa hi ramyo vanoddeśo maithilī tatra raṃsyate  Ram
sa deśaḥ ślāghanīyaś ca nātidūre ca rāghava
godāvaryāḥ samīpe ca maithilī tatra raṃsyate  Ram
prājyamūlaphalaiś caiva nānādvijagaṇair yutaḥ
viviktaś ca mahābāho puṇyo ramyas tathaiva ca  Ram
bhavān api sadāraś ca śaktaś ca parirakṣaṇe
api cātra vasan rāmas tāpasān pālayiṣyasi  Ram
etad ālakṣyate vīra madhūkānāṃ mahad vanam
uttareṇāsya gantavyaṃ nyagrodham abhigacchatā  Ram
tataḥ sthalam upāruhya parvatasyāvidūrataḥ
khyātaḥ pañcavaṭīty eva nityapuṣpitakānanaḥ  Ram
agastyenaivam uktas tu rāmaḥ saumitriṇā saha
satkṛtyāmantrayāmāsa tam ṛṣiṃ satyavādinam  Ram
tau tu tenābhyanujñātau kṛtapādābhivandanau
tadāśramāt pañcavaṭīṃ jagmatuḥ saha sītayā  Ram
gṛhītacāpau tu narādhipātmajau viṣaktatūṇī samareṣv akātarau
yathopadiṣṭena pathā maharṣiṇā prajagmatuḥ pañcavaṭīṃ samāhitau  Ram
atha pañcavaṭīṃ gacchann antarā raghunandanaḥ
āsasāda mahākāyaṃ gṛdhraṃ bhīmaparākramam  Ram
taṃ dṛṣṭvā tau mahābhāgau vanasthaṃ rāmalakṣmaṇau
menāte rākṣasaṃ pakṣiṃ bruvāṇau ko bhavān iti  Ram
sa tau madhurayā vācā saumyayā prīṇayann iva
uvāca vatsa māṃ viddhi vayasyaṃ pitur ātmanaḥ  Ram
sa taṃ pitṛsakhaṃ buddhvā pūjayāmāsa rāghavaḥ
sa tasya kulam avyagram atha papraccha nāma ca  Ram
rāmasya vacanaṃ śrutvā kulam ātmānam eva ca
ācacakṣe dvijas tasmai sarvabhūtasamudbhavam  Ram
pūrvakāle mahābāho ye prajāpatayo 'bhavan
tān me nigadataḥ sarvān āditaḥ śṛṇu rāghava  Ram
kardamaḥ prathamas teṣāṃ vikṛtas tadanantaram
śeṣaś ca saṃśrayaś caiva bahuputraś ca vīryavān  Ram
sthāṇur marīcir atriś ca kratuś caiva mahābalaḥ
pulastyaś cāṅgirāś caiva pracetāḥ pulahas tathā  Ram
dakṣo vivasvān aparo 'riṣṭanemiś ca rāghava
kaśyapaś ca mahātejās teṣām āsīc ca paścimaḥ  Ram
prajāpates tu dakṣasya babhūvur iti naḥ śrutam
ṣaṣṭir duhitaro rāma yaśasvinyo mahāyaśaḥ  Ram
kaśyapaḥ pratijagrāha tāsām aṣṭau sumadhyamāḥ
aditiṃ ca ditiṃ caiva danum api ca kālakām  Ram
tāmrāṃ krodhavaśāṃ caiva manuṃ cāpy analām api
tās tu kanyās tataḥ prītaḥ kaśyapaḥ punar abravīt  Ram
putrāṃs trailokyabhartṝn vai janayiṣyatha matsamān
aditis tanmanā rāma ditiś ca danur eva ca  Ram
kālakā ca mahābāho śeṣās tv amanaso 'bhavan
adityāṃ jajñire devās trayastriṃśad ariṃdama  Ram
ādityā vasavo rudrā aśvinau ca paraṃtapa
ditis tv ajanayat putrān daityāṃs tāta yaśasvinaḥ  Ram
teṣām iyaṃ vasumatī purāsīt savanārṇavā
danus tv ajanayat putram aśvagrīvam ariṃdama  Ram
narakaṃ kālakaṃ caiva kālakāpi vyajāyata
krauñcīṃ bhāsīṃ tathā śyenīṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrīṃ tathā śukīm  Ram
tāmrāpi suṣuve kanyāḥ pañcaitā lokaviśrutāḥ
ulūkāñ janayat krauñcī bhāsī bhāsān vyajāyata  Ram
śyenī śyenāṃś ca gṛdhrāṃś ca vyajāyata sutejasaḥ
dhṛtarāṣṭrī tu haṃsāṃś ca kalahaṃsāṃś ca sarvaśaḥ  Ram
cakravākāṃś ca bhadraṃ te vijajñe sāpi bhāminī
śukī natāṃ vijajñe tu natāyā vinatā sutā  Ram
daśa krodhavaśā rāma vijajñe 'py ātmasambhavāḥ
mṛgīṃ ca mṛgamandāṃ ca harīṃ bhadramadām api  Ram
mātaṃgīm atha śārdūlīṃ śvetāṃ ca surabhīṃ tathā
sarvalakṣaṇasampannāṃ surasāṃ kadrukām api  Ram
apatyaṃ tu mṛgāḥ sarve mṛgyā naravarottama
ṛkṣāś ca mṛgamandāyāḥ sṛmarāś camarās tathā  Ram
tatas tv irāvatīṃ nāma jajñe bhadramadā sutām
tasyās tv airāvataḥ putro lokanātho mahāgajaḥ  Ram
haryāś ca harayo 'patyaṃ vānarāś ca tapasvinaḥ
golāṅgūlāṃś ca śārdūlī vyāghrāṃś cājanayat sutān  Ram
mātaṃgyās tv atha mātaṃgā apatyaṃ manujarṣabha
diśāgajaṃ tu śvetākṣaṃ śvetā vyajanayat sutam  Ram
tato duhitarau rāma surabhir devy ajāyata
rohiṇīṃ nāma bhadraṃ te gandharvīṃ ca yaśasvinīm  Ram
rohiṇy ajanayad gā vai gandharvī vājinaḥ sutān
surasājanayan nāgān rāma kadrūś ca pannagān  Ram
manur manuṣyāñ janayat kaśyapasya mahātmanaḥ
brāhmaṇān kṣatriyān vaiśyāñ śūdrāṃś ca manujarṣabha  Ram
mukhato brāhmaṇā jātā urasaḥ kṣatriyās tathā
ūrubhyāṃ jajñire vaiśyāḥ padbhyāṃ śūdrā iti śrutiḥ  Ram
sarvān puṇyaphalān vṛkṣān analāpi vyajāyata
vinatā ca śukī pautrī kadrūś ca surasā svasā  Ram
kadrūr nāgaṃ sahasraṃ tu vijajñe dharaṇīdharam
dvau putrau vinatāyās tu garuḍo 'ruṇa eva ca  Ram
tasmāj jāto 'ham aruṇāt sampātiś ca mamāgrajaḥ
jaṭāyur iti māṃ viddhi śyenīputram ariṃdama  Ram
so 'haṃ vāsasahāyas te bhaviṣyāmi yadīcchasi
sītāṃ ca tāta rakṣiṣye tvayi yāte salakṣmaṇe  Ram
jaṭāyuṣaṃ tu pratipūjya rāghavo mudā pariṣvajya ca saṃnato 'bhavat
pitur hi śuśrāva sakhitvam ātmavāñ jaṭāyuṣā saṃkathitaṃ punaḥ punaḥ  Ram
sa tatra sītāṃ paridāya maithilīṃ sahaiva tenātibalena pakṣiṇā
jagāma tāṃ pañcavaṭīṃ salakṣmaṇo ripūn didhakṣañ śalabhān ivānalaḥ  Ram
tataḥ pañcavaṭīṃ gatvā nānāvyālamṛgāyutām
uvāca bhrātaraṃ rāmo lakṣmaṇaṃ dīptatejasam  Ram
āgatāḥ sma yathoddiṣṭam amuṃ deśaṃ maharṣiṇā
ayaṃ pañcavaṭīdeśaḥ saumya puṣpitakānanaḥ  Ram
sarvataś cāryatāṃ dṛṣṭiḥ kānane nipuṇo hy asi
āśramaḥ katarasmin no deśe bhavati saṃmataḥ  Ram
ramate yatra vaidehī tvam ahaṃ caiva lakṣmaṇa
tādṛśo dṛśyatāṃ deśaḥ saṃnikṛṣṭajalāśayaḥ  Ram
vanarāmaṇyakaṃ yatra jalarāmaṇyakaṃ tathā
saṃnikṛṣṭaṃ ca yatra syāt samitpuṣpakuśodakam  Ram
evam uktas tu rāmeṇa lakṣmaṇaḥ saṃyatāñjaliḥ
sītāsamakṣaṃ kākutstham idaṃ vacanam abravīt  Ram
paravān asmi kākutstha tvayi varṣaśataṃ sthite
svayaṃ tu rucire deśe kriyatām iti māṃ vada  Ram
suprītas tena vākyena lakṣmaṇasya mahādyutiḥ
vimṛśan rocayāmāsa deśaṃ sarvaguṇānvitam  Ram
sa taṃ ruciram ākramya deśam āśramakarmaṇi
hastau gṛhītvā hastena rāmaḥ saumitrim abravīt  Ram
ayaṃ deśaḥ samaḥ śrīmān puṣpitais tarubhir vṛtaḥ
ihāśramapadaṃ saumya yathāvat kartum arhasi  Ram
iyam ādityasaṃkāśaiḥ padmaiḥ surabhigandhibhiḥ
adūre dṛśyate ramyā padminī padmaśobhitā  Ram
yathākhyātam agastyena muninā bhāvitātmanā
iyaṃ godāvarī ramyā puṣpitais tarubhir vṛtā  Ram
haṃsakāraṇḍavākīrṇā cakravākopaśobhitā
nātidūre na cāsanne mṛgayūthanipīḍitā  Ram
mayūranāditā ramyāḥ prāṃśavo bahukandarāḥ
dṛśyante girayaḥ saumya phullais tarubhir āvṛtāḥ  Ram
sauvarṇe rājatais tāmrair deśe deśe ca dhātubhiḥ
gavākṣitā ivābhānti gajāḥ paramabhaktibhiḥ  Ram
sālais tālais tamālaiś ca kharjūraiḥ panasāmrakaiḥ
nīvārais timiśaiś caiva puṃnāgaiś copaśobhitāḥ  Ram
cūtair aśokais tilakaiś campakaiḥ ketakair api
puṣpagulmalatopetais tais tais tarubhir āvṛtāḥ  Ram
candanaiḥ syandanair nīpaiḥ panasair lakucair api
dhavāśvakarṇakhadiraiḥ śamīkiṃśukapāṭalaiḥ  Ram
idaṃ puṇyam idaṃ medhyam idaṃ bahumṛgadvijam
iha vatsyāma saumitre sārdham etena pakṣiṇā  Ram
evam uktas tu rāmeṇa lakṣmaṇaḥ paravīrahā
acireṇāśramaṃ bhrātuś cakāra sumahābalaḥ  Ram
parṇaśālāṃ suvipulāṃ tatra saṃghātamṛttikām
sustambhāṃ maskarair dīrghaiḥ kṛtavaṃśāṃ suśobhanām  Ram
sa gatvā lakṣmaṇaḥ śrīmān nadīṃ godāvarīṃ tadā
snātvā padmāni cādāya saphalaḥ punar āgataḥ  Ram
tataḥ puṣpabaliṃ kṛtvā śāntiṃ ca sa yathāvidhi
darśayāmāsa rāmāya tad āśramapadaṃ kṛtam  Ram
sa taṃ dṛṣṭvā kṛtaṃ saumyam āśramaṃ saha sītayā
rāghavaḥ parṇaśālāyāṃ harṣam āhārayat param  Ram
susaṃhṛṣṭaḥ pariṣvajya bāhubhyāṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ tadā
atisnigdhaṃ ca gāḍhaṃ ca vacanaṃ cedam abravīt  Ram
prīto 'smi te mahat karma tvayā kṛtam idaṃ prabho
pradeyo yannimittaṃ te pariṣvaṅgo mayā kṛtaḥ  Ram
bhāvajñena kṛtajñena dharmajñena ca lakṣmaṇa
tvayā putreṇa dharmātmā na saṃvṛttaḥ pitā mama  Ram
evaṃ lakṣmaṇam uktvā tu rāghavo lakṣmivardhanaḥ
tasmin deśe bahuphale nyavasat sa sukhaṃ vaśī  Ram
kaṃcit kālaṃ sa dharmātmā sītayā lakṣmaṇena ca
anvāsyamāno nyavasat svargaloke yathāmaraḥ  Ram
asatas tasya tu sukhaṃ rāghavasya mahātmanaḥ
śaradvyapāye hemanta ṛtur iṣṭaḥ pravartate  Ram
sa kadācit prabhātāyāṃ śarvaryāṃ raghunandanaḥ
prayayāv abhiṣekārthaṃ ramyāṃ godāvarīṃ nadīm  Ram
prahvaḥ kalaśahastas taṃ sītayā saha vīryavān
pṛṣṭhato 'nuvrajan bhrātā saumitrir idam abravīt  Ram
ayaṃ sa kālaḥ samprāptaḥ priyo yas te priyaṃvada
alaṃkṛta ivābhāti yena saṃvatsaraḥ śubhaḥ  Ram
nīhāraparuṣo lokaḥ pṛthivī sasyamālinī
jalāny anupabhogyāni subhago havyavāhanaḥ  Ram
navāgrayaṇapūjābhir abhyarcya pitṛdevatāḥ
kṛtāgrayaṇakāḥ kāle santo vigatakalmaṣāḥ  Ram
prājyakāmā janapadāḥ sampannataragorasāḥ
vicaranti mahīpālā yātrārthaṃ vijigīṣavaḥ  Ram
sevamāne dṛḍhaṃ sūrye diśam antakasevitām
vihīnatilakeva strī nottarā dik prakāśate  Ram
prakṛtyā himakośāḍhyo dūrasūryaś ca sāmpratam
yathārthanāmā suvyaktaṃ himavān himavān giriḥ  Ram
atyantasukhasaṃcārā madhyāhne sparśataḥ sukhāḥ
divasāḥ subhagādityāś chāyāsaliladurbhagāḥ  Ram
mṛdusūryāḥ sanīhārāḥ paṭuśītāḥ samārutāḥ
śūnyāraṇyā himadhvastā divasā bhānti sāmpratam  Ram
nivṛttākāśaśayanāḥ puṣyanītā himāruṇāḥ
śītā vṛddhatarāyāmās triyāmā yānti sāmpratam  Ram
ravisaṃkrāntasaubhāgyas tuṣārāruṇamaṇḍalaḥ
niḥśvāsāndha ivādarśaś candramā na prakāśate  Ram
jyotsnā tuṣāramalinā paurṇamāsyāṃ na rājate
sīteva cātapaśyāmā lakṣyate na tu śobhate  Ram
prakṛtyā śītalasparśo himaviddhaś ca sāmpratam
pravāti paścimo vāyuḥ kāle dviguṇaśītalaḥ  Ram
bāṣpacchannānyaraṇyāni yavagodhūmavanti ca
śobhante 'bhyudite sūrye nadadbhiḥ krauñcasārasaiḥ  Ram
kharjūrapuṣpākṛtibhiḥ śirobhiḥ pūrṇataṇḍulaiḥ
śobhante kiṃcidālambāḥ śālayaḥ kanakaprabhāḥ  Ram
mayūkhair upasarpadbhir himanīhārasaṃvṛtaiḥ
dūram abhyuditaḥ sūryaḥ śaśāṅka iva lakṣyate  Ram
agrāhyavīryaḥ pūrvāhṇe madhyāhne sparśataḥ sukhaḥ
saṃraktaḥ kiṃcid āpāṇḍur ātapaḥ śobhate kṣitau  Ram
avaśyāyanipātena kiṃcit praklinnaśādvalā
vanānāṃ śobhate bhūmir niviṣṭataruṇātapā  Ram
avaśyāyatamonaddhā nīhāratamasāvṛtāḥ
prasuptā iva lakṣyante vipuṣpā vanarājayaḥ  Ram
bāṣpasaṃchannasalilā rutavijñeyasārasāḥ
himārdravālukais tīraiḥ sarito bhānti sāmpratam  Ram
tuṣārapatanāc caiva mṛdutvād bhāskarasya ca
śaityād agāgrastham api prāyeṇa rasavaj jalam  Ram
jarājarjaritaiḥ parṇaiḥ śīrṇakesarakarṇikaiḥ
nālaśeṣā himadhvastā na bhānti kamalākarāḥ  Ram
asmiṃs tu puruṣavyāghra kāle duḥkhasamanvitaḥ
tapaś carati dharmātmā tvadbhaktyā bharataḥ pure  Ram
tyaktvā rājyaṃ ca mānaṃ ca bhogāṃś ca vividhān bahūn
tapasvī niyatāhāraḥ śete śīte mahītale  Ram
so 'pi velām imāṃ nūnam abhiṣekārtham udyataḥ
vṛtaḥ prakṛtibhir nityaṃ prayāti sarayūṃ nadīm  Ram
atyantasukhasaṃvṛddhaḥ sukumāro himārditaḥ
kathaṃ tv apararātreṣu sarayūm avagāhate  Ram
padmapattrekṣaṇaḥ śyāmaḥ śrīmān nirudaro mahān
dharmajñaḥ satyavādī ca hrīniṣedho jitendriyaḥ  Ram
priyābhibhāṣī madhuro dīrghabāhur ariṃdamaḥ
saṃtyajya vividhān bhogān āryaṃ sarvātmanāśritaḥ  Ram
jitaḥ svargas tava bhrātrā bharatena mahātmanā
vanastham api tāpasye yas tvām anuvidhīyate  Ram
na pitryam anuvartante mātṛkaṃ dvipadā iti
khyāto lokapravādo 'yaṃ bharatenānyathākṛtaḥ  Ram
bhartā daśaratho yasyāḥ sādhuś ca bharataḥ sutaḥ
kathaṃ nu sāmbā kaikeyī tādṛśī krūradarśinī  Ram
ity evaṃ lakṣmaṇe vākyaṃ snehād bruvati dhārmike
parivādaṃ jananyās tam asahan rāghavo 'bravīt  Ram
na te 'mbā madhyamā tāta garhitavyā kathaṃcana
tām evekṣvākunāthasya bharatasya kathāṃ kuru  Ram
niścitāpi hi me buddhir vanavāse dṛḍhavratā
bharatasnehasaṃtaptā bāliśī kriyate punaḥ  Ram
ity evaṃ vilapaṃs tatra prāpya godāvarīṃ nadīm
cakre 'bhiṣekaṃ kākutsthaḥ sānujaḥ saha sītayā  Ram
tarpayitvātha salilais te pitṝn daivatāni ca
stuvanti smoditaṃ sūryaṃ devatāś ca samāhitāḥ  Ram
kṛtābhiṣekaḥ sa rarāja rāmaḥ sītādvitīyaḥ saha lakṣmaṇena
kṛtābhiṣekas tv agarājaputryā rudraḥ sanandī bhagavān iveśaḥ  Ram
kṛtābhiṣeko rāmas tu sītā saumitrir eva ca
tasmād godāvarītīrāt tato jagmuḥ svam āśramam  Ram
āśramaṃ tam upāgamya rāghavaḥ sahalakṣmaṇaḥ
kṛtvā paurvāhṇikaṃ karma parṇaśālām upāgamat  Ram
sa rāmaḥ parṇaśālāyām āsīnaḥ saha sītayā
virarāja mahābāhuś citrayā candramā iva
lakṣmaṇena saha bhrātrā cakāra vividhāḥ kathāḥ  Ram
tadāsīnasya rāmasya kathāsaṃsaktacetasaḥ
taṃ deśaṃ rākṣasī kācid ājagāma yadṛcchayā  Ram
sā tu śūrpaṇakhā nāma daśagrīvasya rakṣasaḥ
bhaginī rāmam āsādya dadarśa tridaśopamam  Ram
siṃhoraskaṃ mahābāhuṃ padmapattranibhekṣaṇam
sukumāraṃ mahāsattvaṃ pārthivavyañjanānvitam  Ram
rāmam indīvaraśyāmaṃ kandarpasadṛśaprabham
babhūvendropamaṃ dṛṣṭvā rākṣasī kāmamohitā  Ram
sumukhaṃ durmukhī rāmaṃ vṛttamadhyaṃ mahodarī
viśālākṣaṃ virūpākṣī sukeśaṃ tāmramūrdhajā  Ram
priyarūpaṃ virūpā sā susvaraṃ bhairavasvarā
taruṇaṃ dāruṇā vṛddhā dakṣiṇaṃ vāmabhāṣiṇī  Ram
nyāyavṛttaṃ sudurvṛttā priyam apriyadarśanā
śarīrajasamāviṣṭā rākṣasī rāmam abravīt  Ram
jaṭī tāpasarūpeṇa sabhāryaḥ śaracāpadhṛk
āgatas tvam imaṃ deśaṃ kathaṃ rākṣasasevitam  Ram
evam uktas tu rākṣasyā śūrpaṇakhyā paraṃtapaḥ
ṛjubuddhitayā sarvam ākhyātum upacakrame  Ram
āsīd daśaratho nāma rājā tridaśavikramaḥ
tasyāham agrajaḥ putro rāmo nāma janaiḥ śrutaḥ  Ram
bhrātāyaṃ lakṣmaṇo nāma yavīyān mām anuvrataḥ
iyaṃ bhāryā ca vaidehī mama sīteti viśrutā  Ram
niyogāt tu narendrasya pitur mātuś ca yantritaḥ
dharmārthaṃ dharmakāṅkṣī ca vanaṃ vastum ihāgataḥ  Ram
tvāṃ tu veditum icchāmi kathyatāṃ kāsi kasya vā
iha vā kiṃnimittaṃ tvam āgatā brūhi tattvataḥ  Ram
sābravīd vacanaṃ śrutvā rākṣasī madanārditā
śrūyatāṃ rāma vakṣyāmi tattvārthaṃ vacanaṃ mama  Ram
ahaṃ śūrpaṇakhā nāma rākṣasī kāmarūpiṇī
araṇyaṃ vicarāmīdam ekā sarvabhayaṃkarā  Ram
rāvaṇo nāma me bhrātā rākṣaso rākṣaseśvaraḥ
pravṛddhanidraś ca sadā kumbhakarṇo mahābalaḥ  Ram
vibhīṣaṇas tu dharmātmā na tu rākṣasaceṣṭitaḥ
prakhyātavīryau ca raṇe bhrātarau kharadūṣaṇau  Ram
tān ahaṃ samatikrāntā rāma tvā pūrvadarśanāt
samupetāsmi bhāvena bhartāraṃ puruṣottamam
cirāya bhava bhartā me sītayā kiṃ kariṣyasi  Ram
vikṛtā ca virūpā ca na seyaṃ sadṛśī tava
aham evānurūpā te bhāryā rūpeṇa paśya mām  Ram
imāṃ virūpām asatīṃ karālāṃ nirṇatodarīm
anena saha te bhrātrā bhakṣayiṣyāmi mānuṣīm  Ram
tataḥ parvataśṛṅgāṇi vanāni vividhāni ca
paśyan saha mayā kānta daṇḍakān vicariṣyasi  Ram
ity evam uktaḥ kākutsthaḥ prahasya madirekṣaṇām
idaṃ vacanam ārebhe vaktuṃ vākyaviśāradaḥ  Ram
tāṃ tu śūrpaṇakhāṃ rāmaḥ kāmapāśāvapāśitām
svacchayā ślakṣṇayā vācā smitapūrvam athābravīt  Ram
kṛtadāro 'smi bhavati bhāryeyaṃ dayitā mama
tvadvidhānāṃ tu nārīṇāṃ suduḥkhā sasapatnatā  Ram
anujas tv eṣa me bhrātā śīlavān priyadarśanaḥ
śrīmān akṛtadāraś ca lakṣmaṇo nāma vīryavān  Ram
apūrvī bhāryayā cārthī taruṇaḥ priyadarśanaḥ
anurūpaś ca te bhartā rūpasyāsya bhaviṣyati  Ram
enaṃ bhaja viśālākṣi bhartāraṃ bhrātaraṃ mama
asapatnā varārohe merum arkaprabhā yathā  Ram
iti rāmeṇa sā proktā rākṣasī kāmamohitā
visṛjya rāmaṃ sahasā tato lakṣmaṇam abravīt  Ram
asya rūpasya te yuktā bhāryāhaṃ varavarṇinī
mayā saha sukhaṃ sarvān daṇḍakān vicariṣyasi  Ram
evam uktas tu saumitrī rākṣasyā vākyakovidaḥ
tataḥ śūrpaṇakhīṃ smitvā lakṣmaṇo yuktam abravīt  Ram
kathaṃ dāsasya me dāsī bhāryā bhavitum icchasi
so 'ham āryeṇa paravān bhrātrā kamalavarṇini  Ram
samṛddhārthasya siddhārthā muditāmalavarṇinī
āryasya tvaṃ viśālākṣi bhāryā bhava yavīyasī  Ram
etāṃ virūpām asatīṃ karālāṃ nirṇatodarīm
bhāryāṃ vṛddhāṃ parityajya tvām evaiṣa bhajiṣyati  Ram
ko hi rūpam idaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ saṃtyajya varavarṇini
mānuṣeṣu varārohe kuryād bhāvaṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ  Ram
iti sā lakṣmaṇenoktā karālā nirṇatodarī
manyate tad vacaḥ satyaṃ parihāsāvicakṣaṇā  Ram
sā rāmaṃ parṇaśālāyām upaviṣṭaṃ paraṃtapam
sītayā saha durdharṣam abravīt kāmamohitā  Ram
imāṃ virūpām asatīṃ karālāṃ nirṇatodarīm
vṛddhāṃ bhāryām avaṣṭabhya na māṃ tvaṃ bahu manyase  Ram
adyemāṃ bhakṣayiṣyāmi paśyatas tava mānuṣīm
tvayā saha cariṣyāmi niḥsapatnā yathāsukham  Ram
ity uktvā mṛgaśāvākṣīm alātasadṛśekṣaṇā
abhyadhāvat susaṃkruddhā maholkā rohiṇīm iva  Ram
tāṃ mṛtyupāśapratimām āpatantīṃ mahābalaḥ
nigṛhya rāmaḥ kupitas tato lakṣmaṇam abravīt  Ram
krūrair anāryaiḥ saumitre parihāsaḥ kathaṃcana
na kāryaḥ paśya vaidehīṃ kathaṃcit saumya jīvatīm  Ram
imāṃ virūpām asatīm atimattāṃ mahodarīm
rākṣasīṃ puruṣavyāghra virūpayitum arhasi  Ram
ity ukto lakṣmaṇas tasyāḥ kruddho rāmasya paśyataḥ
uddhṛtya khaḍgaṃ cicheda karṇanāsaṃ mahābalaḥ  Ram
nikṛttakarṇanāsā tu visvaraṃ sā vinadya ca
yathāgataṃ pradudrāva ghorā śūrpaṇakhā vanam  Ram
sā virūpā mahāghorā rākṣasī śoṇitokṣitā
nanāda vividhān nādān yathā prāvṛṣi toyadaḥ  Ram
sā vikṣarantī rudhiraṃ bahudhā ghoradarśanā
pragṛhya bāhū garjantī praviveśa mahāvanam  Ram
tatas tu sā rākṣasasaṃghasaṃvṛtaṃ kharaṃ janasthānagataṃ virūpitā
upetya taṃ bhrātaram ugratejasaṃ papāta bhūmau gaganād yathāśaniḥ  Ram
tataḥ sabhāryaṃ bhayamohamūrchitā salakṣmaṇaṃ rāghavam āgataṃ vanam
virūpaṇaṃ cātmani śoṇitokṣitā śaśaṃsa sarvaṃ bhaginī kharasya sā  Ram
tāṃ tathā patitāṃ dṛṣṭvā virūpāṃ śoṇitokṣitām
bhaginīṃ krodhasaṃtaptaḥ kharaḥ papraccha rākṣasaḥ  Ram
balavikramasampannā kāmagā kāmarūpiṇī
imām avasthāṃ nītā tvaṃ kenāntakasamā gatā  Ram
devagandharvabhūtānām ṛṣīṇāṃ ca mahātmanām
ko 'yam evaṃ mahāvīryas tvāṃ virūpāṃ cakāra ha  Ram
na hi paśyāmy ahaṃ loke yaḥ kuryān mama vipriyam
antarena sahasrākṣaṃ mahendraṃ pākaśāsanam  Ram
adyāhaṃ mārgaṇaiḥ prāṇān ādāsye jīvitāntakaiḥ
salile kṣīram āsaktaṃ niṣpibann iva sārasaḥ  Ram
nihatasya mayā saṃkhye śarasaṃkṛttamarmaṇaḥ
saphenaṃ rudhiraṃ raktaṃ medinī kasya pāsyati  Ram
kasya pattrarathāḥ kāyān māṃsam utkṛtya saṃgatāḥ
prahṛṣṭā bhakṣayiṣyanti nihatasya mayā raṇe  Ram
taṃ na devā na gandharvā na piśācā na rākṣasāḥ
mayāpakṛṣṭaṃ kṛpaṇaṃ śaktās trātuṃ mahāhave  Ram
upalabhya śanaiḥ saṃjñāṃ taṃ me śaṃsitum arhasi
yena tvaṃ durvinītena vane vikramya nirjitā  Ram
iti bhrātur vacaḥ śrutvā kruddhasya ca viśeṣataḥ
tataḥ śūrpaṇakhā vākyaṃ sabāṣpam idam abravīt  Ram
taruṇau rūpasampannau sukumārau mahābalau
puṇḍarīkaviśālākṣau cīrakṛṣṇājināmbarau  Ram
gandharvarājapratimau pārthivavyañjanānvitau
devau vā mānuṣau vā tau na tarkayitum utsahe  Ram
taruṇī rūpasampannā sarvābharaṇabhūṣitā
dṛṣṭā tatra mayā nārī tayor madhye sumadhyamā  Ram
tābhyām ubhābhyāṃ sambhūya pramadām adhikṛtya tām
imām avasthāṃ nītāhaṃ yathānāthāsatī tathā  Ram
tasyāś cānṛjuvṛttāyās tayoś ca hatayor aham
saphenaṃ pātum icchāmi rudhiraṃ raṇamūrdhani  Ram
eṣa me prathamaḥ kāmaḥ kṛtas tāta tvayā bhavet
tasyās tayoś ca rudhiraṃ pibeyam aham āhave  Ram
iti tasyāṃ bruvāṇāyāṃ caturdaśa mahābalān
vyādideśa kharaḥ kruddho rākṣasān antakopamān  Ram
mānuṣau śastrasampannau cīrakṛṣṇājināmbarau
praviṣṭau daṇḍakāraṇyaṃ ghoraṃ pramadayā saha  Ram
tau hatvā tāṃ ca durvṛttām upāvartitum arhatha
iyaṃ ca rudhiraṃ teṣāṃ bhaginī mama pāsyati  Ram
manoratho 'yam iṣṭo 'syā bhaginyā mama rākṣasāḥ
śīghraṃ saṃpadyatāṃ gatvā tau pramathya svatejasā  Ram
iti pratisamādiṣṭā rākṣasās te caturdaśa
tatra jagmus tayā sārdhaṃ ghanā vāteritā yathā  Ram
ataḥ śūrpaṇakhā ghorā rāghavāśramam āgatā
rakṣasām ācacakṣe tau bhrātarau saha sītayā  Ram
te rāmaṃ parṇaśālāyām upaviṣṭaṃ mahābalam
dadṛśuḥ sītayā sārdhaṃ vaidehyā lakṣmaṇena ca  Ram
tān dṛṣṭvā rāghavaḥ śrīmān āgatāṃ tāṃ ca rākṣasīm
abravīd bhrātaraṃ rāmo lakṣmaṇaṃ dīptatejasam  Ram
muhūrtaṃ bhava saumitre sītāyāḥ pratyanantaraḥ
imān asyā vadhiṣyāmi padavīm āgatān iha  Ram
vākyam etat tataḥ śrutvā rāmasya viditātmanaḥ
tatheti lakṣmaṇo vākyaṃ rāmasya pratyapūjayat  Ram
rāghavo 'pi mahac cāpaṃ cāmīkaravibhūṣitam
cakāra sajyaṃ dharmātmā tāni rakṣāṃsi cābravīt  Ram
putrau daśarathasyāvāṃ bhrātarau rāmalakṣmaṇau
praviṣṭau sītayā sārdhaṃ duścaraṃ daṇḍakāvanam  Ram
phalamūlāśanau dāntau tāpasau dharmacāriṇau
vasantau daṇḍakāraṇye kimartham upahiṃsatha  Ram
yuṣmān pāpātmakān hantuṃ viprakārān mahāvane
ṛṣīṇāṃ tu niyogena prāpto 'haṃ saśarāsanaḥ  Ram
tiṣṭhataivātra saṃtuṣṭā nopasarpitum arhatha
yadi prāṇair ihārtho vo nivartadhvaṃ niśācarāḥ  Ram
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā rākṣasās te caturdaśa
ūcur vācaṃ susaṃkruddhā brahmaghnāḥ śūlapāṇayaḥ  Ram
saṃraktanayanā ghorā rāmaṃ raktāntalocanam
paruṣāmadhurābhāṣaṃ hṛṣṭā dṛṣṭaparākramam  Ram
krodham utpādya no bhartuḥ kharasya sumahātmanaḥ
tvam eva hāsyase prāṇān adyāsmābhir hato yudhi  Ram
kā hi te śaktir ekasya bahūnāṃ raṇamūrdhani
asmākam agrataḥ sthātuṃ kiṃ punar yoddhum āhave  Ram
ebhir bāhuprayuktair naḥ parighaiḥ śūlapaṭṭiśaiḥ
prāṇāṃs tyakṣyasi vīryaṃ ca dhanuś ca karapīḍitam  Ram
ity evam uktvā saṃrabdhā rākṣasās te caturdaśa
udyatāyudhanistriṃśā rāmam evābhidudruvuḥ
cikṣipus tāni śūlāni rāghavaṃ prati durjayam  Ram
tāni śūlāni kākutsthaḥ samastāni caturdaśa
tāvadbhir eva cicheda śaraiḥ kāñcanabhūṣaṇaiḥ  Ram
tataḥ paścān mahātejā nārācān sūryasaṃnibhān
jagrāha paramakruddhaś caturdaśa śilāśitān  Ram
gṛhītvā dhanur āyamya lakṣyān uddiśya rākṣasān
mumoca rāghavo bāṇān vajrān iva śatakratuḥ  Ram
rukmapuṅkhāś ca viśikhāḥ pradīptā hemabhūṣaṇāḥ
antarikṣe maholkānāṃ babhūvus tulyavarcasaḥ  Ram
te bhittvā rakṣasāṃ vegād vakṣāṃsi rudhirāplutāḥ
viniṣpetus tadā bhūmau nyamajjantāśanisvanāḥ  Ram
te bhinnahṛdayā bhūmau chinnamūlā iva drumāḥ
nipetuḥ śoṇitārdrāṅgā vikṛtā vigatāsavaḥ  Ram
tān bhūmau patitān dṛṣṭvā rākṣasī krodhamūrchitā
paritrastā punas tatra vyasṛjad bhairavaṃ ravam  Ram
sā nadantī mahānādaṃ javāc chūrpaṇakhā punaḥ
upagamya kharaṃ sā tu kiṃcit saṃśuṣkaśoṇitā
papāta punar evārtā saniryāseva vallarī  Ram
nipātitān prekṣya raṇe tu rākṣasān pradhāvitā śūrpaṇakhā punas tataḥ
vadhaṃ ca teṣāṃ nikhilena rakṣasāṃ śaśaṃsa sarvaṃ bhaginī kharasya sā  Ram
sa punaḥ patitāṃ dṛṣṭvā krodhāc chūrpaṇakhāṃ kharaḥ
uvāca vyaktayā vācā tām anarthārtham āgatām  Ram
mayā tv idānīṃ śūrās te rākṣasā rudhirāśanāḥ
tvatpriyārthaṃ vinirdiṣṭāḥ kimarthaṃ rudyate punaḥ  Ram
bhaktāś caivānuraktāś ca hitāś ca mama nityaśaḥ
ghnanto 'pi na nihantavyā na na kuryur vaco mama  Ram
kim etac chrotum icchāmi kāraṇaṃ yatkṛte punaḥ
hā nātheti vinardantī sarpavad veṣṭase kṣitau  Ram
anāthavad vilapasi kiṃ nu nāthe mayi sthite
uttiṣṭhottiṣṭha mā bhaiṣīr vaiklavyaṃ tyajyatām iha  Ram
ity evam uktā durdharṣā khareṇa parisāntvitā
vimṛjya nayane sāsre kharaṃ bhrātaram abravīt  Ram
preṣitāś ca tvayā śūrā rākṣasās te caturdaśa
nihantuṃ rāghavaṃ ghorā matpriyārthaṃ salakṣmaṇam  Ram
te tu rāmeṇa sāmarṣāḥ śūlapaṭṭiśapāṇayaḥ
samare nihatāḥ sarve sāyakair marmabhedibhiḥ  Ram
tān bhūmau patitān dṛṣṭvā kṣaṇenaiva mahābalān
rāmasya ca mahat karma mahāṃs trāso 'bhavan mama  Ram
sāsmi bhītā samudvignā viṣaṇṇā ca niśācara
śaraṇaṃ tvāṃ punaḥ prāptā sarvato bhayadarśinī  Ram
viṣādanakrādhyuṣite paritrāsormimālini
kiṃ māṃ na trāyase magnāṃ vipule śokasāgare  Ram
ete ca nihatā bhūmau rāmeṇa niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
ye ca me padavīṃ prāptā rākṣasāḥ piśitāśanāḥ  Ram
mayi te yady anukrośo yadi rakṣaḥsu teṣu ca
rāmeṇa yadi śaktis te tejo vāsti niśācara
daṇḍakāraṇyanilayaṃ jahi rākṣasakaṇṭakam  Ram
yadi rāmaṃ mamāmitram adya tvaṃ na vadhiṣyasi
tava caivāgrataḥ prāṇāṃs tyakṣyāmi nirapatrapā  Ram
buddhyāham anupaśyāmi na tvaṃ rāmasya saṃyuge
sthātuṃ pratimukhe śaktaḥ sacāpasya mahāraṇe  Ram
śūramānī na śūras tvaṃ mithyāropitavikramaḥ
mānuṣau yan na śaknoṣi hantuṃ tau rāmalakṣmaṇau  Ram
apayāhi janasthānāt tvaritaḥ sahabāndhavaḥ
niḥsattvasyālpavīryasya vāsas te kīdṛśas tv iha  Ram
rāmatejo'bhibhūto hi tvaṃ kṣipraṃ vinaśiṣyasi
sa hi tejaḥsamāyukto rāmo daśarathātmajaḥ
bhrātā cāsya mahāvīryo yena cāsmi virūpitā  Ram
evam ādharṣitaḥ śūraḥ śūrpaṇakhyā kharas tadā
uvāca rakṣasāṃ madhye kharaḥ kharataraṃ vacaḥ  Ram
tavāpamānaprabhavaḥ krodho 'yam atulo mama
na śakyate dhārayituṃ lavaṇāmbha ivotthitam  Ram
na rāmaṃ gaṇaye vīryān mānuṣaṃ kṣīṇajīvitam
ātmā duścaritaiḥ prāṇān hato yo 'dya vimokṣyati  Ram
bāṣpaḥ saṃhriyatām eṣa sambhramaś ca vimucyatām
ahaṃ rāmaṃ saha bhrātrā nayāmi yamasādanam  Ram
paraśvadhahatasyādya mandaprāṇasya bhūtale
rāmasya rudhiraṃ raktam uṣṇaṃ pāsyasi rākṣasi  Ram
sā prahṛṣṭā vacaḥ śrutvā kharasya vadanāc cyutam
praśaśaṃsa punar maurkhyād bhrātaraṃ rakṣasāṃ varam  Ram
tayā paruṣitaḥ pūrvaṃ punar eva praśaṃsitaḥ
abravīd dūṣaṇaṃ nāma kharaḥ senāpatiṃ tadā  Ram
caturdaśa sahasrāṇi mama cittānuvartinām
rakṣasāṃ bhīmavegānāṃ samareṣv anivartinām  Ram
nīlajīmūtavarṇānāṃ ghorāṇāṃ krūrakarmaṇām
lokahiṃsāvihārāṇāṃ balinām ugratejasām  Ram
teṣāṃ śārdūladarpāṇāṃ mahāsyānāṃ mahaujasām
sarvodyogam udīrṇānāṃ rakṣasāṃ saumya kāraya  Ram
upasthāpaya me kṣipraṃ rathaṃ saumya dhanūṃṣi ca
śarāṃś ca citrān khaḍgāṃś ca śaktīś ca vividhāḥ śitāḥ  Ram
agre niryātum icchāmi paulastyānāṃ mahātmanām
vadhārthaṃ durvinītasya rāmasya raṇakovidaḥ  Ram
iti tasya bruvāṇasya sūryavarṇaṃ mahāratham
sadaśvaiḥ śabalair yuktam ācacakṣe 'tha dūṣaṇaḥ  Ram
taṃ meruśikharākāraṃ taptakāñcanabhūṣaṇam
hemacakram asaṃbādhaṃ vaidūryamayakūbaram  Ram
matsyaiḥ puṣpair drumaiḥ śailaiś candrasūryaiś ca kāñcanaiḥ
māṅgalyaiḥ pakṣisaṃghaiś ca tārābhiś ca samāvṛtam  Ram
dhvajanistriṃśasampannaṃ kiṅkiṇīkavibhūṣitam
sadaśvayuktaṃ so 'marṣād āruroha rathaṃ kharaḥ  Ram
niśāmya taṃ rathagataṃ rākṣasā bhīmavikramāḥ
tasthuḥ saṃparivāryainaṃ dūṣaṇaṃ ca mahābalam  Ram
kharas tu tān maheṣvāsān ghoracarmāyudhadhvajān
niryātety abravīd dṛṣṭvā rathasthaḥ sarvarākṣasān  Ram
tatas tad rākṣasaṃ sainyaṃ ghoracarmāyudhadhvajam
nirjagāma janasthānān mahānādaṃ mahājavam  Ram
mudgaraiḥ paṭṭiśaiḥ śūlaiḥ sutīkṣṇaiś ca paraśvadhaiḥ
khaḍgaiś cakraiś ca hastasthair bhrājamānaiś ca tomaraiḥ  Ram
śaktibhiḥ parighair ghorair atimātraiś ca kārmukaiḥ
gadāsimusalair vajrair gṛhītair bhīmadarśanaiḥ  Ram
rākṣasānāṃ sughorāṇāṃ sahasrāṇi caturdaśa
niryātāni janasthānāt kharacittānuvartinām  Ram
tāṃs tv abhidravato dṛṣṭvā rākṣasān bhīmavikramān
kharasyāpi rathaḥ kiṃcij jagāma tadanantaram  Ram
tatas tāñ śabalān aśvāṃs taptakāñcanabhūṣitān
kharasya matam ājñāya sārathiḥ samacodayat  Ram
sa codito rathaḥ śīghraṃ kharasya ripughātinaḥ
śabdenāpūrayām āsa diśaḥ pratidiśas tathā  Ram
pravṛddhamanyus tu kharaḥ kharasvano ripor vadhārthaṃ tvarito yathāntakaḥ
acūcudat sārathim unnadan punar mahābalo megha ivāśmavarṣavān  Ram
tat prayātaṃ balaṃ ghoram aśivaṃ śoṇitodakam
abhyavarṣan mahāmeghas tumulo gardabhāruṇaḥ  Ram
nipetus turagās tasya rathayuktā mahājavāḥ
same puṣpacite deśe rājamārge yadṛcchayā  Ram
śyāmaṃ rudhiraparyantaṃ babhūva pariveṣaṇam
alātacakrapratimaṃ pratigṛhya divākaram  Ram
tato dhvajam upāgamya hemadaṇḍaṃ samucchritam
samākramya mahākāyas tasthau gṛdhraḥ sudāruṇaḥ  Ram
janasthānasamīpe ca samākramya kharasvanāḥ
visvarān vividhāṃś cakrur māṃsādā mṛgapakṣiṇaḥ  Ram
vyājahruś ca pradīptāyāṃ diśi vai bhairavasvanam
aśivaṃ yātudhānānāṃ śivā ghorā mahāsvanāḥ  Ram
prabhinnagirisaṃkāśās toyaśoṣitadhāriṇaḥ
ākāśaṃ tad anākāśaṃ cakrur bhīmā balāhakāḥ  Ram
babhūva timiraṃ ghoram uddhataṃ romaharṣaṇam
diśo vā vidiśo vāpi suvyaktaṃ na cakāśire  Ram
kṣatajārdrasavarṇābhā saṃdhyākālaṃ vinā babhau
kharasyābhimukhaṃ nedus tadā ghorā mṛgāḥ khagāḥ  Ram
nityāśivakarā yuddhe śivā ghoranidarśanāḥ
nedur balasyābhimukhaṃ jvālodgāribhir ānanaiḥ  Ram
kabandhaḥ parighābhāso dṛśyate bhāskarāntike
jagrāha sūryaṃ svarbhānur aparvaṇi mahāgrahaḥ  Ram
pravāti mārutaḥ śīghraṃ niṣprabho 'bhūd divākaraḥ
utpetuś ca vinā rātriṃ tārāḥ khadyotasaprabhāḥ  Ram
saṃlīnamīnavihagā nalinyaḥ puṣpapaṅkajāḥ
tasmin kṣaṇe babhūvuś ca vinā puṣpaphalair drumāḥ  Ram
uddhūtaś ca vinā vātaṃ reṇur jaladharāruṇaḥ
vīcīkūcīti vāśyanto babhūvus tatra sārikāḥ  Ram
ulkāś cāpi sanirghoṣā nipetur ghoradarśanāḥ
pracacāla mahī cāpi saśailavanakānanā  Ram
kharasya ca rathasthasya nardamānasya dhīmataḥ
prākampata bhujaḥ savyaḥ kharaś cāsyāvasajjata  Ram
sāsrā saṃpadyate dṛṣṭiḥ paśyamānasya sarvataḥ
lalāṭe ca rujā jātā na ca mohān nyavartata  Ram
tān samīkṣya mahotpātān utthitān romaharṣaṇān
abravīd rākṣasān sarvān prahasan sa kharas tadā  Ram
mahotpātān imān sarvān utthitān ghoradarśanān
na cintayāmy ahaṃ vīryād balavān durbalān iva  Ram
tārā api śarais tīkṣṇaiḥ pātayeyaṃ nabhastalāt
mṛtyuṃ maraṇadharmeṇa saṃkruddho yojayāmy aham  Ram
rāghavaṃ taṃ balotsiktaṃ bhrātaraṃ cāpi lakṣmaṇam
ahatvā sāyakais tīkṣṇair nopāvartitum utsahe  Ram
sakāmā bhaginī me 'stu pītvā tu rudhiraṃ tayoḥ
yannimittaṃ tu rāmasya lakṣmaṇasya viparyayaḥ  Ram
na kvacit prāptapūrvo me saṃyugeṣu parājayaḥ
yuṣmākam etat pratyakṣaṃ nānṛtaṃ kathayāmy aham  Ram
devarājam api kruddho mattairāvatayāyinam
vajrahastaṃ raṇe hanyāṃ kiṃ punas tau ca mānuṣau  Ram
sā tasya garjitaṃ śrutvā rākṣasasya mahācamūḥ
praharṣam atulaṃ lebhe mṛtyupāśāvapāśitā  Ram
sameyuś ca mahātmāno yuddhadarśanakāṅkṣiṇaḥ
ṛṣayo devagandharvāḥ siddhāś ca saha cāraṇaiḥ  Ram
sametya cocuḥ sahitās te 'nyonyaṃ puṇyakarmaṇaḥ
svasti gobrāhmaṇebhyo 'stu lokānāṃ ye ca saṃmatāḥ  Ram
jayatāṃ rāghavo yuddhe paulastyān rajanīcarān
cakrahasto yathā yuddhe sarvān asurapuṃgavān  Ram
etac cānyac ca bahuśo bruvāṇāḥ paramarṣayaḥ
dadṛśur vāhinīṃ teṣāṃ rākṣasānāṃ gatāyuṣām  Ram
rathena tu kharo vegāt sainyasyāgrād viniḥsṛtaḥ
taṃ dṛṣṭvā rākṣasaṃ bhūyo rākṣasāś ca viniḥsṛtāḥ  Ram
śyenagāmī pṛthugrīvo yajñaśatrur vihaṃgamaḥ
durjayaḥ karavīrākṣaḥ paruṣaḥ kālakārmukaḥ  Ram
meghamālī mahāmālī sarpāsyo rudhirāśanaḥ
dvādaśaite mahāvīryāḥ pratasthur abhitaḥ kharam  Ram
mahākapālaḥ sthūlākṣaḥ pramāthī triśirās tathā
catvāra ete senāgryā dūṣaṇaṃ pṛṣṭhato 'nvayuḥ  Ram
sā bhīmavegā samarābhikāmā sudāruṇā rākṣasavīrasenā
tau rājaputrau sahasābhyupetā mālā grahāṇām iva candrasūryau  Ram
āśramaṃ pratiyāte tu khare kharaparākrame
tān evautpātikān rāmaḥ saha bhrātrā dadarśa ha  Ram
tān utpātān mahāghorān utthitān romaharṣaṇān
prajānām ahitān dṛṣṭvā vākyaṃ lakṣmaṇam abravīt  Ram
imān paśya mahābāho sarvabhūtāpahāriṇaḥ
samutthitān mahotpātān saṃhartuṃ sarvarākṣasān  Ram
amī rudhiradhārās tu visṛjantaḥ kharasvanān
vyomni meghā vivartante paruṣā gardabhāruṇāḥ  Ram
sadhūmāś ca śarāḥ sarve mama yuddhābhinandinaḥ
rukmapṛṣṭhāni cāpāni viveṣṭante ca lakṣmaṇa  Ram
yādṛśā iha kūjanti pakṣiṇo vanacāriṇaḥ
agrato no bhayaṃ prāptaṃ saṃśayo jīvitasya ca  Ram
samprahāras tu sumahān bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ
ayam ākhyāti me bāhuḥ sphuramāṇo muhur muhuḥ  Ram
saṃnikarṣe tu naḥ śūra jayaṃ śatroḥ parājayam
suprabhaṃ ca prasannaṃ ca tava vaktraṃ hi lakṣyate  Ram
udyatānāṃ hi yuddhārthaṃ yeṣāṃ bhavati lakṣmaṇaḥ
niṣprabhaṃ vadanaṃ teṣāṃ bhavaty āyuḥparikṣayaḥ  Ram
anāgatavidhānaṃ tu kartavyaṃ śubham icchatā
āpadaṃ śaṅkamānena puruṣeṇa vipaścitā  Ram
tasmād gṛhītvā vaidehīṃ śarapāṇir dhanurdharaḥ
guhām āśraya śailasya durgāṃ pādapasaṃkulām  Ram
pratikūlitum icchāmi na hi vākyam idaṃ tvayā
śāpito mama pādābhyāṃ gamyatāṃ vatsa māciram  Ram
evam uktas tu rāmeṇa lakṣmaṇaḥ saha sītayā
śarān ādāya cāpaṃ ca guhāṃ durgāṃ samāśrayat  Ram
tasmin praviṣṭe tu guhāṃ lakṣmaṇe saha sītayā
hanta niryuktam ity uktvā rāmaḥ kavacam āviśat  Ram
sa tenāgninikāśena kavacena vibhūṣitaḥ
babhūva rāmas timire vidhūmo 'gnir ivotthitaḥ  Ram
sa cāpam udyamya mahac charān ādāya vīryavān
babhūvāvasthitas tatra jyāsvanaiḥ pūrayan diśaḥ  Ram
tato devāḥ sagandharvāḥ siddhāś ca saha cāraṇaiḥ
ūcuḥ paramasaṃtrastā guhyakāś ca parasparam  Ram
caturdaśa sahasrāṇi rakṣasāṃ bhīmakarmaṇām
ekaś ca rāmo dharmātmā kathaṃ yuddhaṃ bhaviṣyati  Ram
tato gambhīranirhrādaṃ ghoravarmāyudhadhvajam
anīkaṃ yātudhānānāṃ samantāt pratyadṛśyata  Ram
siṃhanādaṃ visṛjatām anyonyam abhigarjatām
cāpāni visphārayatāṃ jṛmbhatāṃ cāpy abhīkṣṇaśaḥ  Ram
vipraghuṣṭasvanānāṃ ca dundubhīṃś cāpi nighnatām
teṣāṃ sutumulaḥ śabdaḥ pūrayāmāsa tad vanam  Ram
tena śabdena vitrastāḥ śvāpadā vanacāriṇaḥ
dudruvur yatra niḥśabdaṃ pṛṣṭhato nāvalokayan  Ram
tat tv anīkaṃ mahāvegaṃ rāmaṃ samupasarpata
dhṛtanānāpraharaṇaṃ gambhīraṃ sāgaropamam  Ram
rāmo 'pi cārayaṃś cakṣuḥ sarvato raṇapaṇḍitaḥ
dadarśa kharasainyaṃ tad yuddhābhimukham udyatam  Ram
vitatya ca dhanur bhīmaṃ tūṇyāś coddhṛtya sāyakān
krodham āhārayat tīvraṃ vadhārthaṃ sarvarakṣasām  Ram
duṣprekṣyaḥ so 'bhavat kruddho yugāntāgnir iva jvalan
taṃ dṛṣṭvā tejasāviṣṭaṃ prāvyathan vanadevatāḥ  Ram
tasya kruddhasya rūpaṃ tu rāmasya dadṛśe tadā
dakṣasyeva kratuṃ hantum udyatasya pinākinaḥ  Ram
avaṣṭabdhadhanuṃ rāmaṃ kruddhaṃ ca ripughātinam
dadarśāśramam āgamya kharaḥ saha puraḥsaraiḥ  Ram
taṃ dṛṣṭvā saguṇaṃ cāpam udyamya kharaniḥsvanam
rāmasyābhimukhaṃ sūtaṃ codyatām ity acodayat  Ram
sa kharasyājñayā sūtas turagān samacodayat
yatra rāmo mahābāhur eko dhunvan dhanuḥ sthitaḥ  Ram
taṃ tu niṣpatitaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve te rajanīcarāḥ
nardamānā mahānādaṃ sacivāḥ paryavārayan  Ram
sa teṣāṃ yātudhānānāṃ madhye rato gataḥ kharaḥ
babhūva madhye tārāṇāṃ lohitāṅga ivoditaḥ  Ram
tatas taṃ bhīmadhanvānaṃ kruddhāḥ sarve niśācarāḥ
rāmaṃ nānāvidhaiḥ śastrair abhyavarṣanta durjayam  Ram
mudgarair āyasaiḥ śūlaiḥ prāsaiḥ khaḍgaiḥ paraśvadhaiḥ
rākṣasāḥ samare rāmaṃ nijaghnū roṣatatparāḥ  Ram
te balāhakasaṃkāśā mahānādā mahābalāḥ
abhyadhāvanta kākutsthaṃ rāmaṃ yuddhe jighāṃsavaḥ  Ram
te rāme śaravarṣāṇi vyasṛjan rakṣasāṃ guṇāḥ
śailendram iva dhārābhir varṣamāṇā balāhakāḥ  Ram
sa taiḥ parivṛto ghorai rāghavo rakṣasāṃ gaṇaiḥ
tithiṣv iva mahādevo vṛtaḥ pāriṣadāṃ gaṇaiḥ  Ram
tāni muktāni śastrāṇi yātudhānaiḥ sa rāghavaḥ
pratijagrāha viśikhair nadyoghān iva sāgaraḥ  Ram
sa taiḥ praharaṇair ghorair bhinnagātro na vivyathe
rāmaḥ pradīptair bahubhir vajrair iva mahācalaḥ  Ram
sa viddhaḥ kṣatajādigdhaḥ sarvagātreṣu rāghavaḥ
babhūva rāmaḥ saṃdhyābhrair divākara ivāvṛtaḥ  Ram
viṣedur devagandharvāḥ siddhāś ca paramarṣayaḥ
ekaṃ sahasrair bahubhis tadā dṛṣṭvā samāvṛtam  Ram
tato rāmaḥ susaṃkruddho maṇḍalīkṛtakārmukaḥ
sasarja niśitān bāṇāñ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ  Ram
durāvārān durviṣahān kālapāśopamān raṇe
mumoca līlayā rāmaḥ kaṅkapattrān ajihmagān  Ram
te śarāḥ śatrusainyeṣu muktā rāmeṇa līlayā
ādadū rakṣasāṃ prāṇān pāśāḥ kālakṛtā iva  Ram
bhittvā rākṣasadehāṃs tāṃs te śarā rudhirāplutāḥ
antarikṣagatā rejur dīptāgnisamatejasaḥ  Ram
asaṃkhyeyās tu rāmasya sāyakāś cāpamaṇḍalāt
viniṣpetur atīvogrā rakṣaḥprāṇāpahāriṇaḥ  Ram
tair dhanūṃṣi dhvajāgrāṇi varmāṇi ca śirāṃsi ca
bahūn sahastābharaṇān ūrūn karikaropamān  Ram
tato nālīkanārācais tīkṣṇāgraiś ca vikarṇibhiḥ
bhīmam ārtasvaraṃ cakrur bhidyamānā niśācarāḥ  Ram
tat sainyaṃ niśitair bāṇair arditaṃ marmabhedibhiḥ
rāmeṇa na sukhaṃ lebhe śuṣkaṃ vanam ivāgninā  Ram
kecid bhīmabalāḥ śūrāḥ śūlān khaḍgān paraśvadhān
cikṣipuḥ paramakruddhā rāmāya rajanīcarāḥ  Ram
tāni bāṇair mahābāhuḥ śastrāṇy āvārya rāghavaḥ
jahāra samare prāṇāṃś cicheda ca śirodharān  Ram
avaśiṣṭāś ca ye tatra viṣaṇṇāś ca niśācarāḥ
kharam evābhyadhāvanta śaraṇārthaṃ śarārditāḥ  Ram
tān sarvān punar ādāya samāśvāsya ca dūṣaṇaḥ
abhyadhāvata kākutsthaṃ kruddho rudram ivāntakaḥ  Ram
nivṛttās tu punaḥ sarve dūṣaṇāśrayanirbhayāḥ
rāmam evābhyadhāvanta sālatālaśilāyudhāḥ  Ram
tad babhūvādbhutaṃ yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ romaharṣaṇam
rāmasyāsya mahāghoraṃ punas teṣāṃ ca rakṣasām  Ram
tad drumāṇāṃ śilānāṃ ca varṣaṃ prāṇaharaṃ mahat
pratijagrāha dharmātmā rāghavas tīkṣṇasāyakaiḥ  Ram
pratigṛhya ca tad varaṃ nimīlita ivarṣabhaḥ
rāmaḥ krodhaṃ paraṃ bheje vadhārthaṃ sarvarakṣasām  Ram
tataḥ krodhasamāviṣṭaḥ pradīpta iva tejasā
śarair abhyakirat sainyaṃ sarvataḥ sahadūṣaṇam  Ram
tataḥ senāpatiḥ kruddho dūṣaṇaḥ śatrudūṣaṇaḥ
jagrāha giriśṛṅgābhaṃ parighaṃ romaharṣaṇam  Ram
veṣṭitaṃ kāñcanaiḥ paṭṭair devasainyābhimardanam
āyasaiḥ śaṅkubhis tīkṣṇaiḥ kīrṇaṃ paravasokṣitam  Ram
vajrāśanisamasparśaṃ paragopuradāraṇam
taṃ mahoragasaṃkāśaṃ pragṛhya parighaṃ raṇe
dūṣaṇo 'bhyapatad rāmaṃ krūrakarmā niśācaraḥ  Ram
tasyābhipatamānasya dūṣaṇasya sa rāghavaḥ
dvābhyāṃ śarābhyāṃ cicheda sahastābharaṇau bhujau  Ram
bhraṣṭas tasya mahākāyaḥ papāta raṇamūrdhani
parighaś chinnahastasya śakradhvaja ivāgrataḥ  Ram
sa karābhyāṃ vikīrṇābhyāṃ papāta bhuvi dūṣaṇaḥ
viṣāṇābhyāṃ viśīrṇābhyāṃ manasvīva mahāgajaḥ  Ram
dṛṣṭvā taṃ patitaṃ bhūmau dūṣaṇaṃ nihataṃ raṇe
sādhu sādhv iti kākutsthaṃ sarvabhūtāny apūjayan  Ram
etasminn antare kruddhās trayaḥ senāgrayāyinaḥ
saṃhatyābhyadravan rāmaṃ mṛtyupāśāvapāśitāḥ
mahākapālaḥ sthūlākṣaḥ pramāthī ca mahābalaḥ  Ram
mahākapālo vipulaṃ śūlam udyamya rākṣasaḥ
sthūlākṣaḥ paṭṭiśaṃ gṛhya pramāthī ca paraśvadham  Ram
dṛṣṭvaivāpatatas tāṃs tu rāghavaḥ sāyakaiḥ śitaiḥ
tīkṣṇāgraiḥ pratijagrāha samprāptān atithīn iva  Ram
mahākapālasya śiraś cicheda raghunandanaḥ
asaṃkhyeyais tu bāṇaughaiḥ pramamātha pramāthinam  Ram
sthūlākṣasyākṣiṇī tīkṣṇaiḥ pūrayāmāsa sāyakaiḥ
sa papāta hato bhūmau viṭapīva mahādrumaḥ  Ram
tataḥ pāvakasaṃkāśair hemavajravibhūṣitaiḥ
jaghanaśeṣaṃ tejasvī tasya sainyasya sāyakaiḥ  Ram
te rukmapuṅkhā viśikhāḥ sadhūmā iva pāvakāḥ
nijaghnus tāni rakṣāṃsi vajrā iva mahādrumān  Ram
rakṣasāṃ tu śataṃ rāmaḥ śatenaikena karṇinā
sahasraṃ ca sahasreṇa jaghāna raṇamūrdhani  Ram
tair bhinnavarmābharaṇāś chinnabhinnaśarāsanāḥ
nipetuḥ śoṇitādigdhā dharaṇyāṃ rajanīcarāḥ  Ram
tair muktakeśaiḥ samare patitaiḥ śoṇitokṣitaiḥ
āstīrṇā vasudhā kṛtsnā mahāvediḥ kuśair iva  Ram
kṣaṇena tu mahāghoraṃ vanaṃ nihatarākṣasam
babhūva nirayaprakhyaṃ māṃsaśoṇitakardamam  Ram
caturdaśa sahasrāṇi rakṣasāṃ bhīmakarmaṇām
hatāny ekena rāmeṇa mānuṣeṇa padātinā  Ram
tasya sainyasya sarvasya kharaḥ śeṣo mahārathaḥ
rākṣasas triśirāś caiva rāmaś ca ripusūdanaḥ  Ram
tatas tu tad bhīmabalaṃ mahāhave samīkṣya rāmeṇa hataṃ balīyasā
rathena rāmaṃ mahatā kharas tataḥ samāsasādendra ivodyatāśaniḥ  Ram
kharaṃ tu rāmābhimukhaṃ prayāntaṃ vāhinīpatiḥ
rākṣasas triśirā nāma saṃnipatyedam abravīt  Ram
māṃ niyojaya vikrānta saṃnivartasva sāhasāt
paśya rāmaṃ mahābāhuṃ saṃyuge vinipātitam  Ram
pratijānāmi te satyam āyudhaṃ cāham ālabhe
yathā rāmaṃ vadhiṣyāmi vadhārhaṃ sarvarakṣasām  Ram
ahaṃ vāsya raṇe mṛtyur eṣa vā samare mama
vinivartya raṇotsāhaṃ muhūrtaṃ prāśniko bhava  Ram
prahṛṣṭo vā hate rāme janasthānaṃ prayāsyasi
mayi vā nihate rāmaṃ saṃyugāyopayāsyasi  Ram
kharas triśirasā tena mṛtyulobhāt prasāditaḥ
gaccha yudhyety anujñāto rāghavābhimukho yayau  Ram
triśirāś ca rathenaiva vājiyuktena bhāsvatā
abhyadravad raṇe rāmaṃ triśṛṅga iva parvataḥ  Ram
śaradhārāsamūhān sa mahāmegha ivotsṛjan
vyasṛjat sadṛśaṃ nādaṃ jalārdrasyeva dundubheḥ  Ram
āgacchantaṃ triśirasaṃ rākṣasaṃ prekṣya rāghavaḥ
dhanuṣā pratijagrāha vidhunvan sāyakāñ śitān  Ram
sa samprahāras tumulo rāmatriśirasor mahān
babhūvātīva balinoḥ siṃhakuñjarayor iva  Ram
tatas triśirasā bāṇair lalāṭe tāḍitas tribhiḥ
amarṣī kupito rāmaḥ saṃrabdham idam abravīt  Ram
aho vikramaśūrasya rākṣasasyedṛśaṃ balam
puṣpair iva śarair yasya lalāṭe 'smi parikṣataḥ
mamāpi pratigṛhṇīṣva śarāṃś cāpaguṇacyutān  Ram
evam uktvā tu saṃrabdhaḥ śarān āśīviṣopamān
triśirovakṣasi kruddho nijaghāna caturdaśa  Ram
caturbhis turagān asya śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
nyapātayata tejasvī caturas tasya vājinaḥ  Ram
aṣṭabhiḥ sāyakaiḥ sūtaṃ rathopasthe nyapātayat
rāmaś cicheda bāṇena dhvajaṃ cāsya samucchritam  Ram
tato hatarathāt tasmād utpatantaṃ niśācaram
bibheda rāmas taṃ bāṇair hṛdaye so 'bhavaj jaḍaḥ  Ram
sāyakaiś cāprameyātmā sāmarṣas tasya rakṣasaḥ
śirāṃsy apātayat trīṇi vegavadbhis tribhiḥ śataiḥ  Ram
sa bhūmau śoṇitodgārī rāmabāṇābhipīḍitaḥ
nyapatat patitaiḥ pūrvaṃ svaśirobhir niśācaraḥ  Ram
hataśeṣās tato bhagnā rākṣasāḥ kharasaṃśrayāḥ
dravanti sma na tiṣṭhanti vyāghratrastā mṛgā iva  Ram
tān kharo dravato dṛṣṭvā nivartya ruṣitaḥ svayam
rāmam evābhidudrāva rāhuś candramasaṃ yathā  Ram
nihataṃ dūṣaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā raṇe triśirasā saha
kharasyāpy abhavat trāso dṛṣṭvā rāmasya vikramam  Ram
sa dṛṣṭvā rākṣasaṃ sainyam aviṣahyaṃ mahābalam
hatam ekena rāmeṇa dūṣaṇas triśirā api  Ram
tad balaṃ hatabhūyiṣṭhaṃ vimanāḥ prekṣya rākṣasaḥ
āsasāda kharo rāmaṃ namucir vāsavaṃ yathā  Ram
vikṛṣya balavac cāpaṃ nārācān raktabhojanān
kharaś cikṣepa rāmāya kruddhān āśīviṣān iva  Ram
jyāṃ vidhunvan subahuśaḥ śikṣayāstrāṇi darśayan
cacāra samare mārgāñ śarai rathagataḥ kharaḥ  Ram
sa sarvāś ca diśo bāṇaiḥ pradiśaś ca mahārathaḥ
pūrayāmāsa taṃ dṛṣṭvā rāmo 'pi sumahad dhanuḥ  Ram
sa sāyakair durviṣahaiḥ sasphuliṅgair ivāgnibhiḥ
nabhaś cakārāvivaraṃ parjanya iva vṛṣṭibhiḥ  Ram
tad babhūva śitair bāṇaiḥ khararāmavisarjitaiḥ
paryākāśam anākāśaṃ sarvataḥ śarasaṃkulam  Ram
śarajālāvṛtaḥ sūryo na tadā sma prakāśate
anyonyavadhasaṃrambhād ubhayoḥ samprayudhyatoḥ  Ram
tato nālīkanārācais tīkṣṇāgraiś ca vikarṇibhiḥ
ājaghāna raṇe rāmaṃ totrair iva mahādvipam  Ram
taṃ rathasthaṃ dhanuṣpāṇiṃ rākṣasaṃ paryavasthitam
dadṛśuḥ sarvabhūtāni pāśahastam ivāntakam  Ram
taṃ siṃham iva vikrāntaṃ siṃhavikrāntagāminam
dṛṣṭvā nodvijate rāmaḥ siṃhaḥ kṣudramṛgaṃ yathā  Ram
tataḥ sūryanikāśena rathena mahatā kharaḥ
āsasāda raṇe rāmaṃ pataṃga iva pāvakam  Ram
tato 'sya saśaraṃ cāpaṃ muṣṭideśe mahātmanaḥ
kharaś cicheda rāmasya darśayan pāṇilāghavam  Ram
sa punas tv aparān sapta śarān ādāya varmaṇi
nijaghāna raṇe kruddhaḥ śakrāśanisamaprabhān  Ram
tatas tat prahataṃ bāṇaiḥ kharamuktaiḥ suparvabhiḥ
papāta kavacaṃ bhūmau rāmasyādityavarcasaḥ  Ram
sa śarair arpitaḥ kruddhaḥ sarvagātreṣu rāghavaḥ
rarāja samare rāmo vidhūmo 'gnir iva jvalan  Ram
tato gambhīranirhrādaṃ rāmaḥ śatrunibarhaṇaḥ
cakārāntāya sa ripoḥ sajyam anyan mahad dhanuḥ  Ram
sumahad vaiṣṇavaṃ yat tad atisṛṣṭaṃ maharṣiṇā
varaṃ tad dhanur udyamya kharaṃ samabhidhāvata  Ram
tataḥ kanakapuṅkhais tu śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
cicheda rāmaḥ saṃkruddhaḥ kharasya samare dhvajam  Ram
sa darśanīyo bahudhā vicchinnaḥ kāñcano dhvajaḥ
jagāma dharaṇīṃ sūryo devatānām ivājñayā  Ram
taṃ caturbhiḥ kharaḥ kruddho rāmaṃ gātreṣu mārgaṇaiḥ
vivyādha hṛdi marmajño mātaṃgam iva tomaraiḥ  Ram
sa rāmo bahubhir bāṇaiḥ kharakārmukaniḥsṛtaiḥ
viddho rudhirasiktāṅgo babhūva ruṣito bhṛśam  Ram
sa dhanur dhanvināṃ śreṣṭhaḥ pragṛhya paramāhave
mumoca parameṣvāsaḥ ṣaṭ śarān abhilakṣitān  Ram
śirasy ekena bāṇena dvābhyāṃ bāhvor athārpayat
tribhiś candrārdhavaktraiś ca vakṣasy abhijaghāna ha  Ram
tataḥ paścān mahātejā nārācān bhāskaropamān
jighāṃsū rākṣasaṃ kruddhas trayodaśa śilāśitān  Ram
tato 'sya yugam ekena caturbhiś caturo hayān
ṣaṣṭhena ca śiraḥ saṃkhye cicheda kharasāratheḥ  Ram
tribhis triveṇuṃ balavān dvābhyām akṣaṃ mahābalaḥ
dvādaśena tu bāṇena kharasya saśaraṃ dhanuḥ  Ram
chittvā vajranikāśena rāghavaḥ prahasann iva
trayodaśenendrasamo bibheda samare kharam  Ram
prabhagnadhanvā viratho hatāśvo hatasārathiḥ
gadāpāṇir avaplutya tasthau bhūmau kharas tadā  Ram
tat karma rāmasya mahārathasya sametya devāś ca maharṣayaś ca
apūjayan prāñjalayaḥ prahṛṣṭās tadā vimānāgragatāḥ sametāḥ  Ram
kharaṃ tu virathaṃ rāmo gadāpāṇim avasthitam
mṛdupūrvaṃ mahātejāḥ paruṣaṃ vākyam abravīt  Ram
gajāśvarathasambādhe bale mahati tiṣṭhatā
kṛtaṃ sudāruṇaṃ karma sarvalokajugupsitam  Ram
udvejanīyo bhūtānāṃ nṛśaṃsaḥ pāpakarmakṛt
trayāṇām api lokānām īśvaro 'pi na tiṣṭhati  Ram
karma lokaviruddhaṃ tu kurvāṇaṃ kṣaṇadācara
tīkṣṇaṃ sarvajano hanti sarpaṃ duṣṭam ivāgatam  Ram
lobhāt pāpāni kurvāṇaḥ kāmād vā yo na budhyate
bhraṣṭaḥ paśyati tasyāntaṃ brāhmaṇī karakād iva  Ram
vasato daṇḍakāraṇye tāpasān dharmacāriṇaḥ
kiṃ nu hatvā mahābhāgān phalaṃ prāpsyasi rākṣasa  Ram
na ciraṃ pāpakarmāṇaḥ krūrā lokajugupsitāḥ
aiśvaryaṃ prāpya tiṣṭhanti śīrṇamūlā iva drumāḥ  Ram
avaśyaṃ labhate kartā phalaṃ pāpasya karmaṇaḥ
ghoraṃ paryāgate kāle drumaḥ puṣpam ivārtavam  Ram
nacirāt prāpyate loke pāpānāṃ karmaṇāṃ phalam
saviṣāṇām ivānnānāṃ bhuktānāṃ kṣaṇadācara  Ram
pāpam ācaratāṃ ghoraṃ lokasyāpriyam icchatām
aham āsādito rājā prāṇān hantuṃ niśācara  Ram
adya hi tvāṃ mayā muktāḥ śarāḥ kāñcanabhūṣaṇāḥ
vidārya nipatiṣyanti valmīkam iva pannagāḥ  Ram
ye tvayā daṇḍakāraṇye bhakṣitā dharmacāriṇaḥ
tān adya nihataḥ saṃkhye sasainyo 'nugamiṣyasi  Ram
adya tvāṃ nihataṃ bāṇaiḥ paśyantu paramarṣayaḥ
nirayasthaṃ vimānasthā ye tvayā hiṃsitāḥ purā  Ram
prahara tvaṃ yathākāmaṃ kuru yatnaṃ kulādhama
adya te pātayiṣyāmi śiras tālaphalaṃ yathā  Ram
evam uktas tu rāmeṇa kruddhaḥ saṃraktalocanaḥ
pratyuvāca tato rāmaṃ prahasan krodhamūrchitaḥ  Ram
prākṛtān rākṣasān hatvā yuddhe daśarathātmaja
ātmanā katham ātmānam apraśasyaṃ praśaṃsasi  Ram
vikrāntā balavanto vā ye bhavanti nararṣabhāḥ
kathayanti na te kiṃcit tejasā svena garvitāḥ  Ram
prākṛtās tv akṛtātmāno loke kṣatriyapāṃsanāḥ
nirarthakaṃ vikatthante yathā rāma vikatthase  Ram
kulaṃ vyapadiśan vīraḥ samare ko 'bhidhāsyati
mṛtyukāle hi samprāpte svayam aprastave stavam  Ram
sarvathā tu laghutvaṃ te katthanena vidarśitam
suvarṇapratirūpeṇa tapteneva kuśāgninā  Ram
na tu mām iha tiṣṭhantaṃ paśyasi tvaṃ gadādharam
dharādharam ivākampyaṃ parvataṃ dhātubhiś citam  Ram
paryāpto 'haṃ gadāpāṇir hantuṃ prāṇān raṇe tava
trayāṇām api lokānāṃ pāśahasta ivāntakaḥ  Ram
kāmaṃ bahv api vaktavyaṃ tvayi vakṣyāmi na tv aham
astaṃ gaccheddhi savitā yuddhavighnas tato bhavet  Ram
caturdaśa sahasrāṇi rākṣasānāṃ hatāni te
tvadvināśāt karomy adya teṣām aśrupramārjanam  Ram
ity uktvā paramakruddhas tāṃ gadāṃ paramāṅgadaḥ
kharaś cikṣepa rāmāya pradīptām aśaniṃ yathā  Ram
kharabāhupramuktā sā pradīptā mahatī gadā
bhasma vṛkṣāṃś ca gulmāṃś ca kṛtvāgāt tatsamīpataḥ  Ram
tām āpatantīṃ jvalitāṃ mṛtyupāśopamāṃ gadām
antarikṣagatāṃ rāmaś cicheda bahudhā śaraiḥ  Ram
sā viśīrṇā śarair bhinnā papāta dharaṇītale
gadāmantrauṣadhibalair vyālīva vinipātitā  Ram
bhittvā tu tāṃ gadāṃ bāṇai rāghavo dharmavatsalaḥ
smayamānaḥ kharaṃ vākyaṃ saṃrabdham idam abravīt  Ram
etat te balasarvasvaṃ darśitaṃ rākṣasādhama
śaktihīnataro matto vṛthā tvam avagarjasi  Ram
eṣā bāṇavinirbhinnā gadā bhūmitalaṃ gatā
abhidhānapragalbhasya tava pratyayaghātinī  Ram
yat tvayoktaṃ vinaṣṭānām idam aśrupramārjanam
rākṣasānāṃ karomīti mithyā tad api te vacaḥ  Ram
nīcasya kṣudraśīlasya mithyāvṛttasya rakṣasaḥ
prāṇān apahariṣyāmi garutmān amṛtaṃ yathā  Ram
adya te bhinnakaṇṭhasya phenabudbudabhūṣitam
vidāritasya madbāṇair mahī pāsyati śoṇitam  Ram
pāṃsurūṣitasarvāṅgaḥ srastanyastabhujadvayaḥ
svapsyase gāṃ samāśliṣya durlabhāṃ pramadām iva  Ram
pravṛddhanidre śayite tvayi rākṣasapāṃsane
bhaviṣyanty aśaraṇyānāṃ śaraṇyā daṇḍakā ime  Ram
janasthāne hatasthāne tava rākṣasa maccharaiḥ
nirbhayā vicariṣyanti sarvato munayo vane  Ram
adya viprasariṣyanti rākṣasyo hatabāndhavāḥ
bāṣpārdravadanā dīnā bhayād anyabhayāvahāḥ  Ram
adya śokarasajñās tā bhaviṣyanti niśācara
anurūpakulāḥ patnyo yāsāṃ tvaṃ patir īdṛśaḥ  Ram
nṛśaṃsaśīla kṣudrātman nityaṃ brāhmaṇakaṇṭaka
tvatkṛte śaṅkitair agnau munibhiḥ pātyate haviḥ  Ram
tam evam abhisaṃrabdhaṃ bruvāṇaṃ rāghavaṃ raṇe
kharo nirbhartsayāmāsa roṣāt kharatarasvanaḥ  Ram
dṛḍhaṃ khalv avalipto 'si bhayeṣv api ca nirbhayaḥ
vācyāvācyaṃ tato hi tvaṃ mṛtyuvaśyo na budhyase  Ram
kālapāśaparikṣiptā bhavanti puruṣā hi ye
kāryākāryaṃ na jānanti te nirastaṣaḍindriyāḥ  Ram
evam uktvā tato rāmaṃ saṃrudhya bhrukuṭiṃ tataḥ
sa dadarśa mahāsālam avidūre niśācaraḥ  Ram
raṇe praharaṇasyārthe sarvato hy avalokayan
sa tam utpāṭayāmāsa saṃdṛśya daśanacchadam  Ram
taṃ samutkṣipya bāhubhyāṃ vinarditvā mahābalaḥ
rāmam uddiśya cikṣepa hatas tvam iti cābravīt  Ram
tam āpatantaṃ bāṇaughaiś chittvā rāmaḥ pratāpavān
roṣam āhārayat tīvraṃ nihantuṃ samare kharam  Ram
jātasvedas tato rāmo roṣād raktāntalocanaḥ
nirbibheda sahasreṇa bāṇānāṃ samare kharam  Ram
tasya bāṇāntarād raktaṃ bahu susrāva phenilam
gireḥ prasravaṇasyeva toyadhārāparisravaḥ  Ram
vihvalaḥ sa kṛto bāṇaiḥ kharo rāmeṇa saṃyuge
matto rudhiragandhena tam evābhyadravad drutam  Ram
tam āpatantaṃ saṃrabdhaṃ kṛtāstro rudhirāplutam
apāsarpat pratipadaṃ kiṃcit tvaritavikramaḥ  Ram
tataḥ pāvakasaṃkāśaṃ vadhāya samare śaram
kharasya rāmo jagrāha brahmadaṇḍam ivāparam  Ram
sa tad dattaṃ maghavatā surarājena dhīmatā
saṃdadhe ca sa dharmātmā mumoca ca kharaṃ prati  Ram
sa vimukto mahābāṇo nirghātasamaniḥsvanaḥ
rāmeṇa dhanur udyamya kharasyorasi cāpatat  Ram
sa papāta kharo bhūmau dahyamānaḥ śarāgninā
rudreṇaiva vinirdagdhaḥ śvetāraṇye yathāndhakaḥ  Ram
sa vṛtra iva vajreṇa phenena namucir yathā
balo vendrāśanihato nipapāta hataḥ kharaḥ  Ram
tato rājarṣayaḥ sarve saṃgatāḥ paramarṣayaḥ
sabhājya muditā rāmam idaṃ vacanam abruvan  Ram
etadarthaṃ mahātejā mahendraḥ pākaśāsanaḥ
śarabhaṅgāśramaṃ puṇyam ājagāma puraṃdaraḥ  Ram
ānītas tvam imaṃ deśam upāyena maharṣibhiḥ
eṣāṃ vadhārthaṃ krūrāṇāṃ rakṣasāṃ pāpakarmaṇām  Ram
tad idaṃ naḥ kṛtaṃ kāryaṃ tvayā daśarathātmaja
sukhaṃ dharmaṃ cariṣyanti daṇḍakeṣu maharṣayaḥ  Ram
etasminn antare vīro lakṣmaṇaḥ saha sītayā
giridurgād viniṣkramya saṃviveśāśramaṃ sukhī  Ram
tato rāmas tu vijayī pūjyamāno maharṣibhiḥ
praviveśāśramaṃ vīro lakṣmaṇenābhivāditaḥ  Ram
taṃ dṛṣṭvā śatruhantāraṃ maharṣīṇāṃ sukhāvaham
babhūva hṛṣṭā vaidehī bhartāraṃ pariṣasvaje  Ram
tataḥ śūrpaṇakhā dṛṣṭvā sahasrāṇi caturdaśa
hatāny ekena rāmeṇa rakṣasāṃ bhīmakarmaṇām  Ram
dūṣaṇaṃ ca kharaṃ caiva hataṃ triśirasaṃ raṇe
dṛṣṭvā punar mahānādaṃ nanāda jaladopamā  Ram
sā dṛṣṭvā karma rāmasya kṛtam anyaiḥ suduṣkaram
jagāma paramodvignā laṅkāṃ rāvaṇapālitām  Ram
sā dadarśa vimānāgre rāvaṇaṃ dīptatejasam
upopaviṣṭaṃ sacivair marudbhir iva vāsavam  Ram
āsīnaṃ sūryasaṃkāśe kāñcane paramāsane
rukmavedigataṃ prājyaṃ jvalantam iva pāvakam  Ram
devagandharvabhūtānām ṛṣīṇāṃ ca mahātmanām
ajeyaṃ samare śūraṃ vyāttānanam ivāntakam  Ram
devāsuravimardeṣu vajrāśanikṛtavraṇam
airāvataviṣāṇāgrair utkṛṣṭakiṇavakṣasam  Ram
viṃśadbhujaṃ daśagrīvaṃ darśanīyaparicchadam
viśālavakṣasaṃ vīraṃ rājalakṣmaṇalakṣitam  Ram
snigdhavaiḍūryasaṃkāśaṃ taptakāñcanakuṇḍalam
subhujaṃ śukladaśanaṃ mahāsyaṃ parvatopamam  Ram
viṣṇucakranipātaiś ca śataśo devasaṃyuge
āhatāṅgaṃ samastaiś ca devapraharaṇais tathā  Ram
akṣobhyāṇāṃ samudrāṇāṃ kṣobhaṇaṃ kṣiprakāriṇam
kṣeptāraṃ parvatāgrāṇāṃ surāṇāṃ ca pramardanam  Ram
ucchettāraṃ ca dharmāṇāṃ paradārābhimarśanam
sarvadivyāstrayoktāraṃ yajñavighnakaraṃ sadā  Ram
purīṃ bhogavatīṃ gatvā parājitya ca vāsukim
takṣakasya priyāṃ bhāryāṃ parājitya jahāra yaḥ  Ram
kailāsaṃ parvataṃ gatvā vijitya naravāhanam
vimānaṃ puṣpakaṃ tasya kāmagaṃ vai jahāra yaḥ  Ram
vanaṃ caitrarathaṃ divyaṃ nalinīṃ nandanaṃ vanam
vināśayati yaḥ krodhād devodyānāni vīryavān  Ram
candrasūryau mahābhāgāv uttiṣṭhantau paraṃtapau
nivārayati bāhubhyāṃ yaḥ śailaśikharopamaḥ  Ram
daśavarṣasahasrāṇi tapas taptvā mahāvane
purā svayambhuve dhīraḥ śirāṃsy upajahāra yaḥ  Ram
devadānavagandharvapiśācapatagoragaiḥ
abhayaṃ yasya saṃgrāme mṛtyuto mānuṣād ṛte  Ram
mantrair abhiṣutaṃ puṇyam adhvareṣu dvijātibhiḥ
havirdhāneṣu yaḥ somam upahanti mahābalaḥ  Ram
āptayajñaharaṃ krūraṃ brahmaghnaṃ duṣṭacāriṇam
karkaśaṃ niranukrośaṃ prajānām ahite ratam
rāvaṇaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ sarvalokabhayāvaham  Ram
rākṣasī bhrātaraṃ krūraṃ sā dadarśa mahābalam
taṃ divyavastrābharaṇaṃ divyamālyopaśobhitam
rākṣasendraṃ mahābhāgaṃ paulastyakulanandanam  Ram
tam abravīd dīptaviśālalocanaṃ pradarśayitvā bhayamohamūrchitā
sudāruṇaṃ vākyam abhītacāriṇī mahātmanā śūrpaṇakhā virūpitā  Ram
tataḥ śūrpaṇakhā dīnā rāvaṇaṃ lokarāvaṇam
amātyamadhye saṃkruddhā paruṣaṃ vākyam abravīt  Ram
pramattaḥ kāmabhogeṣu svairavṛtto niraṅkuśaḥ
samutpannaṃ bhayaṃ ghoraṃ boddhavyaṃ nāvabudhyase  Ram
saktaṃ grāmyeṣu bhogeṣu kāmavṛttaṃ mahīpatim
lubdhaṃ na bahu manyante śmaśānāgnim iva prajāḥ  Ram
svayaṃ kāryāṇi yaḥ kāle nānutiṣṭhati pārthivaḥ
sa tu vai saha rājyena taiś ca kāryair vinaśyati  Ram
ayuktacāraṃ durdarśam asvādhīnaṃ narādhipam
varjayanti narā dūrān nadīpaṅkam iva dvipāḥ  Ram
ye na rakṣanti viṣayam asvādhīnā narādhipāḥ
te na vṛddhyā prakāśante girayaḥ sāgare yathā  Ram
ātmavadbhir vigṛhya tvaṃ devagandharvadānavaiḥ
ayuktacāraś capalaḥ kathaṃ rājā bhaviṣyasi  Ram
yeṣāṃ cāraś ca kośaś ca nayaś ca jayatāṃ vara
asvādhīnā narendrāṇāṃ prākṛtais te janaiḥ samāḥ  Ram
yasmāt paśyanti dūrasthān sarvān arthān narādhipāḥ
cāreṇa tasmād ucyante rājāno dīrghacakṣuṣaḥ  Ram
ayuktacāraṃ manye tvāṃ prākṛtaiḥ sacivair vṛtam
svajanaṃ ca janasthānaṃ hataṃ yo nāvabudhyase  Ram
caturdaśa sahasrāṇi rakṣasāṃ bhīmakarmaṇām
hatāny ekena rāmeṇa kharaś ca sahadūṣaṇaḥ  Ram
ṛṣīṇām abhayaṃ dattaṃ kṛtakṣemāś ca daṇḍakāḥ
dharṣitaṃ ca janasthānaṃ rāmeṇākliṣṭakarmaṇā  Ram
tvaṃ tu lubdhaḥ pramattaś ca parādhīnaś ca rāvaṇa
viṣaye sve samutpannaṃ bhayaṃ yo nāvabudhyase  Ram
tīkṣṇam alpapradātāraṃ pramattaṃ garvitaṃ śaṭham
vyasane sarvabhūtāni nābhidhāvanti pārthivam  Ram
atimāninam agrāhyam ātmasaṃbhāvitaṃ naram
krodhanaṃ vyasane hanti svajano 'pi narādhipam  Ram
nānutiṣṭhati kāryāṇi bhayeṣu na bibheti ca
kṣipraṃ rājyāc cyuto dīnas tṛṇais tulyo bhaviṣyati  Ram
śuṣkakāṣṭhair bhavet kāryaṃ loṣṭair api ca pāṃsubhiḥ
na tu sthānāt paribhraṣṭaiḥ kāryaṃ syād vasudhādhipaiḥ  Ram
upabhuktaṃ yathā vāsaḥ srajo vā mṛditā yathā
evaṃ rājyāt paribhraṣṭaḥ samartho 'pi nirarthakaḥ  Ram
apramattaś ca yo rājā sarvajño vijitendriyaḥ
kṛtajño dharmaśīlaś ca sa rājā tiṣṭhate ciram  Ram
nayanābhyāṃ prasupto 'pi jāgarti nayacakṣuṣā
vyaktakrodhaprasādaś ca sa rājā pūjyate janaiḥ  Ram
tvaṃ tu rāvaṇa durbuddhir guṇair etair vivarjitaḥ
yasya te 'viditaś cārai rakṣasāṃ sumahān vadhaḥ  Ram
parāvamantā viṣayeṣu saṃgato na deśakālapravibhāgatattvavit
ayuktabuddhir guṇadoṣaniścaye vipannarājyo na cirād vipatsyate  Ram
iti svadoṣān parikīrtitāṃs tayā samīkṣya buddhyā kṣaṇadācareśvaraḥ
dhanena darpeṇa balena cānvito vicintayāmāsa ciraṃ sa rāvaṇaḥ  Ram
tataḥ śūrpaṇakhāṃ kruddhāṃ bruvatīṃ paruṣaṃ vacaḥ
amātyamadhye saṃkruddhaḥ paripapraccha rāvaṇaḥ  Ram
kaś ca rāmaḥ kathaṃvīryaḥ kiṃrūpaḥ kiṃparākramaḥ
kimarthaṃ daṇḍakāraṇyaṃ praviṣṭaś ca suduścaram  Ram
āyudhaṃ kiṃ ca rāmasya nihatā yena rākṣasāḥ
kharaś ca nihataḥ saṃkhye dūṣaṇas triśirās tathā  Ram
ity uktā rākṣasendreṇa rākṣasī krodhamūrchitā
tato rāmaṃ yathānyāyam ākhyātum upacakrame  Ram
dīrghabāhur viśālākṣaś cīrakṛṣṇājināmbaraḥ
kandarpasamarūpaś ca rāmo daśarathātmajaḥ  Ram
śakracāpanibhaṃ cāpaṃ vikṛṣya kanakāṅgadam
dīptān kṣipati nārācān sarpān iva mahāviṣān  Ram
nādadānaṃ śarān ghorān na muñcantaṃ mahābalam
na kārmukaṃ vikarṣantaṃ rāmaṃ paśyāmi saṃyuge  Ram
hanyamānaṃ tu tat sainyaṃ paśyāmi śaravṛṣṭibhiḥ
